alif-Lam-meem الٓمٓ Alif Laam Meem

1

1.

Alif, Lam, Meem.

1

dhālika ذَلِكَ That l-kitābu الْكِتَابُ (is) the Book lā لَا no rayba رَيْبَ doubt fīhi فِيهِ in it hudan هُدًى a Guidance lil'muttaqīna لِلْمُتَّقِينَ for the God-conscious

2

2.

This is the Book about which there is no doubt, a guidance for those conscious of Allah -

2

alladhīna الَّذِينَ Those who yu'minūna يُؤْمِنُونَ believe bil-ghaybi بِالْغَيْبِ in the unseen wayuqīmūna وَيُقِيمُونَ and establish l-ṣalata الصَّلَوةَ the prayer wamimmā وَمِمَّا and out of what razaqnāhum رَزَقْنَاهُمْ We have provided them yunfiqūna يُنْفِقُونَ they spend

3

3.

Who believe in the unseen, establish prayer, and spend out of what We have provided for them,

3

wa-alladhīna وَالَّذِينَ And those who yu'minūna يُؤْمِنُونَ believe bimā بِمَا in what unzila أُنْزِلَ (is) sent down ilayka إِلَيْكَ to you wamā وَمَا and what unzila أُنْزِلَ was sent down min مِنْ from qablika قَبْلِكَ before you wabil-ākhirati وَبِالْءَاخِرَةِ and in the Hereafter hum هُمْ they yūqinūna يُوقِنُونَ firmly believe

4

4.

And who believe in what has been revealed to you, [O Muhammad], and what was revealed before you, and of the Hereafter they are certain [in faith].

4

ulāika أُولَئِكَ Those ʿalā عَلَى (are) on hudan هُدًى Guidance min مِنْ from rabbihim رَبِّهِمْ their Lord wa-ulāika وَأُولَئِكَ and those humu هُمُ they l-muf'liḥūna الْمُفْلِحُونَ (are) the successful ones

5

5.

Those are upon [right] guidance from their Lord, and it is those who are the successful.

5

inna إِنَّ Indeed alladhīna الَّذِينَ those who kafarū كَفَرُوا disbelieve[d] sawāon سَوَاءٌ (it) is same ʿalayhim عَلَيْهِمْ to them a-andhartahum ءَأَنْذَرْتَهُمْ whether you warn them am أَمْ or lam لَمْ not tundhir'hum تُنْذِرْهُمْ you warn them lā لَا not yu'minūna يُؤْمِنُونَ they believe

6

6.

Indeed, those who disbelieve - it is all the same for them whether you warn them or do not warn them - they will not believe.

6

khatama خَتَمَ Has set a seal l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah ʿalā عَلَى on qulūbihim قُلُوبِهِمْ their hearts waʿalā وَعَلَى and on samʿihim سَمْعِهِمْ their hearing waʿalā وَعَلَى and on abṣārihim أَبْصَارِهِمْ their vision ghishāwatun غِشَاوَةٌ (is) a veil walahum وَلَهُمْ And for them ʿadhābun عَذَابٌ (is) a punishment ʿaẓīmun عَظِيمٌ great

7

7.

Allah has set a seal upon their hearts and upon their hearing, and over their vision is a veil. And for them is a great punishment.

7

wamina وَمِنَ And of l-nāsi النَّاسِ the people man مَنْ (are some) who yaqūlu يَقُولُ say āmannā ءَامَنَّا We believed bil-lahi بِاللَّهِ in Allah wabil-yawmi وَبِالْيَوْمِ and in the Day l-ākhiri الْءَاخِرِ [the] Last wamā وَمَا but not hum هُمْ they bimu'minīna بِمُؤْمِنِينَ (are) believers (at all)

8

8.

And of the people are some who say, "We believe in Allah and the Last Day," but they are not believers.

8

yukhādiʿūna يُخَادِعُونَ They seek to deceive l-laha اللَّهَ Allah wa-alladhīna وَالَّذِينَ and those who āmanū ءَامَنُوا believe[d] wamā وَمَا and not yakhdaʿūna يَخْدَعُونَ they deceive illā إِلَّا except anfusahum أَنْفُسَهُمْ themselves wamā وَمَا and not yashʿurūna يَشْعُرُونَ they realize (it)

9

9.

They [think to] deceive Allah and those who believe, but they deceive not except themselves and perceive [it] not.

9

fī فِي In qulūbihim قُلُوبِهِمْ their hearts maraḍun مَرَضٌ (is) a disease fazādahumu فَزَادَهُمُ so has increased them l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah maraḍan مَرَضًا (in) disease walahum وَلَهُمْ and for them ʿadhābun عَذَابٌ (is) a punishment alīmun أَلِيمٌ painful bimā بِمَا because kānū كَانُوا they used (to) yakdhibūna يَكْذِبُونَ [they] lie

10

10.

In their hearts is disease, so Allah has increased their disease; and for them is a painful punishment because they [habitually] used to lie.

10

wa-idhā وَإِذَا And when qīla قِيلَ it is said lahum لَهُمْ to them lā لَا (Do) not tuf'sidū تُفْسِدُوا spread corruption fī فِي in l-arḍi الْأَرْضِ the earth qālū قَالُوا they say innamā إِنَّمَا Only naḥnu نَحْنُ we muṣ'liḥūna مُصْلِحُونَ (are) reformers

11

11.

And when it is said to them, "Do not cause corruption on the earth," they say, "We are but reformers."

11

alā أَلَا Beware innahum إِنَّهُمْ indeed they humu هُمُ themselves l-muf'sidūna الْمُفْسِدُونَ (are) the ones who spread corruption walākin وَلَكِنْ [and] but lā لَا not yashʿurūna يَشْعُرُونَ they realize (it)

12

12.

Unquestionably, it is they who are the corrupters, but they perceive [it] not.

12

wa-idhā وَإِذَا And when qīla قِيلَ it is said lahum لَهُمْ to them āminū ءَامِنُوا Believe kamā كَمَا as āmana ءَامَنَ believed l-nāsu النَّاسُ the people qālū قَالُوا they say anu'minu أَنُؤْمِنُ Should we believe kamā كَمَا as āmana ءَامَنَ believed l-sufahāu السُّفَهَاءُ the fools alā أَلَا Beware innahum إِنَّهُمْ certainly they humu هُمُ themselves l-sufahāu السُّفَهَاءُ (are) the fools walākin وَلَكِنْ [and] but lā لَا not yaʿlamūna يَعْلَمُونَ they know

13

13.

And when it is said to them, "Believe as the people have believed," they say, "Should we believe as the foolish have believed?" Unquestionably, it is they who are the foolish, but they know [it] not.

13

wa-idhā وَإِذَا And when laqū لَقُوا they meet alladhīna الَّذِينَ those who āmanū ءَامَنُوا believe[d] qālū قَالُوا they say āmannā ءَامَنَّا We believe[d] wa-idhā وَإِذَا But when khalaw خَلَوْا they are alone ilā إِلَى with shayāṭīnihim شَيَاطِينِهِمْ their evil ones qālū قَالُوا they say innā إِنَّا Indeed, we maʿakum مَعَكُمْ (are) with you innamā إِنَّمَا only naḥnu نَحْنُ we mus'tahziūna مُسْتَهْزِءُونَ (are) mockers

14

14.

And when they meet those who believe, they say, "We believe"; but when they are alone with their evil ones, they say, "Indeed, we are with you; we were only mockers."

14

al-lahu اللَّهُ Allah yastahzi-u يَسْتَهْزِئُ mocks bihim بِهِمْ at them wayamudduhum وَيَمُدُّهُمْ and prolongs them fī فِي in ṭugh'yānihim طُغْيَانِهِمْ their transgression yaʿmahūna يَعْمَهُونَ they wander blindly

15

15.

[But] Allah mocks them and prolongs them in their transgression [while] they wander blindly.

15

ulāika أُولَئِكَ Those alladhīna الَّذِينَ (are) the ones who ish'tarawū اشْتَرَوُا bought l-ḍalālata الضَّلَالَةَ [the] astraying bil-hudā بِالْهُدَى for [the] guidance famā فَمَا So not rabiḥat رَبِحَتْ profited tijāratuhum تِجَارَتُهُمْ their commerce wamā وَمَا and not kānū كَانُوا were they muh'tadīna مُهْتَدِينَ guided-ones

16

16.

Those are the ones who have purchased error [in exchange] for guidance, so their transaction has brought no profit, nor were they guided.

16

mathaluhum مَثَلُهُمْ Their example kamathali كَمَثَلِ (is) like (the) example alladhī الَّذِي (of) the one who is'tawqada اسْتَوْقَدَ kindled nāran نَارًا a fire falammā فَلَمَّا then, when aḍāat أَضَاءَتْ it lighted mā مَا what ḥawlahu حَوْلَهُ his surroundings dhahaba ذَهَبَ took away l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah binūrihim بِنُورِهِمْ their light watarakahum وَتَرَكَهُمْ and left them fī فِي in ẓulumātin ظُلُمَاتٍ darkness[es] lā لَا (so) not yub'ṣirūna يُبْصِرُونَ (do) they see

17

17.

Their example is that of one who kindled a fire, but when it illuminated what was around him, Allah took away their light and left them in darkness [so] they could not see.

17

ṣummun صُمٌّ Deaf buk'mun بُكْمٌ dumb ʿum'yun عُمْيٌ blind fahum فَهُمْ so they lā لَا not yarjiʿūna يَرْجِعُونَ [they] will not return

18

18.

Deaf, dumb and blind - so they will not return [to the right path].

18

aw أَوْ Or kaṣayyibin كَصَيِّبٍ like a rainstorm mina مِنَ from l-samāi السَّمَاءِ the sky fīhi فِيهِ in it (are) ẓulumātun ظُلُمَاتٌ darkness[es] waraʿdun وَرَعْدٌ and thunder wabarqun وَبَرْقٌ and lightning yajʿalūna يَجْعَلُونَ They put aṣābiʿahum أَصَابِعَهُمْ their fingers fī فِي in ādhānihim ءَاذَانِهِمْ their ears mina مِنَ from l-ṣawāʿiqi الصَّوَاعِقِ the thunderclaps ḥadhara حَذَرَ (in) fear (of) l-mawti الْمَوْتِ [the] death wal-lahu وَاللَّهُ And Allah muḥīṭun مُحِيطٌ (is) [the One Who] encompasses bil-kāfirīna بِالْكَافِرِينَ the disbelievers

19

19.

Or [it is] like a rainstorm from the sky within which is darkness, thunder and lightning. They put their fingers in their ears against the thunderclaps in dread of death. But Allah is encompassing of the disbelievers.

19

yakādu يَكَادُ Almost l-barqu الْبَرْقُ the lightning yakhṭafu يَخْطَفُ snatches away abṣārahum أَبْصَارَهُمْ their sight kullamā كُلَّمَا Whenever aḍāa أَضَاءَ it flashes lahum لَهُمْ for them mashaw مَشَوْا they walk fīhi فِيهِ in it wa-idhā وَإِذَا and when aẓlama أَظْلَمَ it darkens ʿalayhim عَلَيْهِمْ on them qāmū قَامُوا they stand (still) walaw وَلَوْ And if shāa شَاءَ had willed l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah ladhahaba لَذَهَبَ He would certainly have taken away bisamʿihim بِسَمْعِهِمْ their hearing wa-abṣārihim وَأَبْصَارِهِمْ and their sight inna إِنَّ Indeed l-laha اللَّهَ Allah ʿalā عَلَى (is) on kulli كُلِّ every shayin شَيْءٍ thing qadīrun قَدِيرٌ All-Powerful

20

20.

The lightning almost snatches away their sight. Every time it lights [the way] for them, they walk therein; but when darkness comes over them, they stand [still]. And if Allah had willed, He could have taken away their hearing and their sight. Indeed, Allah is over all things competent.

20

yāayyuhā يَاأَيُّهَا O you l-nāsu النَّاسُ mankind uʿ'budū اعْبُدُوا worship rabbakumu رَبَّكُمُ your Lord alladhī الَّذِي the One Who khalaqakum خَلَقَكُمْ created you wa-alladhīna وَالَّذِينَ and those [who] min مِنْ from qablikum قَبْلِكُمْ before you laʿallakum لَعَلَّكُمْ so that you may tattaqūna تَتَّقُونَ become righteous

21

21.

O mankind, worship your Lord, who created you and those before you, that you may become righteous -

21

alladhī الَّذِي The One Who jaʿala جَعَلَ made lakumu لَكُمُ for you l-arḍa الْأَرْضَ the earth firāshan فِرَاشًا a resting place wal-samāa وَالسَّمَاءَ and the sky bināan بِنَاءً a canopy wa-anzala وَأَنْزَلَ and sent down mina مِنَ from l-samāi السَّمَاءِ the sky māan مَاءً water fa-akhraja فَأَخْرَجَ then brought forth bihi بِهِ therewith mina مِنَ [of] l-thamarāti الثَّمَرَاتِ the fruits riz'qan رِزْقًا (as) provision lakum لَكُمْ for you falā فَلَا So (do) not tajʿalū تَجْعَلُوا set up lillahi لِلَّهِ to Allah andādan أَنْدَادًا rivals wa-antum وَأَنْتُمْ while you taʿlamūna تَعْلَمُونَ [you] know

22

22.

[He] who made for you the earth a bed [spread out] and the sky a ceiling and sent down from the sky, rain and brought forth thereby fruits as provision for you. So do not attribute to Allah equals while you know [that there is nothing similar to Him].

22

wa-in وَإِنْ And if kuntum كُنْتُمْ you are fī فِي in raybin رَيْبٍ doubt mimmā مِمَّا about what nazzalnā نَزَّلْنَا We have revealed ʿalā عَلَى to ʿabdinā عَبْدِنَا Our slave fatū فَأْتُوا then produce bisūratin بِسُورَةٍ a chapter min مِنْ [of] mith'lihi مِثْلِهِ like it wa-id'ʿū وَادْعُوا and call shuhadāakum شُهَدَاءَكُمْ your witnesses min مِنْ from dūni دُونِ other than l-lahi اللَّهِ Allah in إِنْ if kuntum كُنْتُمْ you are ṣādiqīna صَادِقِينَ truthful

23

23.

And if you are in doubt about what We have sent down upon Our Servant [Muhammad], then produce a surah the like thereof and call upon your witnesses other than Allah, if you should be truthful.

23

fa-in فَإِنْ But if lam لَمْ not tafʿalū تَفْعَلُوا you do walan وَلَنْ and never tafʿalū تَفْعَلُوا will you do fa-ittaqū فَاتَّقُوا then fear l-nāra النَّارَ the Fire allatī الَّتِي whose waqūduhā وَقُودُهَا [its] fuel l-nāsu النَّاسُ (is) [the] men wal-ḥijāratu وَالْحِجَارَةُ and [the] stones uʿiddat أُعِدَّتْ prepared lil'kāfirīna لِلْكَافِرِينَ for the disbelievers

24

24.

But if you do not - and you will never be able to - then fear the Fire, whose fuel is men and stones, prepared for the disbelievers.

24

wabashiri وَبَشِّرِ And give good news alladhīna الَّذِينَ (to) those who āmanū ءَامَنُوا believe waʿamilū وَعَمِلُوا and do l-ṣāliḥāti الصَّالِحَاتِ [the] righteous deeds anna أَنَّ that lahum لَهُمْ for them jannātin جَنَّاتٍ (will be) Gardens tajrī تَجْرِي flow min مِنْ [from] taḥtihā تَحْتِهَا under them l-anhāru الْأَنْهَارُ the rivers kullamā كُلَّمَا Every time ruziqū رُزِقُوا they are provided min'hā مِنْهَا therefrom min مِنْ of thamaratin ثَمَرَةٍ fruit riz'qan رِزْقًا (as) provision qālū قَالُوا they (will) say hādhā هَذَا This (is) alladhī الَّذِي the one which ruziq'nā رُزِقْنَا we were provided min مِنْ from qablu قَبْلُ before wa-utū وَأُتُوا And they will be given bihi بِهِ therefrom mutashābihan مُتَشَابِهًا (things) in resemblance walahum وَلَهُمْ And for them fīhā فِيهَا therein azwājun أَزْوَاجٌ spouses muṭahharatun مُطَهَّرَةٌ purified wahum وَهُمْ and they fīhā فِيهَا therein khālidūna خَالِدُونَ (will) abide forever

25

25.

And give good tidings to those who believe and do righteous deeds that they will have gardens [in Paradise] beneath which rivers flow. Whenever they are provided with a provision of fruit therefrom, they will say, "This is what we were provided with before." And it is given to them in likeness. And they will have therein purified spouses, and they will abide therein eternally.

25

inna إِنَّ Indeed l-laha اللَّهَ Allah lā لَا (is) not yastaḥyī يَسْتَحْيِي ashamed an أَنْ to yaḍriba يَضْرِبَ set forth mathalan مَثَلًا an example mā مَا (like) even baʿūḍatan بَعُوضَةً (of) a mosquito famā فَمَا and (even) something fawqahā فَوْقَهَا above it fa-ammā فَأَمَّا Then as for alladhīna الَّذِينَ those who āmanū ءَامَنُوا believed fayaʿlamūna فَيَعْلَمُونَ [thus] they will know annahu أَنَّهُ that it l-ḥaqu الْحَقُّ (is) the truth min مِنْ from rabbihim رَبِّهِمْ their Lord wa-ammā وَأَمَّا And as for alladhīna الَّذِينَ those who kafarū كَفَرُوا disbelieved fayaqūlūna فَيَقُولُونَ [thus] they will say mādhā مَاذَا what arāda أَرَادَ (did) intend l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah bihādhā بِهَذَا by this mathalan مَثَلًا example yuḍillu يُضِلُّ He lets go astray bihi بِهِ by it kathīran كَثِيرًا many wayahdī وَيَهْدِي and He guides bihi بِهِ by it kathīran كَثِيرًا many wamā وَمَا And not yuḍillu يُضِلُّ He lets go astray bihi بِهِ by it illā إِلَّا except l-fāsiqīna الْفَاسِقِينَ the defiantly disobedient

26

26.

Indeed, Allah is not timid to present an example - that of a mosquito or what is smaller than it. And those who have believed know that it is the truth from their Lord. But as for those who disbelieve, they say, "What did Allah intend by this as an example?" He misleads many thereby and guides many thereby. And He misleads not except the defiantly disobedient,

26

alladhīna الَّذِينَ Those who yanquḍūna يَنْقُضُونَ break ʿahda عَهْدَ (the) Covenant l-lahi اللَّهِ (of) Allah min مِنْ from baʿdi بَعْدِ after mīthāqihi مِيثَاقِهِ its ratification wayaqṭaʿūna وَيَقْطَعُونَ and [they] cut mā مَا what amara أَمَرَ has ordered l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah bihi بِهِ it an أَنْ to yūṣala يُوصَلَ be joined wayuf'sidūna وَيُفْسِدُونَ and [they] spread corruption fī فِي in l-arḍi الْأَرْضِ the earth ulāika أُولَئِكَ Those humu هُمُ they l-khāsirūna الْخَاسِرُونَ (are) the losers

27

27.

Who break the covenant of Allah after contracting it and sever that which Allah has ordered to be joined and cause corruption on earth. It is those who are the losers.

27

kayfa كَيْفَ How takfurūna تَكْفُرُونَ (can) you disbelieve bil-lahi بِاللَّهِ in Allah wakuntum وَكُنْتُمْ While you were amwātan أَمْوَاتًا dead fa-aḥyākum فَأَحْيَاكُمْ then He gave you life thumma ثُمَّ then yumītukum يُمِيتُكُمْ He will cause you to die thumma ثُمَّ then yuḥ'yīkum يُحْيِيكُمْ He will give you life thumma ثُمَّ then ilayhi إِلَيْهِ to Him tur'jaʿūna تُرْجَعُونَ you will be returned

28

28.

How can you disbelieve in Allah when you were lifeless and He brought you to life; then He will cause you to die, then He will bring you [back] to life, and then to Him you will be returned.

28

huwa هُوَ He alladhī الَّذِي (is) the One Who khalaqa خَلَقَ created lakum لَكُمْ for you mā مَا what fī فِي (is) in l-arḍi الْأَرْضِ the earth jamīʿan جَمِيعًا all thumma ثُمَّ Moreover is'tawā اسْتَوَى He turned ilā إِلَى to l-samāi السَّمَاءِ the heaven fasawwāhunna فَسَوَّاهُنَّ and fashioned them sabʿa سَبْعَ seven samāwātin سَمَاوَاتٍ heavens wahuwa وَهُوَ And He bikulli بِكُلِّ of every shayin شَيْءٍ thing ʿalīmun عَلِيمٌ (is) All-Knowing

29

29.

It is He who created for you all of that which is on the earth. Then He directed Himself to the heaven, [His being above all creation], and made them seven heavens, and He is Knowing of all things.

29

wa-idh وَإِذْ And when qāla قَالَ said rabbuka رَبُّكَ your Lord lil'malāikati لِلْمَلَائِكَةِ to the angels innī إِنِّي Indeed, I (am) jāʿilun جَاعِلٌ going to place fī فِي in l-arḍi الْأَرْضِ the earth khalīfatan خَلِيفَةً a vicegerent qālū قَالُوا they said atajʿalu أَتَجْعَلُ Will You place fīhā فِيهَا in it man مَنْ (one) who yuf'sidu يُفْسِدُ will spread corruption fīhā فِيهَا in it wayasfiku وَيَسْفِكُ and will shed l-dimāa الدِّمَاءَ [the] blood[s] wanaḥnu وَنَحْنُ while we nusabbiḥu نُسَبِّحُ [we] glorify (You) biḥamdika بِحَمْدِكَ with Your praises wanuqaddisu وَنُقَدِّسُ and we sanctify laka لَكَ [to] You qāla قَالَ He said innī إِنِّي Indeed, I aʿlamu أَعْلَمُ [I] know mā مَا what lā لَا (do) not taʿlamūna تَعْلَمُونَ you know

30

30.

And [mention, O Muhammad], when your Lord said to the angels, "Indeed, I will make upon the earth a successive authority." They said, "Will You place upon it one who causes corruption therein and sheds blood, while we declare Your praise and sanctify You?" Allah said, "Indeed, I know that which you do not know."

30

waʿallama وَعَلَّمَ And He taught ādama ءَادَمَ Adam l-asmāa الْأَسْمَاءَ the names kullahā كُلَّهَا all of them thumma ثُمَّ Then ʿaraḍahum عَرَضَهُمْ He displayed them ʿalā عَلَى to l-malāikati الْمَلَائِكَةِ the angels faqāla فَقَالَ then He said anbiūnī أَنْبِئُونِي Inform Me bi-asmāi بِأَسْمَاءِ of (the) names hāulāi هَؤُلَاءِ (of) these in إِنْ if kuntum كُنْتُمْ you are ṣādiqīna صَادِقِينَ truthful

31

31.

And He taught Adam the names - all of them. Then He showed them to the angels and said, "Inform Me of the names of these, if you are truthful."

31

qālū قَالُوا They said sub'ḥānaka سُبْحَانَكَ Glory be to You lā لَا No ʿil'ma عِلْمَ knowledge lanā لَنَا (is) for us illā إِلَّا except mā مَا what ʿallamtanā عَلَّمْتَنَا You have taught us innaka إِنَّكَ Indeed You anta أَنْتَ You l-ʿalīmu الْعَلِيمُ (are) the All-Knowing l-ḥakīmu الْحَكِيمُ the All-Wise

32

32.

They said, "Exalted are You; we have no knowledge except what You have taught us. Indeed, it is You who is the Knowing, the Wise."

32

qāla قَالَ He said yāādamu يَاءَادَمُ O Adam! anbi'hum أَنْبِئْهُمْ Inform them bi-asmāihim بِأَسْمَائِهِمْ of their names falammā فَلَمَّا And when anba-ahum أَنْبَأَهُمْ he had informed them bi-asmāihim بِأَسْمَائِهِمْ of their names qāla قَالَ He said alam أَلَمْ Did not aqul أَقُلْ I say lakum لَكُمْ to you innī إِنِّي Indeed, I aʿlamu أَعْلَمُ [I] know ghayba غَيْبَ (the) unseen l-samāwāti السَّمَاوَاتِ (of) the heavens wal-arḍi وَالْأَرْضِ and the earth wa-aʿlamu وَأَعْلَمُ and I know mā مَا what tub'dūna تُبْدُونَ you reveal wamā وَمَا and what kuntum كُنْتُمْ you [were] taktumūna تَكْتُمُونَ conceal

33

33.

He said, "O Adam, inform them of their names." And when he had informed them of their names, He said, "Did I not tell you that I know the unseen [aspects] of the heavens and the earth? And I know what you reveal and what you have concealed."

33

wa-idh وَإِذْ And when qul'nā قُلْنَا We said lil'malāikati لِلْمَلَائِكَةِ to the angels us'judū اسْجُدُوا Prostrate liādama لِءَادَمَ to Adam fasajadū فَسَجَدُوا [so] they prostrated illā إِلَّا except ib'līsa إِبْلِيسَ Iblees abā أَبَى He refused wa-is'takbara وَاسْتَكْبَرَ and was arrogant wakāna وَكَانَ and became mina مِنَ of l-kāfirīna الْكَافِرِينَ the disbelievers

34

34.

And [mention] when We said to the angels, "Prostrate before Adam"; so they prostrated, except for Iblees. He refused and was arrogant and became of the disbelievers.

34

waqul'nā وَقُلْنَا And We said yāādamu يَاءَادَمُ O Adam us'kun اسْكُنْ Dwell anta أَنْتَ you wazawjuka وَزَوْجُكَ and your spouse l-janata الْجَنَّةَ (in) Paradise wakulā وَكُلَا and [you both] eat min'hā مِنْهَا from it raghadan رَغَدًا freely ḥaythu حَيْثُ (from) wherever shi'tumā شِئْتُمَا you [both] wish walā وَلَا But do not taqrabā تَقْرَبَا [you two] approach hādhihi هَذِهِ this l-shajarata الشَّجَرَةَ [the] tree fatakūnā فَتَكُونَا lest you [both] be mina مِنَ of l-ẓālimīna الظَّالِمِينَ the wrongdoers

35

35.

And We said, "O Adam, dwell, you and your wife, in Paradise and eat therefrom in [ease and] abundance from wherever you will. But do not approach this tree, lest you be among the wrongdoers."

35

fa-azallahumā فَأَزَلَّهُمَا Then made [both of] them slip l-shayṭānu الشَّيْطَانُ the Shaitaan ʿanhā عَنْهَا from it fa-akhrajahumā فَأَخْرَجَهُمَا and he got [both of] them out mimmā مِمَّا from what kānā كَانَا they [both] were fīhi فِيهِ in [it] waqul'nā وَقُلْنَا And We said ih'biṭū اهْبِطُوا Go down (all of you) baʿḍukum بَعْضُكُمْ some of you libaʿḍin لِبَعْضٍ to others ʿaduwwun عَدُوٌّ (as) enemy walakum وَلَكُمْ and for you fī فِي in l-arḍi الْأَرْضِ the earth mus'taqarrun مُسْتَقَرٌّ (is) a dwelling place wamatāʿun وَمَتَاعٌ and a provision ilā إِلَى for ḥīnin حِينٍ a period

36

36.

But Satan caused them to slip out of it and removed them from that [condition] in which they had been. And We said, "Go down, [all of you], as enemies to one another, and you will have upon the earth a place of settlement and provision for a time."

36

fatalaqqā فَتَلَقَّى Then received ādamu ءَادَمُ Adam min مِنْ from rabbihi رَبِّهِ his Lord kalimātin كَلِمَاتٍ words fatāba فَتَابَ So (his Lord) turned ʿalayhi عَلَيْهِ towards him innahu إِنَّهُ Indeed He huwa هُوَ He l-tawābu التَّوَّابُ (is) the Oft-returning (to mercy) l-raḥīmu الرَّحِيمُ the Most Merciful

37

37.

Then Adam received from his Lord [some] words, and He accepted his repentance. Indeed, it is He who is the Accepting of repentance, the Merciful.

37

qul'nā قُلْنَا We said ih'biṭū اهْبِطُوا Go down min'hā مِنْهَا from it jamīʿan جَمِيعًا all (of you) fa-immā فَإِمَّا and when yatiyannakum يَأْتِيَنَّكُمْ comes to you minnī مِنِّي from Me hudan هُدًى Guidance faman فَمَنْ then whoever tabiʿa تَبِعَ follows hudāya هُدَايَ My Guidance falā فَلَا [then] no khawfun خَوْفٌ fear ʿalayhim عَلَيْهِمْ (will be) on them walā وَلَا and not hum هُمْ they yaḥzanūna يَحْزَنُونَ will grieve

38

38.

We said, "Go down from it, all of you. And when guidance comes to you from Me, whoever follows My guidance - there will be no fear concerning them, nor will they grieve.

38

wa-alladhīna وَالَّذِينَ And those kafarū كَفَرُوا who disbelieve[d] wakadhabū وَكَذَّبُوا and deny biāyātinā بِءَايَاتِنَا Our Signs ulāika أُولَئِكَ those aṣḥābu أَصْحَابُ (are the) companions l-nāri النَّارِ (of) the Fire hum هُمْ they fīhā فِيهَا in it khālidūna خَالِدُونَ (will) abide forever

39

39.

And those who disbelieve and deny Our signs - those will be companions of the Fire; they will abide therein eternally."

39

yābanī يَابَنِي O Children is'rāīla إِسْرَاءِيلَ (of) Israel! udh'kurū اذْكُرُوا Remember niʿ'matiya نِعْمَتِيَ My Favor allatī الَّتِي which anʿamtu أَنْعَمْتُ I bestowed ʿalaykum عَلَيْكُمْ upon you wa-awfū وَأَوْفُوا and fulfill biʿahdī بِعَهْدِي My Covenant ūfi أُوفِ I will fulfill biʿahdikum بِعَهْدِكُمْ your covenant wa-iyyāya وَإِيَّايَ and Me Alone fa-ir'habūni فَارْهَبُونِ fear [Me]

40

40.

O Children of Israel, remember My favor which I have bestowed upon you and fulfill My covenant [upon you] that I will fulfill your covenant [from Me], and be afraid of [only] Me.

40

waāminū وَءَامِنُوا And believe bimā بِمَا in what anzaltu أَنْزَلْتُ I have sent down muṣaddiqan مُصَدِّقًا confirming limā لِمَا that which maʿakum مَعَكُمْ (is) with you walā وَلَا and (do) not takūnū تَكُونُوا be awwala أَوَّلَ (the) first kāfirin كَافِرٍ disbeliever bihi بِهِ of it walā وَلَا And (do) not tashtarū تَشْتَرُوا exchange biāyātī بِءَايَاتِي My Signs (for) thamanan ثَمَنًا a price qalīlan قَلِيلًا small wa-iyyāya وَإِيَّايَ and Me Alone fa-ittaqūni فَاتَّقُونِ fear [Me]

41

41.

And believe in what I have sent down confirming that which is [already] with you, and be not the first to disbelieve in it. And do not exchange My signs for a small price, and fear [only] Me.

41

walā وَلَا And (do) not talbisū تَلْبِسُوا mix l-ḥaqa الْحَقَّ the Truth bil-bāṭili بِالْبَاطِلِ with [the] falsehood wataktumū وَتَكْتُمُوا and conceal l-ḥaqa الْحَقَّ the Truth wa-antum وَأَنْتُمْ while you taʿlamūna تَعْلَمُونَ [you] know

42

42.

And do not mix the truth with falsehood or conceal the truth while you know [it].

42

wa-aqīmū وَأَقِيمُوا And establish l-ṣalata الصَّلَوةَ the prayer waātū وَءَاتُوا and give l-zakata الزَّكَوةَ zakah wa-ir'kaʿū وَارْكَعُوا and bow down maʿa مَعَ with l-rākiʿīna الرَّاكِعِينَ those who bow down

43

43.

And establish prayer and give zakah and bow with those who bow [in worship and obedience].

43

atamurūna أَتَأْمُرُونَ Do you order l-nāsa النَّاسَ [the] people bil-biri بِالْبِرِّ [the] righteousness watansawna وَتَنْسَوْنَ and you forget anfusakum أَنْفُسَكُمْ yourselves wa-antum وَأَنْتُمْ while you tatlūna تَتْلُونَ [you] recite l-kitāba الْكِتَابَ the Book afalā أَفَلَا Then will not taʿqilūna تَعْقِلُونَ you use reason

44

44.

Do you order righteousness of the people and forget yourselves while you recite the Scripture? Then will you not reason?

44

wa-is'taʿīnū وَاسْتَعِينُوا And seek help bil-ṣabri بِالصَّبْرِ through patience wal-ṣalati وَالصَّلَوةِ and the prayer wa-innahā وَإِنَّهَا and indeed it lakabīratun لَكَبِيرَةٌ (is) surely difficult illā إِلَّا except ʿalā عَلَى on l-khāshiʿīna الْخَاشِعِينَ the humble ones

45

45.

And seek help through patience and prayer, and indeed, it is difficult except for the humbly submissive [to Allah]

45

alladhīna الَّذِينَ Those who yaẓunnūna يَظُنُّونَ believe annahum أَنَّهُمْ that they mulāqū مُلَاقُوا will meet rabbihim رَبِّهِمْ their Lord wa-annahum وَأَنَّهُمْ and that they ilayhi إِلَيْهِ to Him rājiʿūna رَاجِعُونَ will return

46

46.

Who are certain that they will meet their Lord and that they will return to Him.

46

yābanī يَابَنِي O Children is'rāīla إِسْرَاءِيلَ (of) Israel! udh'kurū اذْكُرُوا Remember niʿ'matiya نِعْمَتِيَ My Favor allatī الَّتِي which anʿamtu أَنْعَمْتُ I bestowed ʿalaykum عَلَيْكُمْ upon you wa-annī وَأَنِّي and that I faḍḍaltukum فَضَّلْتُكُمْ [I] preferred you ʿalā عَلَى over l-ʿālamīna الْعَالَمِينَ the worlds

47

47.

O Children of Israel, remember My favor that I have bestowed upon you and that I preferred you over the worlds.

47

wa-ittaqū وَاتَّقُوا And fear yawman يَوْمًا a day lā لَا (will) not tajzī تَجْزِي avail nafsun نَفْسٌ any soul ʿan عَنْ for nafsin نَفْسٍ (another) soul shayan شَيْئًا anything walā وَلَا and not yuq'balu يُقْبَلُ will be accepted min'hā مِنْهَا from it shafāʿatun شَفَاعَةٌ any intercession walā وَلَا and not yu'khadhu يُؤْخَذُ will be taken min'hā مِنْهَا from it ʿadlun عَدْلٌ a compensation walā وَلَا and not hum هُمْ they yunṣarūna يُنْصَرُونَ will be helped

48

48.

And fear a Day when no soul will suffice for another soul at all, nor will intercession be accepted from it, nor will compensation be taken from it, nor will they be aided.

48

wa-idh وَإِذْ And when najjaynākum نَجَّيْنَاكُمْ We saved you min مِنْ from āli ءَالِ (the) people fir'ʿawna فِرْعَوْنَ (of) Firaun yasūmūnakum يَسُومُونَكُمْ (who were) afflicting you (with) sūa سُوءَ horrible l-ʿadhābi الْعَذَابِ torment yudhabbiḥūna يُذَبِّحُونَ slaughtering abnāakum أَبْنَاءَكُمْ your sons wayastaḥyūna وَيَسْتَحْيُونَ and letting live nisāakum نِسَاءَكُمْ your women wafī وَفِي And in dhālikum ذَلِكُمْ that balāon بَلَاءٌ (was) a trial min مِنْ from rabbikum رَبِّكُمْ your Lord ʿaẓīmun عَظِيمٌ great

49

49.

And [recall] when We saved your forefathers from the people of Pharaoh, who afflicted you with the worst torment, slaughtering your [newborn] sons and keeping your females alive. And in that was a great trial from your Lord.

49

wa-idh وَإِذْ And when faraqnā فَرَقْنَا We parted bikumu بِكُمُ for you l-baḥra الْبَحْرَ the sea fa-anjaynākum فَأَنْجَيْنَاكُمْ then We saved you wa-aghraqnā وَأَغْرَقْنَا and We drowned āla ءَالَ (the) people fir'ʿawna فِرْعَوْنَ (of) Firaun wa-antum وَأَنْتُمْ while you tanẓurūna تَنْظُرُونَ (were) looking

50

50.

And [recall] when We parted the sea for you and saved you and drowned the people of Pharaoh while you were looking on.

50

wa-idh وَإِذْ And when wāʿadnā وَاعَدْنَا We appointed mūsā مُوسَى (for) Musa arbaʿīna أَرْبَعِينَ forty laylatan لَيْلَةً nights thumma ثُمَّ Then ittakhadhtumu اتَّخَذْتُمُ you took l-ʿij'la الْعِجْلَ the calf min مِنْ from baʿdihi بَعْدِهِ after him wa-antum وَأَنْتُمْ and you ẓālimūna ظَالِمُونَ (were) wrongdoers

51

51.

And [recall] when We made an appointment with Moses for forty nights. Then you took [for worship] the calf after him, while you were wrongdoers.

51

thumma ثُمَّ Then ʿafawnā عَفَوْنَا We forgave ʿankum عَنْكُمْ you min مِنْ from baʿdi بَعْدِ after dhālika ذَلِكَ that laʿallakum لَعَلَّكُمْ so that you may tashkurūna تَشْكُرُونَ (be) grateful

52

52.

Then We forgave you after that so perhaps you would be grateful.

52

wa-idh وَإِذْ And when ātaynā ءَاتَيْنَا We gave mūsā مُوسَى Musa l-kitāba الْكِتَابَ the Book wal-fur'qāna وَالْفُرْقَانَ and the Criterion laʿallakum لَعَلَّكُمْ perhaps you tahtadūna تَهْتَدُونَ (would be) guided

53

53.

And [recall] when We gave Moses the Scripture and criterion that perhaps you would be guided.

53

wa-idh وَإِذْ And when qāla قَالَ said mūsā مُوسَى Musa liqawmihi لِقَوْمِهِ to his people yāqawmi يَاقَوْمِ O my people! innakum إِنَّكُمْ Indeed you ẓalamtum ظَلَمْتُمْ [you] have wronged anfusakum أَنْفُسَكُمْ yourselves bi-ittikhādhikumu بِاتِّخَاذِكُمُ by your taking l-ʿij'la الْعِجْلَ the calf fatūbū فَتُوبُوا So turn in repentance ilā إِلَى to bāri-ikum بَارِئِكُمْ your Creator fa-uq'tulū فَاقْتُلُوا and kill anfusakum أَنْفُسَكُمْ yourselves dhālikum ذَلِكُمْ That khayrun خَيْرٌ (is) better lakum لَكُمْ for you ʿinda عِنْدَ with bāri-ikum بَارِئِكُمْ your Creator fatāba فَتَابَ Then He turned ʿalaykum عَلَيْكُمْ towards you innahu إِنَّهُ Indeed He! huwa هُوَ He l-tawābu التَّوَّابُ (is) the Oft-returning l-raḥīmu الرَّحِيمُ the Most Merciful

54

54.

And [recall] when Moses said to his people, "O my people, indeed you have wronged yourselves by your taking of the calf [for worship]. So repent to your Creator and kill yourselves. That is best for [all of] you in the sight of your Creator." Then He accepted your repentance; indeed, He is the Accepting of repentance, the Merciful.

54

wa-idh وَإِذْ And when qul'tum قُلْتُمْ you said yāmūsā يَامُوسَى O Musa lan لَنْ Never nu'mina نُؤْمِنَ (will) we believe laka لَكَ in you ḥattā حَتَّى until narā نَرَى we see l-laha اللَّهَ Allah jahratan جَهْرَةً manifestly fa-akhadhatkumu فَأَخَذَتْكُمُ So seized you l-ṣāʿiqatu الصَّاعِقَةُ the thunderbolt wa-antum وَأَنْتُمْ while you tanẓurūna تَنْظُرُونَ (were) looking

55

55.

And [recall] when you said, "O Moses, we will never believe you until we see Allah outright"; so the thunderbolt took you while you were looking on.

55

thumma ثُمَّ Then baʿathnākum بَعَثْنَاكُمْ We revived you min مِنْ from baʿdi بَعْدِ after mawtikum مَوْتِكُمْ your death laʿallakum لَعَلَّكُمْ so that you may tashkurūna تَشْكُرُونَ (be) grateful

56

56.

Then We revived you after your death that perhaps you would be grateful.

56

waẓallalnā وَظَلَّلْنَا And We shaded ʿalaykumu عَلَيْكُمُ [over] you l-ghamāma الْغَمَامَ (with) [the] clouds wa-anzalnā وَأَنْزَلْنَا and We sent down ʿalaykumu عَلَيْكُمُ to you l-mana الْمَنَّ [the] manna wal-salwā وَالسَّلْوَى and [the] quails kulū كُلُوا Eat min مِنْ from ṭayyibāti طَيِّبَاتِ (the) good things mā مَا that razaqnākum رَزَقْنَاكُمْ We have provided you wamā وَمَا And not ẓalamūnā ظَلَمُونَا they wronged Us walākin وَلَكِنْ but kānū كَانُوا they were anfusahum أَنْفُسَهُمْ (to) themselves yaẓlimūna يَظْلِمُونَ doing wrong

57

57.

And We shaded you with clouds and sent down to you manna and quails, [saying], "Eat from the good things with which We have provided you." And they wronged Us not - but they were [only] wronging themselves.

57

wa-idh وَإِذْ And when qul'nā قُلْنَا We said ud'khulū ادْخُلُوا Enter hādhihi هَذِهِ this l-qaryata الْقَرْيَةَ town fakulū فَكُلُوا then eat min'hā مِنْهَا from [it] ḥaythu حَيْثُ wherever shi'tum شِئْتُمْ you wish[ed] raghadan رَغَدًا abundantly wa-ud'khulū وَادْخُلُوا and enter l-bāba الْبَابَ the gate sujjadan سُجَّدًا prostrating waqūlū وَقُولُوا And say ḥiṭṭatun حِطَّةٌ Repentance naghfir نَغْفِرْ We will forgive lakum لَكُمْ for you khaṭāyākum خَطَايَاكُمْ your sins wasanazīdu وَسَنَزِيدُ And We will increase l-muḥ'sinīna الْمُحْسِنِينَ the good-doers (in reward)

58

58.

And [recall] when We said, "Enter this city and eat from it wherever you will in [ease and] abundance, and enter the gate bowing humbly and say, 'Relieve us of our burdens.' We will [then] forgive your sins for you, and We will increase the doers of good [in goodness and reward]."

58

fabaddala فَبَدَّلَ But changed alladhīna الَّذِينَ those who ẓalamū ظَلَمُوا wronged qawlan قَوْلًا (the) word ghayra غَيْرَ other (than) alladhī الَّذِي that which qīla قِيلَ was said lahum لَهُمْ to them fa-anzalnā فَأَنْزَلْنَا so We sent down ʿalā عَلَى upon alladhīna الَّذِينَ those who ẓalamū ظَلَمُوا wronged rij'zan رِجْزًا a punishment mina مِنَ from l-samāi السَّمَاءِ the sky bimā بِمَا because kānū كَانُوا they were yafsuqūna يَفْسُقُونَ defiantly disobeying

59

59.

But those who wronged changed [those words] to a statement other than that which had been said to them, so We sent down upon those who wronged a punishment from the sky because they were defiantly disobeying.

59

wa-idhi وَإِذِ And when is'tasqā اسْتَسْقَى asked (for) water mūsā مُوسَى Musa liqawmihi لِقَوْمِهِ for his people faqul'nā فَقُلْنَا [so] We said iḍ'rib اضْرِبْ Strike biʿaṣāka بِعَصَاكَ with your staff l-ḥajara الْحَجَرَ the stone fa-infajarat فَانْفَجَرَتْ Then gushed forth min'hu مِنْهُ from it ith'natā اثْنَتَا (of) ʿashrata عَشْرَةَ twelve ʿaynan عَيْنًا springs qad قَدْ Indeed ʿalima عَلِمَ knew kullu كُلُّ all unāsin أُنَاسٍ (the) people mashrabahum مَشْرَبَهُمْ their drinking place kulū كُلُوا Eat wa-ish'rabū وَاشْرَبُوا and drink min مِنْ from riz'qi رِزْقِ (the) provision (of) l-lahi اللَّهِ Allah walā وَلَا and (do) not taʿthaw تَعْثَوْا act wickedly fī فِي in l-arḍi الْأَرْضِ the earth muf'sidīna مُفْسِدِينَ spreading corruption

60

60.

And [recall] when Moses prayed for water for his people, so We said, "Strike with your staff the stone." And there gushed forth from it twelve springs, and every people knew its watering place. "Eat and drink from the provision of Allah, and do not commit abuse on the earth, spreading corruption."

60

wa-idh وَإِذْ And when qul'tum قُلْتُمْ you said yāmūsā يَامُوسَى O Musa lan لَنْ Never (will) naṣbira نَصْبِرَ we endure ʿalā عَلَى [on] ṭaʿāmin طَعَامٍ food wāḥidin وَاحِدٍ (of) one (kind) fa-ud'ʿu فَادْعُ so pray lanā لَنَا for us rabbaka رَبَّكَ (to) your Lord yukh'rij يُخْرِجْ to bring forth lanā لَنَا for us mimmā مِمَّا out of what tunbitu تُنْبِتُ grows l-arḍu الْأَرْضُ the earth min مِنْ of baqlihā بَقْلِهَا its herbs waqithāihā وَقِثَّائِهَا [and] its cucumbers wafūmihā وَفُومِهَا [and] its garlic waʿadasihā وَعَدَسِهَا [and] its lentils wabaṣalihā وَبَصَلِهَا and its onions qāla قَالَ He said atastabdilūna أَتَسْتَبْدِلُونَ Would you exchange alladhī الَّذِي that which huwa هُوَ [it] adnā أَدْنَى (is) inferior bi-alladhī بِالَّذِي for that which huwa هُوَ [it] khayrun خَيْرٌ (is) better ih'biṭū اهْبِطُوا Go down miṣ'ran مِصْرًا (to) a city fa-inna فَإِنَّ so indeed lakum لَكُمْ for you mā مَا (is) what sa-altum سَأَلْتُمْ you have asked (for) waḍuribat وَضُرِبَتْ And were struck ʿalayhimu عَلَيْهِمُ on them l-dhilatu الذِّلَّةُ the humiliation wal-maskanatu وَالْمَسْكَنَةُ and the misery wabāū وَبَاءُو and they drew on themselves bighaḍabin بِغَضَبٍ wrath mina مِنَ of l-lahi اللَّهِ Allah dhālika ذَلِكَ That (was) bi-annahum بِأَنَّهُمْ because they kānū كَانُوا used to yakfurūna يَكْفُرُونَ disbelieve biāyāti بِءَايَاتِ in (the) Signs l-lahi اللَّهِ (of) Allah wayaqtulūna وَيَقْتُلُونَ and kill l-nabiyīna النَّبِيِّينَ the Prophets bighayri بِغَيْرِ without (any) l-ḥaqi الْحَقِّ [the] right dhālika ذَلِكَ That bimā بِمَا (was) because ʿaṣaw عَصَوْا they disobeyed wakānū وَكَانُوا and they were yaʿtadūna يَعْتَدُونَ transgressing

61

61.

And [recall] when you said, "O Moses, we can never endure one [kind of] food. So call upon your Lord to bring forth for us from the earth its green herbs and its cucumbers and its garlic and its lentils and its onions." [Moses] said, "Would you exchange what is better for what is less? Go into [any] settlement and indeed, you will have what you have asked." And they were covered with humiliation and poverty and returned with anger from Allah [upon them]. That was because they [repeatedly] disbelieved in the signs of Allah and killed the prophets without right. That was because they disobeyed and were [habitually] transgressing.

61

inna إِنَّ Indeed alladhīna الَّذِينَ those who āmanū ءَامَنُوا believed wa-alladhīna وَالَّذِينَ and those who hādū هَادُوا became Jews wal-naṣārā وَالنَّصَارَى and the Christians wal-ṣābiīna وَالصَّابِءِينَ and the Sabians man مَنْ who āmana ءَامَنَ believed bil-lahi بِاللَّهِ in Allah wal-yawmi وَالْيَوْمِ and the Day l-ākhiri الْءَاخِرِ [the] Last waʿamila وَعَمِلَ and did ṣāliḥan صَالِحًا righteous deeds falahum فَلَهُمْ so for them ajruhum أَجْرُهُمْ (is) their reward ʿinda عِنْدَ with rabbihim رَبِّهِمْ their Lord walā وَلَا and no khawfun خَوْفٌ fear ʿalayhim عَلَيْهِمْ on them walā وَلَا and not hum هُمْ they yaḥzanūna يَحْزَنُونَ will grieve

62

62.

Indeed, those who believed and those who were Jews or Christians or Sabeans [before Prophet Muhammad] - those [among them] who believed in Allah and the Last Day and did righteousness - will have their reward with their Lord, and no fear will there be concerning them, nor will they grieve.

62

wa-idh وَإِذْ And when akhadhnā أَخَذْنَا We took mīthāqakum مِيثَاقَكُمْ your covenant warafaʿnā وَرَفَعْنَا and We raised fawqakumu فَوْقَكُمُ over you l-ṭūra الطُّورَ the mount khudhū خُذُوا Hold mā مَا what ātaynākum ءَاتَيْنَاكُمْ We have given you biquwwatin بِقُوَّةٍ with strength wa-udh'kurū وَاذْكُرُوا and remember mā مَا what fīhi فِيهِ (is) in it laʿallakum لَعَلَّكُمْ perhaps you tattaqūna تَتَّقُونَ (would become) righteous

63

63.

And [recall] when We took your covenant, [O Children of Israel, to abide by the Torah] and We raised over you the mount, [saying], "Take what We have given you with determination and remember what is in it that perhaps you may become righteous."

63

thumma ثُمَّ Then tawallaytum تَوَلَّيْتُمْ you turned away min مِنْ from baʿdi بَعْدِ after dhālika ذَلِكَ that falawlā فَلَوْلَا So if not faḍlu فَضْلُ (for the) Grace l-lahi اللَّهِ (of) Allah ʿalaykum عَلَيْكُمْ upon you waraḥmatuhu وَرَحْمَتُهُ and His Mercy lakuntum لَكُنْتُمْ surely you would have been mina مِنَ of l-khāsirīna الْخَاسِرِينَ the losers

64

64.

Then you turned away after that. And if not for the favor of Allah upon you and His mercy, you would have been among the losers.

64

walaqad وَلَقَدْ And indeed ʿalim'tumu عَلِمْتُمُ you knew alladhīna الَّذِينَ those who iʿ'tadaw اعْتَدَوْا transgressed minkum مِنْكُمْ among you fī فِي in l-sabti السَّبْتِ the (matter of) Sabbath faqul'nā فَقُلْنَا So We said lahum لَهُمْ to them kūnū كُونُوا Be qiradatan قِرَدَةً apes khāsiīna خَاسِئِينَ despised

65

65.

And you had already known about those who transgressed among you concerning the sabbath, and We said to them, "Be apes, despised."

65

fajaʿalnāhā فَجَعَلْنَاهَا So We made it nakālan نَكَالًا a deterrent punishment limā لِمَا for those bayna بَيْنَ (in) front yadayhā يَدَيْهَا (of) them wamā وَمَا and those khalfahā خَلْفَهَا after them wamawʿiẓatan وَمَوْعِظَةً and an admonition lil'muttaqīna لِلْمُتَّقِينَ for those who fear (Allah)

66

66.

And We made it a deterrent punishment for those who were present and those who succeeded [them] and a lesson for those who fear Allah.

66

wa-idh وَإِذْ And when qāla قَالَ said mūsā مُوسَى Musa liqawmihi لِقَوْمِهِ to his people inna إِنَّ Indeed l-laha اللَّهَ Allah yamurukum يَأْمُرُكُمْ commands you an أَنْ that tadhbaḥū تَذْبَحُوا you slaughter baqaratan بَقَرَةً a cow qālū قَالُوا They said atattakhidhunā أَتَتَّخِذُنَا Do you take us huzuwan هُزُوًا (in) ridicule qāla قَالَ He said aʿūdhu أَعُوذُ I seek refuge bil-lahi بِاللَّهِ in Allah an أَنْ that akūna أَكُونَ I be mina مِنَ among l-jāhilīna الْجَاهِلِينَ the ignorant

67

67.

And [recall] when Moses said to his people, "Indeed, Allah commands you to slaughter a cow." They said, "Do you take us in ridicule?" He said, "I seek refuge in Allah from being among the ignorant."

67

qālū قَالُوا They said ud'ʿu ادْعُ Pray lanā لَنَا for us rabbaka رَبَّكَ (to) your Lord yubayyin يُبَيِّنْ to make clear lanā لَنَا to us mā مَا what hiya هِيَ it (is) qāla قَالَ He said innahu إِنَّهُ Indeed He yaqūlu يَقُولُ says innahā إِنَّهَا [Indeed] it baqaratun بَقَرَةٌ (is) a cow lā لَا not fāriḍun فَارِضٌ old walā وَلَا and not bik'run بِكْرٌ young ʿawānun عَوَانٌ middle aged bayna بَيْنَ between dhālika ذَلِكَ that fa-if'ʿalū فَافْعَلُوا so do mā مَا what tu'marūna تُؤْمَرُونَ you are commanded

68

68.

They said, "Call upon your Lord to make clear to us what it is." [Moses] said, "[Allah] says, 'It is a cow which is neither old nor virgin, but median between that,' so do what you are commanded."

68

qālū قَالُوا They said ud'ʿu ادْعُ Pray lanā لَنَا for us rabbaka رَبَّكَ (to) your Lord yubayyin يُبَيِّنْ to make clear lanā لَنَا to us mā مَا what lawnuhā لَوْنُهَا (is) its color qāla قَالَ He said innahu إِنَّهُ Indeed He yaqūlu يَقُولُ says innahā إِنَّهَا [Indeed] it is baqaratun بَقَرَةٌ a cow ṣafrāu صَفْرَاءُ yellow fāqiʿun فَاقِعٌ bright lawnuhā لَوْنُهَا (in) its color tasurru تَسُرُّ pleasing l-nāẓirīna النَّاظِرِينَ (to) those who see (it)

69

69.

They said, "Call upon your Lord to show us what is her color." He said, "He says, 'It is a yellow cow, bright in color - pleasing to the observers.' "

69

qālū قَالُوا They said ud'ʿu ادْعُ Pray lanā لَنَا for us rabbaka رَبَّكَ (to) your Lord yubayyin يُبَيِّنْ to make clear lanā لَنَا to us mā مَا what hiya هِيَ it (is) inna إِنَّ Indeed l-baqara الْبَقَرَ [the] cows tashābaha تَشَابَهَ look alike ʿalaynā عَلَيْنَا to us wa-innā وَإِنَّا And indeed we in إِنْ if shāa شَاءَ wills l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah lamuh'tadūna لَمُهْتَدُونَ (will) surely be those who are guided

70

70.

They said, "Call upon your Lord to make clear to us what it is. Indeed, [all] cows look alike to us. And indeed we, if Allah wills, will be guided."

70

qāla قَالَ He said innahu إِنَّهُ Indeed He yaqūlu يَقُولُ says innahā إِنَّهَا [Indeed] it baqaratun بَقَرَةٌ (is) a cow lā لَا not dhalūlun ذَلُولٌ trained tuthīru تُثِيرُ to plough l-arḍa الْأَرْضَ the earth walā وَلَا and not tasqī تَسْقِي water l-ḥartha الْحَرْثَ the field musallamatun مُسَلَّمَةٌ sound lā لَا no shiyata شِيَةَ blemish fīhā فِيهَا in it qālū قَالُوا They said l-āna الْءَانَ Now ji'ta جِئْتَ you have come bil-ḥaqi بِالْحَقِّ with the truth fadhabaḥūhā فَذَبَحُوهَا So they slaughtered it wamā وَمَا and not kādū كَادُوا they were near yafʿalūna يَفْعَلُونَ (to) doing (it)

71

71.

He said, "He says, 'It is a cow neither trained to plow the earth nor to irrigate the field, one free from fault with no spot upon her.' " They said, "Now you have come with the truth." So they slaughtered her, but they could hardly do it.

71

wa-idh وَإِذْ And when qataltum قَتَلْتُمْ you killed nafsan نَفْسًا a man fa-iddāratum فَادَّارَءْتُمْ then you disputed fīhā فِيهَا concerning it wal-lahu وَاللَّهُ but Allah mukh'rijun مُخْرِجٌ (is) the One Who brought forth mā مَا what kuntum كُنْتُمْ you were taktumūna تَكْتُمُونَ concealing

72

72.

And [recall] when you slew a man and disputed over it, but Allah was to bring out that which you were concealing.

72

faqul'nā فَقُلْنَا So We said iḍ'ribūhu اضْرِبُوهُ Strike him bibaʿḍihā بِبَعْضِهَا with a part of it kadhālika كَذَلِكَ Like this yuḥ'yī يُحْيِي revives l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah l-mawtā الْمَوْتَى the dead wayurīkum وَيُرِيكُمْ and shows you āyātihi ءَايَاتِهِ His Signs laʿallakum لَعَلَّكُمْ perhaps you may taʿqilūna تَعْقِلُونَ use your intellect

73

73.

So, We said, "Strike the slain man with part of it." Thus does Allah bring the dead to life, and He shows you His signs that you might reason.

73

thumma ثُمَّ Then qasat قَسَتْ hardened qulūbukum قُلُوبُكُمْ your hearts min مِنْ from baʿdi بَعْدِ after dhālika ذَلِكَ that fahiya فَهِيَ so they kal-ḥijārati كَالْحِجَارَةِ (became) like [the] stones aw أَوْ or ashaddu أَشَدُّ stronger qaswatan قَسْوَةً (in) hardness wa-inna وَإِنَّ And indeed mina مِنَ from l-ḥijārati الْحِجَارَةِ the stones lamā لَمَا certainly (there are some) which yatafajjaru يَتَفَجَّرُ gush forth min'hu مِنْهُ from it l-anhāru الْأَنْهَارُ [the] rivers wa-inna وَإِنَّ and indeed min'hā مِنْهَا from them lamā لَمَا certainly (there are some) which yashaqqaqu يَشَّقَّقُ split fayakhruju فَيَخْرُجُ so comes out min'hu مِنْهُ from it l-māu الْمَاءُ [the] water wa-inna وَإِنَّ and indeed min'hā مِنْهَا from them lamā لَمَا certainly (there are some) which yahbiṭu يَهْبِطُ fall down min مِنْ from khashyati خَشْيَةِ fear l-lahi اللَّهِ (of) Allah wamā وَمَا And not l-lahu اللَّهُ (is) Allah bighāfilin بِغَافِلٍ unaware ʿammā عَمَّا of what taʿmalūna تَعْمَلُونَ you do

74

74.

Then your hearts became hardened after that, being like stones or even harder. For indeed, there are stones from which rivers burst forth, and there are some of them that split open and water comes out, and there are some of them that fall down for fear of Allah. And Allah is not unaware of what you do.

74

afataṭmaʿūna أَفَتَطْمَعُونَ Do you hope an أَنْ that yu'minū يُؤْمِنُوا they will believe lakum لَكُمْ [for] you waqad وَقَدْ while indeed kāna كَانَ (there) has been farīqun فَرِيقٌ a party min'hum مِنْهُمْ of them yasmaʿūna يَسْمَعُونَ (who used to) hear kalāma كَلَامَ (the) words l-lahi اللَّهِ (of) Allah thumma ثُمَّ then yuḥarrifūnahu يُحَرِّفُونَهُ they distort it min مِنْ from baʿdi بَعْدِ after mā مَا [what] ʿaqalūhu عَقَلُوهُ they understood it wahum وَهُمْ while they yaʿlamūna يَعْلَمُونَ know

75

75.

Do you covet [the hope, O believers], that they would believe for you while a party of them used to hear the words of Allah and then distort the Torah after they had understood it while they were knowing?

75

wa-idhā وَإِذَا And when laqū لَقُوا they meet alladhīna الَّذِينَ those who āmanū ءَامَنُوا believe[d] qālū قَالُوا they say āmannā ءَامَنَّا We have believed wa-idhā وَإِذَا But when khalā خَلَا meet in private baʿḍuhum بَعْضُهُمْ some of them ilā إِلَى with baʿḍin بَعْضٍ some (others) qālū قَالُوا they say atuḥaddithūnahum أَتُحَدِّثُونَهُمْ Do you tell them bimā بِمَا what fataḥa فَتَحَ has l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah ʿalaykum عَلَيْكُمْ to you liyuḥājjūkum لِيُحَاجُّوكُمْ so that they argue with you bihi بِهِ therewith ʿinda عِنْدَ before rabbikum رَبِّكُمْ your Lord afalā أَفَلَا Then do (you) not taʿqilūna تَعْقِلُونَ understand

76

76.

And when they meet those who believe, they say, "We have believed"; but when they are alone with one another, they say, "Do you talk to them about what Allah has revealed to you so they can argue with you about it before your Lord?" Then will you not reason?

76

awalā أَوَلَا Do not yaʿlamūna يَعْلَمُونَ they know anna أَنَّ that l-laha اللَّهَ Allah yaʿlamu يَعْلَمُ knows mā مَا what yusirrūna يُسِرُّونَ they conceal wamā وَمَا and what yuʿ'linūna يُعْلِنُونَ they declare

77

77.

But do they not know that Allah knows what they conceal and what they declare?

77

wamin'hum وَمِنْهُمْ And among them ummiyyūna أُمِّيُّونَ (are) unlettered ones lā لَا (who) do not yaʿlamūna يَعْلَمُونَ know l-kitāba الْكِتَابَ the book illā إِلَّا except amāniyya أَمَانِيَّ wishful thinking wa-in وَإِنْ and not hum هُمْ they illā إِلَّا (do anything) except yaẓunnūna يَظُنُّونَ guess

78

78.

And among them are unlettered ones who do not know the Scripture except in wishful thinking, but they are only assuming.

78

fawaylun فَوَيْلٌ So woe lilladhīna لِلَّذِينَ to those who yaktubūna يَكْتُبُونَ write l-kitāba الْكِتَابَ the book bi-aydīhim بِأَيْدِيهِمْ with their (own) hands thumma ثُمَّ then yaqūlūna يَقُولُونَ they say hādhā هَذَا This min مِنْ (is) ʿindi عِنْدِ from l-lahi اللَّهِ Allah liyashtarū لِيَشْتَرُوا to barter bihi بِهِ with it thamanan ثَمَنًا (for) a price qalīlan قَلِيلًا little fawaylun فَوَيْلٌ So woe lahum لَهُمْ to them mimmā مِمَّا for what katabat كَتَبَتْ have written aydīhim أَيْدِيهِمْ their hands wawaylun وَوَيْلٌ and woe lahum لَهُمْ to them mimmā مِمَّا for what yaksibūna يَكْسِبُونَ they earn

79

79.

So woe to those who write the "scripture" with their own hands, then say, "This is from Allah," in order to exchange it for a small price. Woe to them for what their hands have written and woe to them for what they earn.

79

waqālū وَقَالُوا And they say lan لَنْ Never tamassanā تَمَسَّنَا will touch us l-nāru النَّارُ the Fire illā إِلَّا except ayyāman أَيَّامًا (for) days maʿdūdatan مَعْدُودَةً numbered qul قُلْ Say attakhadhtum أَتَّخَذْتُمْ Have you taken ʿinda عِنْدَ from l-lahi اللَّهِ Allah ʿahdan عَهْدًا a covenant falan فَلَنْ so never yukh'lifa يُخْلِفَ will break l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah ʿahdahu عَهْدَهُ His Covenant am أَمْ Or taqūlūna تَقُولُونَ (do) you say ʿalā عَلَى against l-lahi اللَّهِ Allah mā مَا what lā لَا not taʿlamūna تَعْلَمُونَ you know

80

80.

And they say, "Never will the Fire touch us, except for a few days." Say, "Have you taken a covenant with Allah? For Allah will never break His covenant. Or do you say about Allah that which you do not know?"

80

balā بَلَى Yes man مَنْ whoever kasaba كَسَبَ earned sayyi-atan سَيِّئَةً evil wa-aḥāṭat وَأَحَاطَتْ and surrounded him bihi بِهِ with khaṭīatuhu خَطِيءَتُهُ his sins fa-ulāika فَأُولَئِكَ [so] those aṣḥābu أَصْحَابُ (are the) companions l-nāri النَّارِ (of) the Fire hum هُمْ they fīhā فِيهَا in it khālidūna خَالِدُونَ (will) abide forever

81

81.

Yes, whoever earns evil and his sin has encompassed him - those are the companions of the Fire; they will abide therein eternally.

81

wa-alladhīna وَالَّذِينَ And those who āmanū ءَامَنُوا believed waʿamilū وَعَمِلُوا and did l-ṣāliḥāti الصَّالِحَاتِ righteous deeds ulāika أُولَئِكَ those aṣḥābu أَصْحَابُ (are the) companions l-janati الْجَنَّةِ (of) Paradise hum هُمْ they fīhā فِيهَا in it khālidūna خَالِدُونَ (will) abide forever

82

82.

But they who believe and do righteous deeds - those are the companions of Paradise; they will abide therein eternally.

82

wa-idh وَإِذْ And when akhadhnā أَخَذْنَا We took mīthāqa مِيثَاقَ (the) covenant banī بَنِي (from the) Children is'rāīla إِسْرَاءِيلَ (of) Israel lā لَا Not taʿbudūna تَعْبُدُونَ you will worship illā إِلَّا except l-laha اللَّهَ Allah wabil-wālidayni وَبِالْوَالِدَيْنِ and with [the] parents iḥ'sānan إِحْسَانًا (be) good wadhī وَذِي and (with) l-qur'bā الْقُرْبَى relatives wal-yatāmā وَالْيَتَامَى and [the] orphans wal-masākīni وَالْمَسَاكِينِ and the needy waqūlū وَقُولُوا and speak lilnnāsi لِلنَّاسِ to [the] people ḥus'nan حُسْنًا good wa-aqīmū وَأَقِيمُوا and establish l-ṣalata الصَّلَوةَ the prayer waātū وَءَاتُوا and give l-zakata الزَّكَوةَ the zakah thumma ثُمَّ Then tawallaytum تَوَلَّيْتُمْ you turned away illā إِلَّا except qalīlan قَلِيلًا a few minkum مِنْكُمْ of you wa-antum وَأَنْتُمْ and you (were) muʿ'riḍūna مُعْرِضُونَ refusing

83

83.

And [recall] when We took the covenant from the Children of Israel, [enjoining upon them], "Do not worship except Allah; and to parents do good and to relatives, orphans, and the needy. And speak to people good [words] and establish prayer and give zakah." Then you turned away, except a few of you, and you were refusing.

83

wa-idh وَإِذْ And when akhadhnā أَخَذْنَا We took mīthāqakum مِيثَاقَكُمْ your covenant lā لَا Not tasfikūna تَسْفِكُونَ will you shed dimāakum دِمَاءَكُمْ your blood walā وَلَا and not tukh'rijūna تُخْرِجُونَ (will) evict anfusakum أَنْفُسَكُمْ yourselves min مِنْ from diyārikum دِيَارِكُمْ your homes thumma ثُمَّ then aqrartum أَقْرَرْتُمْ you ratified wa-antum وَأَنْتُمْ while you tashhadūna تَشْهَدُونَ (were) witnessing

84

84.

And [recall] when We took your covenant, [saying], "Do not shed each other's blood or evict one another from your homes." Then you acknowledged [this] while you were witnessing.

84

thumma ثُمَّ Then antum أَنْتُمْ you hāulāi هَؤُلَاءِ (are) those taqtulūna تَقْتُلُونَ (who) kill anfusakum أَنْفُسَكُمْ yourselves watukh'rijūna وَتُخْرِجُونَ and evict farīqan فَرِيقًا a party minkum مِنْكُمْ of you min مِنْ from diyārihim دِيَارِهِمْ their homes taẓāharūna تَظَاهَرُونَ you support one another ʿalayhim عَلَيْهِمْ against them bil-ith'mi بِالْإِثْمِ in sin wal-ʿud'wāni وَالْعُدْوَانِ and [the] transgression wa-in وَإِنْ And if yatūkum يَأْتُوكُمْ they come to you usārā أُسَارَى (as) captives tufādūhum تُفَادُوهُمْ you ransom them wahuwa وَهُوَ while it muḥarramun مُحَرَّمٌ (was) forbidden ʿalaykum عَلَيْكُمْ to you ikh'rājuhum إِخْرَاجُهُمْ their eviction afatu'minūna أَفَتُؤْمِنُونَ So do you believe bibaʿḍi بِبَعْضِ in part (of) l-kitābi الْكِتَابِ the Book watakfurūna وَتَكْفُرُونَ and disbelieve bibaʿḍin بِبَعْضٍ in part famā فَمَا Then what jazāu جَزَاءُ (should be the) recompense man مَنْ (for the one) who yafʿalu يَفْعَلُ does dhālika ذَلِكَ that minkum مِنْكُمْ among you illā إِلَّا except khiz'yun خِزْيٌ disgrace fī فِي in l-ḥayati الْحَيَوةِ the life l-dun'yā الدُّنْيَا (of) the world wayawma وَيَوْمَ and (on the) Day l-qiyāmati الْقِيَامَةِ of [the] Resurrection yuraddūna يُرَدُّونَ they will be sent back ilā إِلَى to ashaddi أَشَدِّ (the) most severe l-ʿadhābi الْعَذَابِ punishment wamā وَمَا And not l-lahu اللَّهُ (is) Allah bighāfilin بِغَافِلٍ unaware ʿammā عَمَّا of what taʿmalūna تَعْمَلُونَ you do

85

85.

Then, you are those [same ones who are] killing one another and evicting a party of your people from their homes, cooperating against them in sin and aggression. And if they come to you as captives, you ransom them, although their eviction was forbidden to you. So do you believe in part of the Scripture and disbelieve in part? Then what is the recompense for those who do that among you except disgrace in worldly life; and on the Day of Resurrection they will be sent back to the severest of punishment. And Allah is not unaware of what you do.

85

ulāika أُولَئِكَ Those alladhīna الَّذِينَ (are) the ones who ish'tarawū اشْتَرَوُا bought l-ḥayata الْحَيَوةَ the life l-dun'yā الدُّنْيَا (of) the world bil-ākhirati بِالْءَاخِرَةِ for the Hereafter falā فَلَا so not yukhaffafu يُخَفَّفُ will be lightened ʿanhumu عَنْهُمُ for them l-ʿadhābu الْعَذَابُ the punishment walā وَلَا and not hum هُمْ they yunṣarūna يُنْصَرُونَ will be helped

86

86.

Those are the ones who have bought the life of this world [in exchange] for the Hereafter, so the punishment will not be lightened for them, nor will they be aided.

86

walaqad وَلَقَدْ And indeed ātaynā ءَاتَيْنَا We gave mūsā مُوسَى Musa l-kitāba الْكِتَابَ the Book waqaffaynā وَقَفَّيْنَا and We followed up min مِنْ from baʿdihi بَعْدِهِ after him bil-rusuli بِالرُّسُلِ with [the] Messengers waātaynā وَءَاتَيْنَا And We gave ʿīsā عِيسَى Isa ib'na ابْنَ (the) son maryama مَرْيَمَ (of) Maryam l-bayināti الْبَيِّنَاتِ [the] clear signs wa-ayyadnāhu وَأَيَّدْنَاهُ and We supported him birūḥi بِرُوحِ (with) l-qudusi الْقُدُسِ the Holy Spirit afakullamā أَفَكُلَّمَا Is it (not) so (that) whenever jāakum جَاءَكُمْ came to you rasūlun رَسُولٌ a Messenger bimā بِمَا with what lā لَا (does) not tahwā تَهْوَى desire anfusukumu أَنْفُسُكُمُ yourselves is'takbartum اسْتَكْبَرْتُمْ you acted arrogantly fafarīqan فَفَرِيقًا So a party kadhabtum كَذَّبْتُمْ you denied wafarīqan وَفَرِيقًا and a party taqtulūna تَقْتُلُونَ you kill(ed)

87

87.

And We did certainly give Moses the Torah and followed up after him with messengers. And We gave Jesus, the son of Mary, clear proofs and supported him with the Pure Spirit. But is it [not] that every time a messenger came to you, [O Children of Israel], with what your souls did not desire, you were arrogant? And a party [of messengers] you denied and another party you killed.

87

waqālū وَقَالُوا And they said qulūbunā قُلُوبُنَا Our hearts ghul'fun غُلْفٌ (are) wrapped bal بَلْ Nay laʿanahumu لَعَنَهُمُ has cursed them l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah bikuf'rihim بِكُفْرِهِمْ for their disbelief faqalīlan فَقَلِيلًا so little mā مَا (is) what yu'minūna يُؤْمِنُونَ they believe

88

88.

And they said, "Our hearts are wrapped." But, [in fact], Allah has cursed them for their disbelief, so little is it that they believe.

88

walammā وَلَمَّا And when jāahum جَاءَهُمْ came to them kitābun كِتَابٌ a Book min مِنْ of ʿindi عِنْدِ from l-lahi اللَّهِ Allah muṣaddiqun مُصَدِّقٌ confirming limā لِمَا what (was) maʿahum مَعَهُمْ with them wakānū وَكَانُوا though they used to min مِنْ from qablu قَبْلُ before yastaftiḥūna يَسْتَفْتِحُونَ (that), pray for victory ʿalā عَلَى over alladhīna الَّذِينَ those who kafarū كَفَرُوا disbelieved falammā فَلَمَّا then when jāahum جَاءَهُمْ came to them mā مَا what ʿarafū عَرَفُوا they recognized kafarū كَفَرُوا they disbelieved bihi بِهِ in it falaʿnatu فَلَعْنَةُ So (the) curse l-lahi اللَّهِ (of) Allah ʿalā عَلَى (is) on l-kāfirīna الْكَافِرِينَ the disbelievers

89

89.

And when there came to them a Book from Allah confirming that which was with them - although before they used to pray for victory against those who disbelieved - but [then] when there came to them that which they recognized, they disbelieved in it; so the curse of Allah will be upon the disbelievers.

89

bi'samā بِئْسَمَا Evil (is) that ish'taraw اشْتَرَوْا (for) which they have sold bihi بِهِ with anfusahum أَنْفُسَهُمْ themselves an أَنْ that yakfurū يَكْفُرُوا they disbelieve bimā بِمَا in what anzala أَنْزَلَ has revealed l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah baghyan بَغْيًا grudging an أَنْ that yunazzila يُنَزِّلَ sends down l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah min مِنْ of faḍlihi فَضْلِهِ His Grace ʿalā عَلَى on man مَنْ whom yashāu يَشَاءُ He wills min مِنْ from ʿibādihi عِبَادِهِ His servants fabāū فَبَاءُو So they have drawn (on themselves) bighaḍabin بِغَضَبٍ wrath ʿalā عَلَى upon ghaḍabin غَضَبٍ wrath walil'kāfirīna وَلِلْكَافِرِينَ And for the disbelievers ʿadhābun عَذَابٌ (is) a punishment muhīnun مُهِينٌ humiliating

90

90.

How wretched is that for which they sold themselves - that they would disbelieve in what Allah has revealed through [their] outrage that Allah would send down His favor upon whom He wills from among His servants. So they returned having [earned] wrath upon wrath. And for the disbelievers is a humiliating punishment.

90

wa-idhā وَإِذَا And when qīla قِيلَ it is said lahum لَهُمْ to them āminū ءَامِنُوا Believe bimā بِمَا in what anzala أَنْزَلَ has revealed l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah qālū قَالُوا they say nu'minu نُؤْمِنُ We believe bimā بِمَا in what unzila أُنْزِلَ was revealed ʿalaynā عَلَيْنَا to us wayakfurūna وَيَكْفُرُونَ And they disbelieve bimā بِمَا in what warāahu وَرَاءَهُ (is) besides it wahuwa وَهُوَ while it l-ḥaqu الْحَقُّ (is) the truth muṣaddiqan مُصَدِّقًا confirming limā لِمَا what maʿahum مَعَهُمْ (is) with them qul قُلْ Say falima فَلِمَ Then why taqtulūna تَقْتُلُونَ (did) you kill anbiyāa أَنْبِيَاءَ (the) Prophets l-lahi اللَّهِ (of) Allah min مِنْ from qablu قَبْلُ before in إِنْ if kuntum كُنْتُمْ you were mu'minīna مُؤْمِنِينَ believers

91

91.

And when it is said to them, "Believe in what Allah has revealed," they say, "We believe [only] in what was revealed to us." And they disbelieve in what came after it, while it is the truth confirming that which is with them. Say, "Then why did you kill the prophets of Allah before, if you are [indeed] believers?"

91

walaqad وَلَقَدْ And indeed jāakum جَاءَكُمْ came to you mūsā مُوسَى Musa bil-bayināti بِالْبَيِّنَاتِ with [the] clear signs thumma ثُمَّ then ittakhadhtumu اتَّخَذْتُمُ you took l-ʿij'la الْعِجْلَ the calf min مِنْ from baʿdihi بَعْدِهِ after him wa-antum وَأَنْتُمْ and you ẓālimūna ظَالِمُونَ (were) wrongdoers

92

92.

And Moses had certainly brought you clear proofs. Then you took the calf [in worship] after that, while you were wrongdoers.

92

wa-idh وَإِذْ And when akhadhnā أَخَذْنَا We took mīthāqakum مِيثَاقَكُمْ your covenant warafaʿnā وَرَفَعْنَا and We raised fawqakumu فَوْقَكُمُ over you l-ṭūra الطُّورَ the mount khudhū خُذُوا Hold mā مَا what ātaynākum ءَاتَيْنَاكُمْ We gave you biquwwatin بِقُوَّةٍ with firmness wa-is'maʿū وَاسْمَعُوا and listen qālū قَالُوا They said samiʿ'nā سَمِعْنَا We heard waʿaṣaynā وَعَصَيْنَا and we disobeyed wa-ush'ribū وَأُشْرِبُوا And they were made to drink fī فِي in qulūbihimu قُلُوبِهِمُ their hearts l-ʿij'la الْعِجْلَ (love of) the calf bikuf'rihim بِكُفْرِهِمْ because of their disbelief qul قُلْ Say bi'samā بِئْسَمَا Evil (is) that yamurukum يَأْمُرُكُمْ orders you (to do) it bihi بِهِ with īmānukum إِيمَانُكُمْ your faith in إِنْ if kuntum كُنْتُمْ you are mu'minīna مُؤْمِنِينَ believers

93

93.

And [recall] when We took your covenant and raised over you the mount, [saying], "Take what We have given you with determination and listen." They said [instead], "We hear and disobey." And their hearts absorbed [the worship of] the calf because of their disbelief. Say, "How wretched is that which your faith enjoins upon you, if you should be believers."

93

qul قُلْ Say in إِنْ If kānat كَانَتْ is lakumu لَكُمُ for you l-dāru الدَّارُ the home l-ākhiratu الْءَاخِرَةُ (of) the Hereafter ʿinda عِنْدَ with l-lahi اللَّهِ Allah khāliṣatan خَالِصَةً exclusively min مِنْ from dūni دُونِ excluding l-nāsi النَّاسِ the mankind fatamannawū فَتَمَنَّوُا then wish l-mawta الْمَوْتَ (for) [the] death in إِنْ if kuntum كُنْتُمْ you are ṣādiqīna صَادِقِينَ truthful

94

94.

Say, [O Muhammad], "If the home of the Hereafter with Allah is for you alone and not the [other] people, then wish for death, if you should be truthful.

94

walan وَلَنْ And never (will) yatamannawhu يَتَمَنَّوْهُ they wish for it abadan أَبَدًا ever bimā بِمَا because qaddamat قَدَّمَتْ (of what) sent ahead aydīhim أَيْدِيهِمْ their hands wal-lahu وَاللَّهُ And Allah ʿalīmun عَلِيمٌ (is) All-Knower bil-ẓālimīna بِالظَّالِمِينَ of the wrongdoers

95

95.

But they will never wish for it, ever, because of what their hands have put forth. And Allah is Knowing of the wrongdoers.

95

walatajidannahum وَلَتَجِدَنَّهُمْ And surely you will find them aḥraṣa أَحْرَصَ (the) most greedy l-nāsi النَّاسِ (of) [the] mankind ʿalā عَلَى for ḥayatin حَيَوةٍ life wamina وَمِنَ and (greedier) than alladhīna الَّذِينَ those who ashrakū أَشْرَكُوا associate[d] partners (with Allah) yawaddu يَوَدُّ Loves aḥaduhum أَحَدُهُمْ (each) one of them law لَوْ if yuʿammaru يُعَمَّرُ he could be granted a life alfa أَلْفَ (of) a thousand sanatin سَنَةٍ year(s) wamā وَمَا But not huwa هُوَ it bimuzaḥziḥihi بِمُزَحْزِحِهِ (will) remove him mina مِنَ from l-ʿadhābi الْعَذَابِ the punishment an أَنْ that yuʿammara يُعَمَّرَ he should be granted life wal-lahu وَاللَّهُ And Allah baṣīrun بَصِيرٌ (is) All-Seer bimā بِمَا of what yaʿmalūna يَعْمَلُونَ they do

96

96.

And you will surely find them the most greedy of people for life - [even] more than those who associate others with Allah. One of them wishes that he could be granted life a thousand years, but it would not remove him in the least from the [coming] punishment that he should be granted life. And Allah is Seeing of what they do.

96

qul قُلْ Say man مَنْ Whoever kāna كَانَ is ʿaduwwan عَدُوًّا an enemy lijib'rīla لِجِبْرِيلَ to Jibreel fa-innahu فَإِنَّهُ then indeed he nazzalahu نَزَّلَهُ brought it down ʿalā عَلَى on qalbika قَلْبِكَ your heart bi-idh'ni بِإِذْنِ by (the) permission l-lahi اللَّهِ (of) Allah muṣaddiqan مُصَدِّقًا confirming limā لِمَا what bayna بَيْنَ (was) yadayhi يَدَيْهِ before it wahudan وَهُدًى and a guidance wabush'rā وَبُشْرَى and glad tiding(s) lil'mu'minīna لِلْمُؤْمِنِينَ for the believers

97

97.

Say, "Whoever is an enemy to Gabriel - it is [none but] he who has brought the Qur'an down upon your heart, [O Muhammad], by permission of Allah, confirming that which was before it and as guidance and good tidings for the believers."

97

man مَنْ Whoever kāna كَانَ is ʿaduwwan عَدُوًّا an enemy lillahi لِلَّهِ (to) Allah wamalāikatihi وَمَلَائِكَتِهِ and His Angels warusulihi وَرُسُلِهِ and His Messengers wajib'rīla وَجِبْرِيلَ and Jibreel wamīkāla وَمِيكَالَ and Meekael fa-inna فَإِنَّ then indeed l-laha اللَّهَ Allah ʿaduwwun عَدُوٌّ (is) an enemy lil'kāfirīna لِلْكَافِرِينَ to the disbelievers

98

98.

Whoever is an enemy to Allah and His angels and His messengers and Gabriel and Michael - then indeed, Allah is an enemy to the disbelievers.

98

walaqad وَلَقَدْ And indeed anzalnā أَنْزَلْنَا We revealed ilayka إِلَيْكَ to you āyātin ءَايَاتٍ Verses bayyinātin بَيِّنَاتٍ clear wamā وَمَا and not yakfuru يَكْفُرُ disbelieves bihā بِهَا in them illā إِلَّا except l-fāsiqūna الْفَاسِقُونَ the defiantly disobedient

99

99.

And We have certainly revealed to you verses [which are] clear proofs, and no one would deny them except the defiantly disobedient.

99

awakullamā أَوَكُلَّمَا And is (it not that) whenever ʿāhadū عَاهَدُوا they took ʿahdan عَهْدًا a covenant nabadhahu نَبَذَهُ threw it away farīqun فَرِيقٌ a party min'hum مِنْهُمْ of them bal بَلْ Nay aktharuhum أَكْثَرُهُمْ most of them lā لَا (do) not yu'minūna يُؤْمِنُونَ believe

100

100.

Is it not [true] that every time they took a covenant a party of them threw it away? But, [in fact], most of them do not believe.

100

walammā وَلَمَّا And when jāahum جَاءَهُمْ came to them rasūlun رَسُولٌ a Messenger min مِنْ (of) ʿindi عِنْدِ from l-lahi اللَّهِ Allah muṣaddiqun مُصَدِّقٌ confirming limā لِمَا what maʿahum مَعَهُمْ (was) with them nabadha نَبَذَ threw away farīqun فَرِيقٌ a party mina مِنَ of alladhīna الَّذِينَ those who ūtū أُوتُوا were given l-kitāba الْكِتَابَ the Book kitāba كِتَابَ (the) Book l-lahi اللَّهِ (of) Allah warāa وَرَاءَ behind ẓuhūrihim ظُهُورِهِمْ their backs ka-annahum كَأَنَّهُمْ as if they lā لَا (do) not yaʿlamūna يَعْلَمُونَ know

101

101.

And when a messenger from Allah came to them confirming that which was with them, a party of those who had been given the Scripture threw the Scripture of Allah behind their backs as if they did not know [what it contained].

101

wa-ittabaʿū وَاتَّبَعُوا And they followed mā مَا what tatlū تَتْلُوا recite(d) l-shayāṭīnu الشَّيَاطِينُ the devils ʿalā عَلَى over mul'ki مُلْكِ (the) kingdom sulaymāna سُلَيْمَانَ (of) Sulaiman wamā وَمَا And not kafara كَفَرَ disbelieved sulaymānu سُلَيْمَانُ Sulaiman walākinna وَلَكِنَّ [and] but l-shayāṭīna الشَّيَاطِينَ the devils kafarū كَفَرُوا disbelieved yuʿallimūna يُعَلِّمُونَ they teach l-nāsa النَّاسَ the people l-siḥ'ra السِّحْرَ [the] magic wamā وَمَا and what unzila أُنْزِلَ was sent down ʿalā عَلَى to l-malakayni الْمَلَكَيْنِ the two angels bibābila بِبَابِلَ in Babylon hārūta هَارُوتَ Harut wamārūta وَمَارُوتَ and Marut wamā وَمَا And not yuʿallimāni يُعَلِّمَانِ they both teach min مِنْ any aḥadin أَحَدٍ one ḥattā حَتَّى unless yaqūlā يَقُولَا they [both] say innamā إِنَّمَا Only naḥnu نَحْنُ we fit'natun فِتْنَةٌ (are) a trial falā فَلَا so (do) not takfur تَكْفُرْ disbelieve fayataʿallamūna فَيَتَعَلَّمُونَ But they learn min'humā مِنْهُمَا from those two mā مَا what yufarriqūna يُفَرِّقُونَ [they] causes separation bihi بِهِ with it bayna بَيْنَ between l-mari الْمَرْءِ the man wazawjihi وَزَوْجِهِ and his spouse wamā وَمَا And not hum هُمْ they (could) biḍārrīna بِضَارِّينَ at all [be those who] harm bihi بِهِ with it min مِنْ any aḥadin أَحَدٍ one illā إِلَّا except bi-idh'ni بِإِذْنِ by permission l-lahi اللَّهِ (of) Allah wayataʿallamūna وَيَتَعَلَّمُونَ And they learn mā مَا what yaḍurruhum يَضُرُّهُمْ harms them walā وَلَا and not yanfaʿuhum يَنْفَعُهُمْ profits them walaqad وَلَقَدْ And indeed ʿalimū عَلِمُوا they knew lamani لَمَنِ that whoever ish'tarāhu اشْتَرَاهُ buys it mā مَا not lahu لَهُ for him fī فِي in l-ākhirati الْءَاخِرَةِ the Hereafter min مِنْ any khalāqin خَلَاقٍ share walabi'sa وَلَبِئْسَ And surely evil mā مَا (is) what sharaw شَرَوْا they sold bihi بِهِ with it anfusahum أَنْفُسَهُمْ themselves law لَوْ if kānū كَانُوا they were yaʿlamūna يَعْلَمُونَ (to) know

102

102.

And they followed [instead] what the devils had recited during the reign of Solomon. It was not Solomon who disbelieved, but the devils disbelieved, teaching people magic and that which was revealed to the two angels at Babylon, Harut and Marut. But the two angels do not teach anyone unless they say, "We are a trial, so do not disbelieve [by practicing magic]." And [yet] they learn from them that by which they cause separation between a man and his wife. But they do not harm anyone through it except by permission of Allah. And the people learn what harms them and does not benefit them. But the Children of Israel certainly knew that whoever purchased the magic would not have in the Hereafter any share. And wretched is that for which they sold themselves, if they only knew.

102

walaw وَلَوْ And if annahum أَنَّهُمْ [that] they āmanū ءَامَنُوا (had) believed wa-ittaqaw وَاتَّقَوْا and feared (Allah) lamathūbatun لَمَثُوبَةٌ surely (the) reward min مِنْ (of) ʿindi عِنْدِ from l-lahi اللَّهِ Allah khayrun خَيْرٌ (would have been) better law لَوْ if kānū كَانُوا they were yaʿlamūna يَعْلَمُونَ (to) know

103

103.

And if they had believed and feared Allah, then the reward from Allah would have been [far] better, if they only knew.

103

yāayyuhā يَاأَيُّهَا O you alladhīna الَّذِينَ who āmanū ءَامَنُوا believe[d]! lā لَا (Do) not taqūlū تَقُولُوا say rāʿinā رَاعِنَا Raina waqūlū وَقُولُوا and say unẓur'nā انْظُرْنَا Unzurna wa-is'maʿū وَاسْمَعُوا and listen walil'kāfirīna وَلِلْكَافِرِينَ And for the disbelievers ʿadhābun عَذَابٌ (is) a punishment alīmun أَلِيمٌ painful

104

104.

O you who have believed, say not [to Allah 's Messenger], "Ra'ina" but say, "Unthurna" and listen. And for the disbelievers is a painful punishment.

104

mā مَا (Do) not yawaddu يَوَدُّ like alladhīna الَّذِينَ those who kafarū كَفَرُوا disbelieve min مِنْ from ahli أَهْلِ (the) People l-kitābi الْكِتَابِ (of) the Book walā وَلَا and not l-mush'rikīna الْمُشْرِكِينَ those who associate partners (with Allah) an أَنْ that yunazzala يُنَزَّلَ (there should) be sent down ʿalaykum عَلَيْكُمْ to you min مِنْ any khayrin خَيْرٍ good min مِنْ from rabbikum رَبِّكُمْ your Lord wal-lahu وَاللَّهُ And Allah yakhtaṣṣu يَخْتَصُّ chooses biraḥmatihi بِرَحْمَتِهِ for His Mercy man مَنْ whom yashāu يَشَاءُ He wills wal-lahu وَاللَّهُ And Allah dhū ذُو (is the) Possessor l-faḍli الْفَضْلِ (of) [the] Bounty l-ʿaẓīmi الْعَظِيمِ [the] Great

105

105.

Neither those who disbelieve from the People of the Scripture nor the polytheists wish that any good should be sent down to you from your Lord. But Allah selects for His mercy whom He wills, and Allah is the possessor of great bounty.

105

mā مَا What nansakh نَنْسَخْ We abrogate min مِنْ (of) āyatin ءَايَةٍ a sign aw أَوْ or nunsihā نُنْسِهَا [We] cause it to be forgotten nati نَأْتِ We bring bikhayrin بِخَيْرٍ better min'hā مِنْهَا than it aw أَوْ or mith'lihā مِثْلِهَا similar (to) it alam أَلَمْ Do not taʿlam تَعْلَمْ you know anna أَنَّ that l-laha اللَّهَ Allah ʿalā عَلَى over kulli كُلِّ every shayin شَيْءٍ thing qadīrun قَدِيرٌ (is) All-Powerful

106

106.

We do not abrogate a verse or cause it to be forgotten except that We bring forth [one] better than it or similar to it. Do you not know that Allah is over all things competent?

106

alam أَلَمْ Do not taʿlam تَعْلَمْ you know anna أَنَّ that l-laha اللَّهَ Allah lahu لَهُ for Him mul'ku مُلْكُ (is the) Kingdom l-samāwāti السَّمَاوَاتِ (of) the heavens wal-arḍi وَالْأَرْضِ and the earth wamā وَمَا And not lakum لَكُمْ (is) for you min مِنْ from dūni دُونِ besides l-lahi اللَّهِ Allah min مِنْ any waliyyin وَلِيٍّ protector walā وَلَا and not naṣīrin نَصِيرٍ any helper

107

107.

Do you not know that to Allah belongs the dominion of the heavens and the earth and [that] you have not besides Allah any protector or any helper?

107

am أَمْ Or turīdūna تُرِيدُونَ (do) you wish an أَنْ that tasalū تَسْءَلُوا you ask rasūlakum رَسُولَكُمْ your Messenger kamā كَمَا as su-ila سُئِلَ was asked mūsā مُوسَى Musa min مِنْ from qablu قَبْلُ before waman وَمَنْ And whoever yatabaddali يَتَبَدَّلِ exchanges l-kuf'ra الْكُفْرَ [the] disbelief bil-īmāni بِالْإِيمَانِ with [the] faith faqad فَقَدْ so certainly ḍalla ضَلَّ he went astray (from) sawāa سَوَاءَ (the) evenness l-sabīli السَّبِيلِ (of) the way

108

108.

Or do you intend to ask your Messenger as Moses was asked before? And whoever exchanges faith for disbelief has certainly strayed from the soundness of the way.

108

wadda وَدَّ Wish[ed] kathīrun كَثِيرٌ many min مِنْ from ahli أَهْلِ (the) People l-kitābi الْكِتَابِ (of) the Book law لَوْ if yaruddūnakum يَرُدُّونَكُمْ they could turn you back min مِنْ from baʿdi بَعْدِ after īmānikum إِيمَانِكُمْ your (having) faith kuffāran كُفَّارًا (to) disbelievers ḥasadan حَسَدًا (out of) jealousy min مِنْ from ʿindi عِنْدِ (of) anfusihim أَنْفُسِهِمْ themselves min مِنْ (even) from baʿdi بَعْدِ after mā مَا [what] tabayyana تَبَيَّنَ became clear lahumu لَهُمُ to them l-ḥaqu الْحَقُّ the truth fa-iʿ'fū فَاعْفُوا So forgive wa-iṣ'faḥū وَاصْفَحُوا and overlook ḥattā حَتَّى until yatiya يَأْتِيَ brings l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah bi-amrihi بِأَمْرِهِ His Command inna إِنَّ Indeed l-laha اللَّهَ Allah ʿalā عَلَى on kulli كُلِّ every shayin شَيْءٍ thing qadīrun قَدِيرٌ (is) All-Powerful

109

109.

Many of the People of the Scripture wish they could turn you back to disbelief after you have believed, out of envy from themselves [even] after the truth has become clear to them. So pardon and overlook until Allah delivers His command. Indeed, Allah is over all things competent.

109

wa-aqīmū وَأَقِيمُوا And establish l-ṣalata الصَّلَوةَ the prayer waātū وَءَاتُوا and give l-zakata الزَّكَوةَ [the] zakah wamā وَمَا And whatever tuqaddimū تُقَدِّمُوا you send forth li-anfusikum لِأَنْفُسِكُمْ for yourselves min مِنْ of khayrin خَيْرٍ good (deeds) tajidūhu تَجِدُوهُ you will find it ʿinda عِنْدَ with l-lahi اللَّهِ Allah inna إِنَّ Indeed l-laha اللَّهَ Allah bimā بِمَا of what taʿmalūna تَعْمَلُونَ you do baṣīrun بَصِيرٌ (is) All-Seer

110

110.

And establish prayer and give zakah, and whatever good you put forward for yourselves - you will find it with Allah. Indeed, Allah of what you do, is Seeing.

110

waqālū وَقَالُوا And they said lan لَنْ Never yadkhula يَدْخُلَ will enter l-janata الْجَنَّةَ the Paradise illā إِلَّا except man مَنْ who kāna كَانَ is hūdan هُودًا (a) Jew[s] aw أَوْ or naṣārā نَصَارَى (a) Christian[s] til'ka تِلْكَ That amāniyyuhum أَمَانِيُّهُمْ (is) their wishful thinking qul قُلْ Say hātū هَاتُوا Bring bur'hānakum بُرْهَانَكُمْ your proof in إِنْ if kuntum كُنْتُمْ you are ṣādiqīna صَادِقِينَ [those who are] truthful

111

111.

And they say, "None will enter Paradise except one who is a Jew or a Christian." That is [merely] their wishful thinking, Say, "Produce your proof, if you should be truthful."

111

balā بَلَى Yes man مَنْ whoever aslama أَسْلَمَ submits wajhahu وَجْهَهُ his face lillahi لِلَّهِ to Allah wahuwa وَهُوَ and he muḥ'sinun مُحْسِنٌ (is) a good-doer falahu فَلَهُ so for him ajruhu أَجْرُهُ (is) his reward ʿinda عِنْدَ with rabbihi رَبِّهِ his Lord walā وَلَا And no khawfun خَوْفٌ fear ʿalayhim عَلَيْهِمْ (will be) on them walā وَلَا and not hum هُمْ they yaḥzanūna يَحْزَنُونَ (will) grieve

112

112.

Yes [on the contrary], whoever submits his face in Islam to Allah while being a doer of good will have his reward with his Lord. And no fear will there be concerning them, nor will they grieve.

112

waqālati وَقَالَتِ And said l-yahūdu الْيَهُودُ the Jews laysati لَيْسَتِ Not l-naṣārā النَّصَارَى the Christians ʿalā عَلَى (are) on shayin شَيْءٍ anything waqālati وَقَالَتِ and said l-naṣārā النَّصَارَى the Christians laysati لَيْسَتِ Not l-yahūdu الْيَهُودُ the Jews ʿalā عَلَى (are) on shayin شَيْءٍ anything wahum وَهُمْ although they yatlūna يَتْلُونَ recite l-kitāba الْكِتَابَ the Book kadhālika كَذَلِكَ Like that qāla قَالَ said alladhīna الَّذِينَ those who lā لَا (do) not yaʿlamūna يَعْلَمُونَ know mith'la مِثْلَ similar qawlihim قَوْلِهِمْ their saying fal-lahu فَاللَّهُ [So] Allah yaḥkumu يَحْكُمُ will judge baynahum بَيْنَهُمْ between them yawma يَوْمَ (on the) Day l-qiyāmati الْقِيَامَةِ (of) Resurrection fīmā فِيمَا in what kānū كَانُوا they were fīhi فِيهِ [in it] yakhtalifūna يَخْتَلِفُونَ differing

113

113.

The Jews say "The Christians have nothing [true] to stand on," and the Christians say, "The Jews have nothing to stand on," although they [both] recite the Scripture. Thus the polytheists speak the same as their words. But Allah will judge between them on the Day of Resurrection concerning that over which they used to differ.

113

waman وَمَنْ And who aẓlamu أَظْلَمُ (is) more unjust mimman مِمَّنْ than (one) who manaʿa مَنَعَ prevents masājida مَسَاجِدَ (the) masajid l-lahi اللَّهِ (of) Allah an أَنْ to yudh'kara يُذْكَرَ be mentioned fīhā فِيهَا in them us'muhu اسْمُهُ His name wasaʿā وَسَعَى and strives fī فِي for kharābihā خَرَابِهَا their destruction ulāika أُولَئِكَ Those! mā مَا Not kāna كَانَ it is lahum لَهُمْ for them an أَنْ that yadkhulūhā يَدْخُلُوهَا they enter them illā إِلَّا except khāifīna خَائِفِينَ (like) those in fear lahum لَهُمْ For them fī فِي in l-dun'yā الدُّنْيَا the world khiz'yun خِزْيٌ (is) disgrace walahum وَلَهُمْ and for them fī فِي in l-ākhirati الْءَاخِرَةِ the Hereafter ʿadhābun عَذَابٌ (is) a punishment ʿaẓīmun عَظِيمٌ great

114

114.

And who are more unjust than those who prevent the name of Allah from being mentioned in His mosques and strive toward their destruction. It is not for them to enter them except in fear. For them in this world is disgrace, and they will have in the Hereafter a great punishment.

114

walillahi وَلِلَّهِ And for Allah l-mashriqu الْمَشْرِقُ (is) the east wal-maghribu وَالْمَغْرِبُ and the west fa-aynamā فَأَيْنَمَا so wherever tuwallū تُوَلُّوا you turn fathamma فَثَمَّ [so] there wajhu وَجْهُ (is the) face l-lahi اللَّهِ (of) Allah inna إِنَّ Indeed l-laha اللَّهَ Allah wāsiʿun وَاسِعٌ (is) All-Encompassing ʿalīmun عَلِيمٌ All-Knowing

115

115.

And to Allah belongs the east and the west. So wherever you [might] turn, there is the Face of Allah. Indeed, Allah is all-Encompassing and Knowing.

115

waqālū وَقَالُوا And they said ittakhadha اتَّخَذَ has taken l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah waladan وَلَدًا a son sub'ḥānahu سُبْحَانَهُ Glory be to Him bal بَلْ Nay lahu لَهُ for Him mā مَا (is) what fī فِي (is) in l-samāwāti السَّمَاوَاتِ the heavens wal-arḍi وَالْأَرْضِ and the earth kullun كُلٌّ All lahu لَهُ to Him qānitūna قَانِتُونَ (are) humbly obedient

116

116.

They say, "Allah has taken a son." Exalted is He! Rather, to Him belongs whatever is in the heavens and the earth. All are devoutly obedient to Him,

116
