badīʿu بَدِيعُ (The) Originator l-samāwāti السَّمَاوَاتِ (of) the heavens wal-arḍi وَالْأَرْضِ and the earth! wa-idhā وَإِذَا And when qaḍā قَضَى He decrees amran أَمْرًا a matter fa-innamā فَإِنَّمَا [so] only yaqūlu يَقُولُ He says lahu لَهُ to it kun كُنْ Be fayakūnu فَيَكُونُ and it becomes

117

117.

Originator of the heavens and the earth. When He decrees a matter, He only says to it, "Be," and it is.

117

waqāla وَقَالَ And said alladhīna الَّذِينَ those who lā لَا (do) not yaʿlamūna يَعْلَمُونَ know lawlā لَوْلَا Why not yukallimunā يُكَلِّمُنَا speaks to us l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah aw أَوْ or tatīnā تَأْتِينَا comes to us āyatun ءَايَةٌ a sign kadhālika كَذَلِكَ Like that qāla قَالَ said alladhīna الَّذِينَ those min مِنْ from qablihim قَبْلِهِمْ before them mith'la مِثْلَ similar qawlihim قَوْلِهِمْ their saying tashābahat تَشَابَهَتْ Became alike qulūbuhum قُلُوبُهُمْ their hearts qad قَدْ Indeed bayyannā بَيَّنَّا We have made clear l-āyāti الْءَايَاتِ the signs liqawmin لِقَوْمٍ for people yūqinūna يُوقِنُونَ (who) firmly believe

118

118.

Those who do not know say, "Why does Allah not speak to us or there come to us a sign?" Thus spoke those before them like their words. Their hearts resemble each other. We have shown clearly the signs to a people who are certain [in faith].

118

innā إِنَّا Indeed We! arsalnāka أَرْسَلْنَاكَ [We] have sent you bil-ḥaqi بِالْحَقِّ with the truth bashīran بَشِيرًا (as) a bearer of good news wanadhīran وَنَذِيرًا and (as) a warner walā وَلَا And not tus'alu تُسْءَلُ you will be asked ʿan عَنْ about aṣḥābi أَصْحَابِ (the) companions l-jaḥīmi الْجَحِيمِ (of) the blazing Fire

119

119.

Indeed, We have sent you, [O Muhammad], with the truth as a bringer of good tidings and a warner, and you will not be asked about the companions of Hellfire.

119

walan وَلَنْ And never tarḍā تَرْضَى will be pleased ʿanka عَنْكَ with you l-yahūdu الْيَهُودُ the Jews walā وَلَا and [not] l-naṣārā النَّصَارَى the Christians ḥattā حَتَّى until tattabiʿa تَتَّبِعَ you follow millatahum مِلَّتَهُمْ their religion qul قُلْ Say inna إِنَّ Indeed hudā هُدَى (the) Guidance l-lahi اللَّهِ (of) Allah huwa هُوَ it l-hudā الْهُدَى (is) the Guidance wala-ini وَلَئِنِ And if ittabaʿta اتَّبَعْتَ you follow ahwāahum أَهْوَاءَهُمْ their desires baʿda بَعْدَ after alladhī الَّذِي what jāaka جَاءَكَ has come to you mina مِنَ of l-ʿil'mi الْعِلْمِ the knowledge mā مَا not laka لَكَ for you mina مِنَ from l-lahi اللَّهِ Allah min مِنْ any waliyyin وَلِيٍّ protector walā وَلَا and not naṣīrin نَصِيرٍ any helper

120

120.

And never will the Jews or the Christians approve of you until you follow their religion. Say, "Indeed, the guidance of Allah is the [only] guidance." If you were to follow their desires after what has come to you of knowledge, you would have against Allah no protector or helper.

120

alladhīna الَّذِينَ Those ātaynāhumu ءَاتَيْنَاهُمُ We have given them l-kitāba الْكِتَابَ the Book yatlūnahu يَتْلُونَهُ recite it ḥaqqa حَقَّ (as it has the) right tilāwatihi تِلَاوَتِهِ (of) its recitation ulāika أُولَئِكَ Those (people) yu'minūna يُؤْمِنُونَ believe bihi بِهِ in it waman وَمَنْ And whoever yakfur يَكْفُرْ disbelieves bihi بِهِ in it fa-ulāika فَأُولَئِكَ then those humu هُمُ they l-khāsirūna الْخَاسِرُونَ (are) the losers

121

121.

Those to whom We have given the Book recite it with its true recital. They [are the ones who] believe in it. And whoever disbelieves in it - it is they who are the losers.

121

yābanī يَابَنِي O Children is'rāīla إِسْرَاءِيلَ (of) Israel! udh'kurū اذْكُرُوا Remember niʿ'matiya نِعْمَتِيَ My Favor allatī الَّتِي which anʿamtu أَنْعَمْتُ I bestowed ʿalaykum عَلَيْكُمْ upon you wa-annī وَأَنِّي and that I faḍḍaltukum فَضَّلْتُكُمْ [I] preferred you ʿalā عَلَى over l-ʿālamīna الْعَالَمِينَ the worlds

122

122.

O Children of Israel, remember My favor which I have bestowed upon you and that I preferred you over the worlds.

122

wa-ittaqū وَاتَّقُوا And fear yawman يَوْمًا a day lā لَا not tajzī تَجْزِي will avail nafsun نَفْسٌ a soul ʿan عَنْ (of) nafsin نَفْسٍ (another) soul shayan شَيْئًا anything walā وَلَا and not yuq'balu يُقْبَلُ will be accepted min'hā مِنْهَا from it ʿadlun عَدْلٌ any compensation walā وَلَا and not tanfaʿuhā تَنْفَعُهَا will benefit it shafāʿatun شَفَاعَةٌ any intercession walā وَلَا and not hum هُمْ they yunṣarūna يُنْصَرُونَ will be helped

123

123.

And fear a Day when no soul will suffice for another soul at all, and no compensation will be accepted from it, nor will any intercession benefit it, nor will they be aided.

123

wa-idhi وَإِذِ And when ib'talā ابْتَلَى tried ib'rāhīma إِبْرَاهِيمَ Ibrahim rabbuhu رَبُّهُ his Lord bikalimātin بِكَلِمَاتٍ with words fa-atammahunna فَأَتَمَّهُنَّ and he fulfilled them qāla قَالَ He said innī إِنِّي Indeed I jāʿiluka جَاعِلُكَ (am) the One to make you lilnnāsi لِلنَّاسِ for the mankind imāman إِمَامًا a leader qāla قَالَ He said wamin وَمِنْ And from dhurriyyatī ذُرِّيَّتِي my offspring qāla قَالَ He said lā لَا (Does) not yanālu يَنَالُ reach ʿahdī عَهْدِي My Covenant l-ẓālimīna الظَّالِمِينَ (to) the wrongdoers

124

124.

And [mention, O Muhammad], when Abraham was tried by his Lord with commands and he fulfilled them. [Allah] said, "Indeed, I will make you a leader for the people." [Abraham] said, "And of my descendants?" [Allah] said, "My covenant does not include the wrongdoers."

124

wa-idh وَإِذْ And when jaʿalnā جَعَلْنَا We made l-bayta الْبَيْتَ the House mathābatan مَثَابَةً a place of return lilnnāsi لِلنَّاسِ for mankind wa-amnan وَأَمْنًا and (a place of) security wa-ittakhidhū وَاتَّخِذُوا and (said) Take min مِنْ [from] maqāmi مَقَامِ (the) standing place ib'rāhīma إِبْرَاهِيمَ (of) Ibrahim muṣallan مُصَلًّى (as) a place of prayer waʿahid'nā وَعَهِدْنَا And We made a covenant ilā إِلَى with ib'rāhīma إِبْرَاهِيمَ Ibrahim wa-is'māʿīla وَإِسْمَاعِيلَ and Ismail an أَنْ [that] ṭahhirā طَهِّرَا [You both] purify baytiya بَيْتِيَ My House lilṭṭāifīna لِلطَّائِفِينَ for those who circumambulate wal-ʿākifīna وَالْعَاكِفِينَ and those who seclude themselves for devotion and prayer wal-rukaʿi وَالرُّكَّعِ and those who bow down l-sujūdi السُّجُودِ and those who prostrate

125

125.

And [mention] when We made the House a place of return for the people and [a place of] security. And take, [O believers], from the standing place of Abraham a place of prayer. And We charged Abraham and Ishmael, [saying], "Purify My House for those who perform Tawaf and those who are staying [there] for worship and those who bow and prostrate [in prayer]."

125

wa-idh وَإِذْ And when qāla قَالَ said ib'rāhīmu إِبْرَاهِيمُ Ibrahim rabbi رَبِّ My Lord ij'ʿal اجْعَلْ make hādhā هَذَا this baladan بَلَدًا a city āminan ءَامِنًا secure wa-ur'zuq وَارْزُقْ and provide ahlahu أَهْلَهُ its people mina مِنَ with l-thamarāti الثَّمَرَاتِ fruits man مَنْ (to) whoever āmana ءَامَنَ believed min'hum مِنْهُمْ from them bil-lahi بِاللَّهِ in Allah wal-yawmi وَالْيَوْمِ and the Day l-ākhiri الْءَاخِرِ the Last qāla قَالَ He said waman وَمَنْ And whoever kafara كَفَرَ disbelieved fa-umattiʿuhu فَأُمَتِّعُهُ [then] I will grant him enjoyment qalīlan قَلِيلًا a little thumma ثُمَّ then aḍṭarruhu أَضْطَرُّهُ I will force him ilā إِلَى to ʿadhābi عَذَابِ (the) punishment l-nāri النَّارِ (of) the Fire wabi'sa وَبِئْسَ and evil l-maṣīru الْمَصِيرُ (is) the destination

126

126.

And [mention] when Abraham said, "My Lord, make this a secure city and provide its people with fruits - whoever of them believes in Allah and the Last Day." [Allah] said. "And whoever disbelieves - I will grant him enjoyment for a little; then I will force him to the punishment of the Fire, and wretched is the destination."

126

wa-idh وَإِذْ And when yarfaʿu يَرْفَعُ (was) raising ib'rāhīmu إِبْرَاهِيمُ Ibrahim l-qawāʿida الْقَوَاعِدَ the foundations mina مِنَ of l-bayti الْبَيْتِ the House wa-is'māʿīlu وَإِسْمَاعِيلُ and Ishmael rabbanā رَبَّنَا (saying), "Our Lord taqabbal تَقَبَّلْ Accept minnā مِنَّا from us innaka إِنَّكَ Indeed You anta أَنْتَ [You] (are) l-samīʿu السَّمِيعُ the All-Hearing l-ʿalīmu الْعَلِيمُ the All-Knowing

127

127.

And [mention] when Abraham was raising the foundations of the House and [with him] Ishmael, [saying], "Our Lord, accept [this] from us. Indeed You are the Hearing, the Knowing.

127

rabbanā رَبَّنَا Our Lord! wa-ij'ʿalnā وَاجْعَلْنَا [and] Make us mus'limayni مُسْلِمَيْنِ both submissive laka لَكَ to You wamin وَمِنْ And from dhurriyyatinā ذُرِّيَّتِنَا our offspring ummatan أُمَّةً a community mus'limatan مُسْلِمَةً submissive laka لَكَ to You wa-arinā وَأَرِنَا And show us manāsikanā مَنَاسِكَنَا our ways of worship watub وَتُبْ and turn ʿalaynā عَلَيْنَا to us innaka إِنَّكَ Indeed You! anta أَنْتَ [You] (are) l-tawābu التَّوَّابُ the Oft-returning l-raḥīmu الرَّحِيمُ the Most Merciful

128

128.

Our Lord, and make us Muslims [in submission] to You and from our descendants a Muslim nation [in submission] to You. And show us our rites and accept our repentance. Indeed, You are the Accepting of repentance, the Merciful.

128

rabbanā رَبَّنَا Our Lord! wa-ib'ʿath وَابْعَثْ [And] raise up fīhim فِيهِمْ in them rasūlan رَسُولًا a Messenger min'hum مِنْهُمْ from them yatlū يَتْلُوا (who) will recite ʿalayhim عَلَيْهِمْ to them āyātika ءَايَاتِكَ Your Verses wayuʿallimuhumu وَيُعَلِّمُهُمُ and will teach them l-kitāba الْكِتَابَ the Book wal-ḥik'mata وَالْحِكْمَةَ and the wisdom wayuzakkīhim وَيُزَكِّيهِمْ and purify them innaka إِنَّكَ Indeed You! anta أَنْتَ You (are) l-ʿazīzu الْعَزِيزُ the All-Mighty l-ḥakīmu الْحَكِيمُ the All-Wise

129

129.

Our Lord, and send among them a messenger from themselves who will recite to them Your verses and teach them the Book and wisdom and purify them. Indeed, You are the Exalted in Might, the Wise."

129

waman وَمَنْ And who yarghabu يَرْغَبُ will turn away ʿan عَنْ from millati مِلَّةِ (the) religion ib'rāhīma إِبْرَاهِيمَ (of) Ibrahim illā إِلَّا except man مَنْ who safiha سَفِهَ fooled nafsahu نَفْسَهُ himself walaqadi وَلَقَدِ And indeed iṣ'ṭafaynāhu اصْطَفَيْنَاهُ We chose him fī فِي in l-dun'yā الدُّنْيَا the world wa-innahu وَإِنَّهُ and indeed he fī فِي in l-ākhirati الْءَاخِرَةِ the Hereafter lamina لَمِنَ surely (will be) among l-ṣāliḥīna الصَّالِحِينَ the righteous

130

130.

And who would be averse to the religion of Abraham except one who makes a fool of himself. And We had chosen him in this world, and indeed he, in the Hereafter, will be among the righteous.

130

idh إِذْ When qāla قَالَ said lahu لَهُ to him rabbuhu رَبُّهُ his Lord aslim أَسْلِمْ Submit (yourself) qāla قَالَ he said aslamtu أَسْلَمْتُ I (have) submitted (myself) lirabbi لِرَبِّ to (the) Lord l-ʿālamīna الْعَالَمِينَ (of) the worlds

131

131.

When his Lord said to him, "Submit", he said "I have submitted [in Islam] to the Lord of the worlds."

131

wawaṣṣā وَوَصَّى And enjoined bihā بِهَا [it] ib'rāhīmu إِبْرَاهِيمُ Ibrahim banīhi بَنِيهِ (upon) his sons wayaʿqūbu وَيَعْقُوبُ and Yaqub yābaniyya يَابَنِيَّ O my sons inna إِنَّ Indeed l-laha اللَّهَ Allah iṣ'ṭafā اصْطَفَى has chosen lakumu لَكُمُ for you l-dīna الدِّينَ the religion falā فَلَا so not tamūtunna تَمُوتُنَّ (should) you die illā إِلَّا except wa-antum وَأَنْتُمْ while you mus'limūna مُسْلِمُونَ (are) submissive

132

132.

And Abraham instructed his sons [to do the same] and [so did] Jacob, [saying], "O my sons, indeed Allah has chosen for you this religion, so do not die except while you are Muslims."

132

am أَمْ Or kuntum كُنْتُمْ were you shuhadāa شُهَدَاءَ witnesses idh إِذْ when ḥaḍara حَضَرَ came to yaʿqūba يَعْقُوبَ Yaqub l-mawtu الْمَوْتُ [the] death idh إِذْ when qāla قَالَ he said libanīhi لِبَنِيهِ to his sons mā مَا What taʿbudūna تَعْبُدُونَ will you worship min مِنْ from baʿdī بَعْدِي after me qālū قَالُوا They said naʿbudu نَعْبُدُ We will worship ilāhaka إِلَهَكَ your God wa-ilāha وَإِلَهَ and (the) God ābāika ءَابَائِكَ (of) your forefathers ib'rāhīma إِبْرَاهِيمَ Ibrahim wa-is'māʿīla وَإِسْمَاعِيلَ and Ismail wa-is'ḥāqa وَإِسْحَاقَ and Ishaq ilāhan إِلَهًا God wāḥidan وَاحِدًا One wanaḥnu وَنَحْنُ And we lahu لَهُ to Him mus'limūna مُسْلِمُونَ (are) submissive

133

133.

Or were you witnesses when death approached Jacob, when he said to his sons, "What will you worship after me?" They said, "We will worship your God and the God of your fathers, Abraham and Ishmael and Isaac - one God. And we are Muslims [in submission] to Him."

133

til'ka تِلْكَ This ummatun أُمَّةٌ (was) a community qad قَدْ (which) khalat خَلَتْ has passed away lahā لَهَا for it mā مَا what kasabat كَسَبَتْ it earned walakum وَلَكُمْ and for you mā مَا what kasabtum كَسَبْتُمْ you earned walā وَلَا And not tus'alūna تُسْءَلُونَ you will be asked ʿammā عَمَّا about what kānū كَانُوا they used to yaʿmalūna يَعْمَلُونَ do

134

134.

That was a nation which has passed on. It will have [the consequence of] what it earned, and you will have what you have earned. And you will not be asked about what they used to do.

134

waqālū وَقَالُوا And they said kūnū كُونُوا Be hūdan هُودًا Jews aw أَوْ or naṣārā نَصَارَى Christians tahtadū تَهْتَدُوا (then) you will be guided qul قُلْ Say bal بَلْ Nay millata مِلَّةَ (the) religion ib'rāhīma إِبْرَاهِيمَ (of) Ibrahim ḥanīfan حَنِيفًا (the) upright wamā وَمَا and not kāna كَانَ he was mina مِنَ of l-mush'rikīna الْمُشْرِكِينَ those who associated partners (with Allah)

135

135.

They say, "Be Jews or Christians [so] you will be guided." Say, "Rather, [we follow] the religion of Abraham, inclining toward truth, and he was not of the polytheists."

135

qūlū قُولُوا Say āmannā ءَامَنَّا We have believed bil-lahi بِاللَّهِ in Allah wamā وَمَا and what unzila أُنْزِلَ (is) revealed ilaynā إِلَيْنَا to us wamā وَمَا and what unzila أُنْزِلَ was revealed ilā إِلَى to ib'rāhīma إِبْرَاهِيمَ Ibrahim wa-is'māʿīla وَإِسْمَاعِيلَ and Ismail wa-is'ḥāqa وَإِسْحَاقَ and Ishaq wayaʿqūba وَيَعْقُوبَ and Yaqub wal-asbāṭi وَالْأَسْبَاطِ and the descendants wamā وَمَا and what ūtiya أُوتِيَ was given mūsā مُوسَى (to) Musa waʿīsā وَعِيسَى and Isa wamā وَمَا and what ūtiya أُوتِيَ was given l-nabiyūna النَّبِيُّونَ (to) the Prophets min مِنْ from rabbihim رَبِّهِمْ their Lord lā لَا Not nufarriqu نُفَرِّقُ we make distinction bayna بَيْنَ between aḥadin أَحَدٍ any min'hum مِنْهُمْ of them wanaḥnu وَنَحْنُ And we lahu لَهُ to Him mus'limūna مُسْلِمُونَ (are) submissive

136

136.

Say, [O believers], "We have believed in Allah and what has been revealed to us and what has been revealed to Abraham and Ishmael and Isaac and Jacob and the Descendants and what was given to Moses and Jesus and what was given to the prophets from their Lord. We make no distinction between any of them, and we are Muslims [in submission] to Him."

136

fa-in فَإِنْ So if āmanū ءَامَنُوا they believe[d] bimith'li بِمِثْلِ in (the) like mā مَا (of) what āmantum ءَامَنْتُمْ you have believed bihi بِهِ in [it] faqadi فَقَدِ then indeed ih'tadaw اهْتَدَوْا they are (rightly) guided wa-in وَإِنْ But if tawallaw تَوَلَّوْا they turn away fa-innamā فَإِنَّمَا then only hum هُمْ they fī فِي (are) in shiqāqin شِقَاقٍ dissension fasayakfīkahumu فَسَيَكْفِيكَهُمُ So will suffice you against them l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah wahuwa وَهُوَ and He l-samīʿu السَّمِيعُ (is) the All-Hearing l-ʿalīmu الْعَلِيمُ the All-Knowing

137

137.

So if they believe in the same as you believe in, then they have been [rightly] guided; but if they turn away, they are only in dissension, and Allah will be sufficient for you against them. And He is the Hearing, the Knowing.

137

ṣib'ghata صِبْغَةَ (The) color (religion) l-lahi اللَّهِ (of) Allah waman وَمَنْ And who aḥsanu أَحْسَنُ (is) better mina مِنَ than l-lahi اللَّهِ Allah ṣib'ghatan صِبْغَةً at coloring wanaḥnu وَنَحْنُ And we lahu لَهُ to Him ʿābidūna عَابِدُونَ (are) worshippers

138

138.

[And say, "Ours is] the religion of Allah. And who is better than Allah in [ordaining] religion? And we are worshippers of Him."

138

qul قُلْ Say atuḥājjūnanā أَتُحَاجُّونَنَا Do you argue with us fī فِي about l-lahi اللَّهِ Allah wahuwa وَهُوَ while He rabbunā رَبُّنَا (is) our Lord warabbukum وَرَبُّكُمْ and your Lord walanā وَلَنَا And for us aʿmālunā أَعْمَالُنَا (are) our deeds walakum وَلَكُمْ and for you aʿmālukum أَعْمَالُكُمْ (are) your deeds wanaḥnu وَنَحْنُ and we lahu لَهُ to Him mukh'liṣūna مُخْلِصُونَ (are) sincere

139

139.

Say, [O Muhammad], "Do you argue with us about Allah while He is our Lord and your Lord? For us are our deeds, and for you are your deeds. And we are sincere [in deed and intention] to Him."

139

am أَمْ Or taqūlūna تَقُولُونَ (do) you say inna إِنَّ that ib'rāhīma إِبْرَاهِيمَ Ibrahim wa-is'māʿīla وَإِسْمَاعِيلَ and Ismail wa-is'ḥāqa وَإِسْحَاقَ and Ishaq wayaʿqūba وَيَعْقُوبَ and Yaqub wal-asbāṭa وَالْأَسْبَاطَ and the descendants kānū كَانُوا were hūdan هُودًا Jews aw أَوْ or naṣārā نَصَارَى Christians qul قُلْ Say a-antum ءَأَنْتُمْ Are you aʿlamu أَعْلَمُ better knowing ami أَمِ or l-lahu اللَّهُ (is) Allah waman وَمَنْ And who aẓlamu أَظْلَمُ (is) more unjust mimman مِمَّنْ than (the one) who katama كَتَمَ concealed shahādatan شَهَادَةً a testimony ʿindahu عِنْدَهُ (that) he has mina مِنَ from l-lahi اللَّهِ Allah wamā وَمَا And not l-lahu اللَّهُ (is) Allah bighāfilin بِغَافِلٍ unaware ʿammā عَمَّا of what taʿmalūna تَعْمَلُونَ you do

140

140.

Or do you say that Abraham and Ishmael and Isaac and Jacob and the Descendants were Jews or Christians? Say, "Are you more knowing or is Allah?" And who is more unjust than one who conceals a testimony he has from Allah? And Allah is not unaware of what you do.

140

til'ka تِلْكَ This ummatun أُمَّةٌ (was) a community qad قَدْ (which) khalat خَلَتْ has passed away lahā لَهَا for it mā مَا what kasabat كَسَبَتْ it earned walakum وَلَكُمْ and for you mā مَا what kasabtum كَسَبْتُمْ you have earned walā وَلَا And not tus'alūna تُسْءَلُونَ you will be asked ʿammā عَمَّا about what kānū كَانُوا they used to yaʿmalūna يَعْمَلُونَ do

141

141.

That is a nation which has passed on. It will have [the consequence of] what it earned, and you will have what you have earned. And you will not be asked about what they used to do.

141

sayaqūlu سَيَقُولُ Will say l-sufahāu السُّفَهَاءُ the foolish ones mina مِنَ from l-nāsi النَّاسِ the people mā مَا What wallāhum وَلَّاهُمْ (has) turned them ʿan عَنْ from qib'latihimu قِبْلَتِهِمُ their direction of prayer allatī الَّتِي which kānū كَانُوا they were used to ʿalayhā عَلَيْهَا [on it] qul قُلْ Say lillahi لِلَّهِ For Allah l-mashriqu الْمَشْرِقُ (is) the east wal-maghribu وَالْمَغْرِبُ and the west yahdī يَهْدِي He guides man مَنْ whom yashāu يَشَاءُ He wills ilā إِلَى to ṣirāṭin صِرَاطٍ a path mus'taqīmin مُسْتَقِيمٍ straight

142

142.

The foolish among the people will say, "What has turned them away from their qiblah, which they used to face?" Say, "To Allah belongs the east and the west. He guides whom He wills to a straight path."

142

wakadhālika وَكَذَلِكَ And thus jaʿalnākum جَعَلْنَاكُمْ We made you ummatan أُمَّةً a community wasaṭan وَسَطًا (of the) middle way litakūnū لِتَكُونُوا so that you will be shuhadāa شُهَدَاءَ witnesses ʿalā عَلَى over l-nāsi النَّاسِ the mankind wayakūna وَيَكُونَ and will be l-rasūlu الرَّسُولُ the Messenger ʿalaykum عَلَيْكُمْ on you shahīdan شَهِيدًا a witness wamā وَمَا And not jaʿalnā جَعَلْنَا We made l-qib'lata الْقِبْلَةَ the direction of prayer allatī الَّتِي which kunta كُنْتَ you were used to ʿalayhā عَلَيْهَا [on it] illā إِلَّا except linaʿlama لِنَعْلَمَ that We make evident man مَنْ (he) who yattabiʿu يَتَّبِعُ follows l-rasūla الرَّسُولَ the Messenger mimman مِمَّنْ from (he) who yanqalibu يَنْقَلِبُ turns back ʿalā عَلَى on ʿaqibayhi عَقِبَيْهِ his heels wa-in وَإِنْ And indeed kānat كَانَتْ it was lakabīratan لَكَبِيرَةً certainly a great (test) illā إِلَّا except ʿalā عَلَى for alladhīna الَّذِينَ those whom hadā هَدَى guided l-lahu اللَّهُ (by) Allah wamā وَمَا And not kāna كَانَ will l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah liyuḍīʿa لِيُضِيعَ let go waste īmānakum إِيمَانَكُمْ your faith inna إِنَّ Indeed l-laha اللَّهَ Allah bil-nāsi بِالنَّاسِ (is) to [the] mankind laraūfun لَرَءُوفٌ Full of Kindness raḥīmun رَحِيمٌ Most Merciful

143

143.

And thus we have made you a just community that you will be witnesses over the people and the Messenger will be a witness over you. And We did not make the qiblah which you used to face except that We might make evident who would follow the Messenger from who would turn back on his heels. And indeed, it is difficult except for those whom Allah has guided. And never would Allah have caused you to lose your faith. Indeed Allah is, to the people, Kind and Merciful.

143

qad قَدْ Indeed narā نَرَى We see taqalluba تَقَلُّبَ (the) turning wajhika وَجْهِكَ (of) your face fī فِي towards l-samāi السَّمَاءِ the heaven falanuwalliyannaka فَلَنُوَلِّيَنَّكَ So We will surely turn you qib'latan قِبْلَةً (to the) direction of prayer tarḍāhā تَرْضَاهَا you will be pleased with fawalli فَوَلِّ So turn wajhaka وَجْهَكَ your face shaṭra شَطْرَ towards the direction l-masjidi الْمَسْجِدِ (of) Al-Masjid l-ḥarāmi الْحَرَامِ Al-Haraam waḥaythu وَحَيْثُ and wherever mā مَا that kuntum كُنْتُمْ you are fawallū فَوَلُّوا [so] turn wujūhakum وُجُوهَكُمْ your faces shaṭrahu شَطْرَهُ (in) its direction wa-inna وَإِنَّ And indeed alladhīna الَّذِينَ those who ūtū أُوتُوا were given l-kitāba الْكِتَابَ the Book layaʿlamūna لَيَعْلَمُونَ surely know annahu أَنَّهُ that it l-ḥaqu الْحَقُّ (is) the truth min مِنْ from rabbihim رَبِّهِمْ their Lord wamā وَمَا And not l-lahu اللَّهُ (is) Allah bighāfilin بِغَافِلٍ unaware ʿammā عَمَّا of what yaʿmalūna يَعْمَلُونَ they do

144

144.

We have certainly seen the turning of your face, [O Muhammad], toward the heaven, and We will surely turn you to a qiblah with which you will be pleased. So turn your face toward al-Masjid al-Haram. And wherever you [believers] are, turn your faces toward it [in prayer]. Indeed, those who have been given the Scripture well know that it is the truth from their Lord. And Allah is not unaware of what they do.

144

wala-in وَلَئِنْ And even if atayta أَتَيْتَ you come alladhīna الَّذِينَ (to) those who ūtū أُوتُوا were given l-kitāba الْكِتَابَ the Book bikulli بِكُلِّ with all āyatin ءَايَةٍ (the) signs mā مَا not tabiʿū تَبِعُوا they would follow qib'lataka قِبْلَتَكَ your direction of prayer wamā وَمَا and not anta أَنْتَ (will) you (be) bitābiʿin بِتَابِعٍ a follower qib'latahum قِبْلَتَهُمْ (of) their direction of prayer wamā وَمَا And not baʿḍuhum بَعْضُهُمْ some of them bitābiʿin بِتَابِعٍ (are) followers qib'lata قِبْلَةَ (of the) direction of prayer baʿḍin بَعْضٍ (of each) other wala-ini وَلَئِنِ And if ittabaʿta اتَّبَعْتَ you followed ahwāahum أَهْوَاءَهُمْ their desires min مِنْ from baʿdi بَعْدِ after mā مَا [what] jāaka جَاءَكَ came to you mina مِنَ of l-ʿil'mi الْعِلْمِ the knowledge innaka إِنَّكَ indeed, you idhan إِذًا (would) then lamina لَمِنَ (be) surely among l-ẓālimīna الظَّالِمِينَ the wrongdoers

145

145.

And if you brought to those who were given the Scripture every sign, they would not follow your qiblah. Nor will you be a follower of their qiblah. Nor would they be followers of one another's qiblah. So if you were to follow their desires after what has come to you of knowledge, indeed, you would then be among the wrongdoers.

145

alladhīna الَّذِينَ (To) those whom ātaynāhumu ءَاتَيْنَاهُمُ We gave [them] l-kitāba الْكِتَابَ the Book yaʿrifūnahu يَعْرِفُونَهُ they recognize it kamā كَمَا like yaʿrifūna يَعْرِفُونَ they recognize abnāahum أَبْنَاءَهُمْ their sons wa-inna وَإِنَّ And indeed farīqan فَرِيقًا a group min'hum مِنْهُمْ of them layaktumūna لَيَكْتُمُونَ surely they conceal l-ḥaqa الْحَقَّ the Truth wahum وَهُمْ while they yaʿlamūna يَعْلَمُونَ know

146

146.

Those to whom We gave the Scripture know him as they know their own sons. But indeed, a party of them conceal the truth while they know [it].

146

al-ḥaqu الْحَقُّ The Truth min مِنْ (is) from rabbika رَبِّكَ your Lord falā فَلَا so (do) not takūnanna تَكُونَنَّ be mina مِنَ among l-mum'tarīna الْمُمْتَرِينَ the doubters

147

147.

The truth is from your Lord, so never be among the doubters.

147

walikullin وَلِكُلٍّ And for everyone wij'hatun وِجْهَةٌ (is) a direction huwa هُوَ he muwallīhā مُوَلِّيهَا turns towards it fa-is'tabiqū فَاسْتَبِقُوا so race l-khayrāti الْخَيْرَاتِ (to) the good ayna أَيْنَ Wherever mā مَا that takūnū تَكُونُوا you will be yati يَأْتِ will bring bikumu بِكُمُ you l-lahu اللَّهُ (by) Allah jamīʿan جَمِيعًا together inna إِنَّ Indeed l-laha اللَّهَ Allah ʿalā عَلَى (is) on kulli كُلِّ every shayin شَيْءٍ thing qadīrun قَدِيرٌ All-Powerful

148

148.

For each [religious following] is a direction toward which it faces. So race to [all that is] good. Wherever you may be, Allah will bring you forth [for judgement] all together. Indeed, Allah is over all things competent.

148

wamin وَمِنْ And from ḥaythu حَيْثُ wherever kharajta خَرَجْتَ you start forth fawalli فَوَلِّ [so] turn wajhaka وَجْهَكَ your face shaṭra شَطْرَ (in the) direction l-masjidi الْمَسْجِدِ (of) Al-Masjid l-ḥarāmi الْحَرَامِ Al-Haraam wa-innahu وَإِنَّهُ And indeed, it lalḥaqqu لَلْحَقُّ (is) surely the truth min مِنْ from rabbika رَبِّكَ your Lord wamā وَمَا And not l-lahu اللَّهُ (is) Allah bighāfilin بِغَافِلٍ unaware ʿammā عَمَّا of what taʿmalūna تَعْمَلُونَ you do

149

149.

So from wherever you go out [for prayer, O Muhammad] turn your face toward al- Masjid al-Haram, and indeed, it is the truth from your Lord. And Allah is not unaware of what you do.

149

wamin وَمِنْ And from ḥaythu حَيْثُ wherever kharajta خَرَجْتَ you start forth fawalli فَوَلِّ [so] turn wajhaka وَجْهَكَ your face shaṭra شَطْرَ (in the) direction l-masjidi الْمَسْجِدِ (of) Al-Masjid l-ḥarāmi الْحَرَامِ Al-Haraam waḥaythu وَحَيْثُ And wherever mā مَا that kuntum كُنْتُمْ you (all) are fawallū فَوَلُّوا [so] turn wujūhakum وُجُوهَكُمْ your faces shaṭrahu شَطْرَهُ (in) its direction li-allā لِئَلَّا so that not yakūna يَكُونَ will be lilnnāsi لِلنَّاسِ for the people ʿalaykum عَلَيْكُمْ against you ḥujjatun حُجَّةٌ any argument illā إِلَّا except alladhīna الَّذِينَ those who ẓalamū ظَلَمُوا wronged min'hum مِنْهُمْ among them falā فَلَا so (do) not takhshawhum تَخْشَوْهُمْ fear them wa-ikh'shawnī وَاخْشَوْنِي but fear Me wali-utimma وَلِأُتِمَّ And that I complete niʿ'matī نِعْمَتِي My favor ʿalaykum عَلَيْكُمْ upon you walaʿallakum وَلَعَلَّكُمْ [and] so that you may tahtadūna تَهْتَدُونَ (be) guided

150

150.

And from wherever you go out [for prayer], turn your face toward al-Masjid al-Haram. And wherever you [believers] may be, turn your faces toward it in order that the people will not have any argument against you, except for those of them who commit wrong; so fear them not but fear Me. And [it is] so I may complete My favor upon you and that you may be guided.

150

kamā كَمَا As arsalnā أَرْسَلْنَا We sent fīkum فِيكُمْ among you rasūlan رَسُولًا a Messenger minkum مِنْكُمْ from you yatlū يَتْلُوا (who) recites ʿalaykum عَلَيْكُمْ to you āyātinā ءَايَاتِنَا Our verses wayuzakkīkum وَيُزَكِّيكُمْ and purifies you wayuʿallimukumu وَيُعَلِّمُكُمُ and teaches you l-kitāba الْكِتَابَ the Book wal-ḥik'mata وَالْحِكْمَةَ and the wisdom wayuʿallimukum وَيُعَلِّمُكُمْ and teaches you mā مَا what lam لَمْ not takūnū تَكُونُوا you were taʿlamūna تَعْلَمُونَ knowing

151

151.

Just as We have sent among you a messenger from yourselves reciting to you Our verses and purifying you and teaching you the Book and wisdom and teaching you that which you did not know.

151

fa-udh'kurūnī فَاذْكُرُونِي So remember Me adhkur'kum أَذْكُرْكُمْ I will remember you wa-ush'kurū وَاشْكُرُوا and be grateful lī لِي to Me walā وَلَا and (do) not takfurūni تَكْفُرُونِ (be) ungrateful to Me

152

152.

So remember Me; I will remember you. And be grateful to Me and do not deny Me.

152

yāayyuhā يَاأَيُّهَا O you alladhīna الَّذِينَ who āmanū ءَامَنُوا believe[d]! is'taʿīnū اسْتَعِينُوا Seek help bil-ṣabri بِالصَّبْرِ through patience wal-ṣalati وَالصَّلَوةِ and the prayer inna إِنَّ Indeed l-laha اللَّهَ Allah maʿa مَعَ (is) with l-ṣābirīna الصَّابِرِينَ the patient ones

153

153.

O you who have believed, seek help through patience and prayer. Indeed, Allah is with the patient.

153

walā وَلَا And (do) not taqūlū تَقُولُوا say liman لِمَنْ for (the ones) who yuq'talu يُقْتَلُ are slain fī فِي in sabīli سَبِيلِ (the) way l-lahi اللَّهِ (of) Allah amwātun أَمْوَاتٌ (They are) dead bal بَلْ Nay aḥyāon أَحْيَاءٌ (they are) alive walākin وَلَكِنْ [and] but lā لَا you (do) not tashʿurūna تَشْعُرُونَ perceive

154

154.

And do not say about those who are killed in the way of Allah, "They are dead." Rather, they are alive, but you perceive [it] not.

154

walanabluwannakum وَلَنَبْلُوَنَّكُمْ And surely We will test you bishayin بِشَيْءٍ with something mina مِنَ of l-khawfi الْخَوْفِ [the] fear wal-jūʿi وَالْجُوعِ and [the] hunger wanaqṣin وَنَقْصٍ and loss mina مِنَ of l-amwāli الْأَمْوَالِ [the] wealth wal-anfusi وَالْأَنْفُسِ and [the] lives wal-thamarāti وَالثَّمَرَاتِ and [the] fruits wabashiri وَبَشِّرِ but give good news l-ṣābirīna الصَّابِرِينَ (to) the patient ones

155

155.

And We will surely test you with something of fear and hunger and a loss of wealth and lives and fruits, but give good tidings to the patient,

155

alladhīna الَّذِينَ Those who idhā إِذَا when aṣābathum أَصَابَتْهُمْ strikes them muṣībatun مُصِيبَةٌ a misfortune qālū قَالُوا they say innā إِنَّا Indeed, we lillahi لِلَّهِ belong to Allah wa-innā وَإِنَّا and indeed we ilayhi إِلَيْهِ towards Him rājiʿūna رَاجِعُونَ will return

156

156.

Who, when disaster strikes them, say, "Indeed we belong to Allah, and indeed to Him we will return."

156

ulāika أُولَئِكَ Those ʿalayhim عَلَيْهِمْ on them ṣalawātun صَلَوَاتٌ (are) blessings min مِنْ from rabbihim رَبِّهِمْ their Lord waraḥmatun وَرَحْمَةٌ and Mercy wa-ulāika وَأُولَئِكَ And those humu هُمُ [they] l-muh'tadūna الْمُهْتَدُونَ (are) the guided ones

157

157.

Those are the ones upon whom are blessings from their Lord and mercy. And it is those who are the [rightly] guided.

157

inna إِنَّ Indeed l-ṣafā الصَّفَا the Safa wal-marwata وَالْمَرْوَةَ and the Marwah min مِنْ (are) from shaʿāiri شَعَائِرِ (the) symbols l-lahi اللَّهِ (of) Allah faman فَمَنْ So whoever ḥajja حَجَّ performs Hajj l-bayta الْبَيْتَ (of) the House awi أَوِ or iʿ'tamara اعْتَمَرَ performs Umrah falā فَلَا so no junāḥa جُنَاحَ blame ʿalayhi عَلَيْهِ on him an أَنْ that yaṭṭawwafa يَطَّوَّفَ he walks bihimā بِهِمَا between [both of] them waman وَمَنْ And whoever taṭawwaʿa تَطَوَّعَ voluntarily does khayran خَيْرًا good fa-inna فَإِنَّ then indeed l-laha اللَّهَ Allah shākirun شَاكِرٌ (is) All-Appreciative ʿalīmun عَلِيمٌ All-Knowing

158

158.

Indeed, as-Safa and al-Marwah are among the symbols of Allah. So whoever makes Hajj to the House or performs 'umrah - there is no blame upon him for walking between them. And whoever volunteers good - then indeed, Allah is appreciative and Knowing.

158

inna إِنَّ Indeed alladhīna الَّذِينَ those who yaktumūna يَكْتُمُونَ conceal mā مَا what anzalnā أَنْزَلْنَا We revealed mina مِنَ of l-bayināti الْبَيِّنَاتِ the clear proofs wal-hudā وَالْهُدَى and the Guidance min مِنْ from baʿdi بَعْدِ after mā مَا [what] bayyannāhu بَيَّنَّاهُ We made clear lilnnāsi لِلنَّاسِ to the people fī فِي in l-kitābi الْكِتَابِ the Book ulāika أُولَئِكَ those yalʿanuhumu يَلْعَنُهُمُ curses them l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah wayalʿanuhumu وَيَلْعَنُهُمُ and curse them l-lāʿinūna اللَّاعِنُونَ the ones who curse

159

159.

Indeed, those who conceal what We sent down of clear proofs and guidance after We made it clear for the people in the Scripture - those are cursed by Allah and cursed by those who curse,

159

illā إِلَّا Except alladhīna الَّذِينَ those tābū تَابُوا who repent[ed] wa-aṣlaḥū وَأَصْلَحُوا and reform[ed] wabayyanū وَبَيَّنُوا and openly declar[ed] fa-ulāika فَأُولَئِكَ Then those atūbu أَتُوبُ I will accept repentance ʿalayhim عَلَيْهِمْ from them wa-anā وَأَنَا and I (am) l-tawābu التَّوَّابُ the Acceptor of Repentance l-raḥīmu الرَّحِيمُ the Most Merciful

160

160.

Except for those who repent and correct themselves and make evident [what they concealed]. Those - I will accept their repentance, and I am the Accepting of repentance, the Merciful.

160

inna إِنَّ Indeed alladhīna الَّذِينَ those who kafarū كَفَرُوا disbelieve[d] wamātū وَمَاتُوا and die[d] wahum وَهُمْ while they kuffārun كُفَّارٌ (were) disbelievers ulāika أُولَئِكَ those ʿalayhim عَلَيْهِمْ on them laʿnatu لَعْنَةُ (is the) curse l-lahi اللَّهِ (of) Allah wal-malāikati وَالْمَلَائِكَةِ and the Angels wal-nāsi وَالنَّاسِ and the mankind ajmaʿīna أَجْمَعِينَ all together

161

161.

Indeed, those who disbelieve and die while they are disbelievers - upon them will be the curse of Allah and of the angels and the people, all together,

161

khālidīna خَالِدِينَ (Will) abide forever fīhā فِيهَا in it lā لَا Not yukhaffafu يُخَفَّفُ will be lightened ʿanhumu عَنْهُمُ for them l-ʿadhābu الْعَذَابُ the punishment walā وَلَا and not hum هُمْ they yunẓarūna يُنْظَرُونَ will be reprieved

162

162.

Abiding eternally therein. The punishment will not be lightened for them, nor will they be reprieved.

162

wa-ilāhukum وَإِلَهُكُمْ And your God ilāhun إِلَهٌ (is) God wāḥidun وَاحِدٌ one (only) lā لَا (there is) no ilāha إِلَهَ god illā إِلَّا except huwa هُوَ Him l-raḥmānu الرَّحْمَنُ the Most Gracious l-raḥīmu الرَّحِيمُ the Most Merciful

163

163.

And your god is one God. There is no deity [worthy of worship] except Him, the Entirely Merciful, the Especially Merciful.

163

inna إِنَّ Indeed fī فِي in khalqi خَلْقِ (the) creation l-samāwāti السَّمَاوَاتِ (of) the heavens wal-arḍi وَالْأَرْضِ and the earth wa-ikh'tilāfi وَاخْتِلَافِ and alternation al-layli اللَّيْلِ of the night wal-nahāri وَالنَّهَارِ and the day wal-ful'ki وَالْفُلْكِ and the ships allatī الَّتِي which tajrī تَجْرِي sail fī فِي in l-baḥri الْبَحْرِ the sea bimā بِمَا with what yanfaʿu يَنْفَعُ benefits l-nāsa النَّاسَ [the] people wamā وَمَا and what anzala أَنْزَلَ (has) sent down l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah mina مِنَ from l-samāi السَّمَاءِ the sky min مِنْ [of] māin مَاءٍ water fa-aḥyā فَأَحْيَا giving life bihi بِهِ thereby l-arḍa الْأَرْضَ (to) the earth baʿda بَعْدَ after mawtihā مَوْتِهَا its death wabatha وَبَثَّ and dispersing fīhā فِيهَا therein min مِنْ [of] kulli كُلِّ every dābbatin دَابَّةٍ moving creature wataṣrīfi وَتَصْرِيفِ and directing l-riyāḥi الرِّيَاحِ (of) the winds wal-saḥābi وَالسَّحَابِ and the clouds l-musakhari الْمُسَخَّرِ [the] controlled bayna بَيْنَ between l-samāi السَّمَاءِ the sky wal-arḍi وَالْأَرْضِ and the earth laāyātin لَءَايَاتٍ surely (are) Signs liqawmin لِقَوْمٍ for a people yaʿqilūna يَعْقِلُونَ who use their intellect

164

164.

Indeed, in the creation of the heavens and earth, and the alternation of the night and the day, and the [great] ships which sail through the sea with that which benefits people, and what Allah has sent down from the heavens of rain, giving life thereby to the earth after its lifelessness and dispersing therein every [kind of] moving creature, and [His] directing of the winds and the clouds controlled between the heaven and the earth are signs for a people who use reason.

164

wamina وَمِنَ And among l-nāsi النَّاسِ the mankind man مَنْ who yattakhidhu يَتَّخِذُ takes min مِنْ from dūni دُونِ besides l-lahi اللَّهِ Allah andādan أَنْدَادًا equals yuḥibbūnahum يُحِبُّونَهُمْ They love them kaḥubbi كَحُبِّ as (they should) love l-lahi اللَّهِ Allah wa-alladhīna وَالَّذِينَ And those who āmanū ءَامَنُوا believe[d] ashaddu أَشَدُّ (are) stronger ḥubban حُبًّا (in) love lillahi لِلَّهِ for Allah walaw وَلَوْ And if yarā يَرَى would see alladhīna الَّذِينَ those who ẓalamū ظَلَمُوا wronged idh إِذْ when yarawna يَرَوْنَ they will see l-ʿadhāba الْعَذَابَ the punishment anna أَنَّ that l-quwata الْقُوَّةَ the power lillahi لِلَّهِ (belongs) to Allah jamīʿan جَمِيعًا all wa-anna وَأَنَّ and [that] l-laha اللَّهَ Allah shadīdu شَدِيدُ (is) severe l-ʿadhābi الْعَذَابِ (in) [the] punishment

165

165.

And [yet], among the people are those who take other than Allah as equals [to Him]. They love them as they [should] love Allah. But those who believe are stronger in love for Allah. And if only they who have wronged would consider [that] when they see the punishment, [they will be certain] that all power belongs to Allah and that Allah is severe in punishment.

165

idh إِذْ When tabarra-a تَبَرَّأَ will disown alladhīna الَّذِينَ those who ittubiʿū اتُّبِعُوا were followed mina مِنَ [from] alladhīna الَّذِينَ those who ittabaʿū اتَّبَعُوا followed wara-awū وَرَأَوُا and they will see l-ʿadhāba الْعَذَابَ the punishment wataqaṭṭaʿat وَتَقَطَّعَتْ [and] will be cut off bihimu بِهِمُ for them l-asbābu الْأَسْبَابُ the relations

166

166.

[And they should consider that] when those who have been followed disassociate themselves from those who followed [them], and they [all] see the punishment, and cut off from them are the ties [of relationship],

166

waqāla وَقَالَ And said alladhīna الَّذِينَ those who ittabaʿū اتَّبَعُوا followed law لَوْ (Only) if anna أَنَّ [that] lanā لَنَا for us karratan كَرَّةً a return fanatabarra-a فَنَتَبَرَّأَ then we will disown min'hum مِنْهُمْ [from] them kamā كَمَا as tabarraū تَبَرَّءُوا they disown minnā مِنَّا [from] us kadhālika كَذَلِكَ Thus yurīhimu يُرِيهِمُ will show them l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah aʿmālahum أَعْمَالَهُمْ their deeds ḥasarātin حَسَرَاتٍ (as) regrets ʿalayhim عَلَيْهِمْ for them wamā وَمَا And not hum هُمْ they bikhārijīna بِخَارِجِينَ will come out mina مِنَ from l-nāri النَّارِ the Fire

167

167.

Those who followed will say, "If only we had another turn [at worldly life] so we could disassociate ourselves from them as they have disassociated themselves from us." Thus will Allah show them their deeds as regrets upon them. And they are never to emerge from the Fire.

167

yāayyuhā يَاأَيُّهَا O l-nāsu النَّاسُ mankind kulū كُلُوا Eat mimmā مِمَّا of what fī فِي (is) in l-arḍi الْأَرْضِ the earth ḥalālan حَلَالًا lawful ṭayyiban طَيِّبًا (and) good walā وَلَا And (do) not tattabiʿū تَتَّبِعُوا follow khuṭuwāti خُطُوَاتِ (the) footsteps (of) l-shayṭāni الشَّيْطَانِ the Shaitaan innahu إِنَّهُ Indeed, he lakum لَكُمْ (is) to you ʿaduwwun عَدُوٌّ an enemy mubīnun مُبِينٌ clear

168

168.

O mankind, eat from whatever is on earth [that is] lawful and good and do not follow the footsteps of Satan. Indeed, he is to you a clear enemy.

168

innamā إِنَّمَا Only yamurukum يَأْمُرُكُمْ he commands you bil-sūi بِالسُّوءِ to (do) the evil wal-faḥshāi وَالْفَحْشَاءِ and the shameful wa-an وَأَنْ and that taqūlū تَقُولُوا you say ʿalā عَلَى about l-lahi اللَّهِ Allah mā مَا what lā لَا not taʿlamūna تَعْلَمُونَ you know

169

169.

He only orders you to evil and immorality and to say about Allah what you do not know.

169

wa-idhā وَإِذَا And when qīla قِيلَ it is said lahumu لَهُمُ to them ittabiʿū اتَّبِعُوا Follow mā مَا what anzala أَنْزَلَ has revealed l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah qālū قَالُوا they said bal بَلْ Nay nattabiʿu نَتَّبِعُ we follow mā مَا what alfaynā أَلْفَيْنَا we found ʿalayhi عَلَيْهِ [on it] ābāanā ءَابَاءَنَا our forefathers (following) awalaw أَوَلَوْ Even though kāna كَانَ [were] ābāuhum ءَابَاؤُهُمْ their forefathers lā لَا (did) not yaʿqilūna يَعْقِلُونَ understand shayan شَيْئًا anything walā وَلَا and not yahtadūna يَهْتَدُونَ were they guided

170

170.

And when it is said to them, "Follow what Allah has revealed," they say, "Rather, we will follow that which we found our fathers doing." Even though their fathers understood nothing, nor were they guided?

170

wamathalu وَمَثَلُ And (the) example alladhīna الَّذِينَ (of) those who kafarū كَفَرُوا disbelieve[d] kamathali كَمَثَلِ (is) like (the) example alladhī الَّذِي (of) the one who yanʿiqu يَنْعِقُ shouts bimā بِمَا at what lā لَا not yasmaʿu يَسْمَعُ (does) hear illā إِلَّا except duʿāan دُعَاءً calls wanidāan وَنِدَاءً and cries ṣummun صُمٌّ deaf buk'mun بُكْمٌ dumb ʿum'yun عُمْيٌ (and) blind fahum فَهُمْ [so] they lā لَا (do) not yaʿqilūna يَعْقِلُونَ understand

171

171.

The example of those who disbelieve is like that of one who shouts at what hears nothing but calls and cries cattle or sheep - deaf, dumb and blind, so they do not understand.

171

yāayyuhā يَاأَيُّهَا O you alladhīna الَّذِينَ who āmanū ءَامَنُوا believe[d] kulū كُلُوا Eat min مِنْ from ṭayyibāti طَيِّبَاتِ (the) good mā مَا what razaqnākum رَزَقْنَاكُمْ We have provided you wa-ush'kurū وَاشْكُرُوا and be grateful lillahi لِلَّهِ to Allah in إِنْ if kuntum كُنْتُمْ you iyyāhu إِيَّاهُ alone taʿbudūna تَعْبُدُونَ worship Him

172

172.

O you who have believed, eat from the good things which We have provided for you and be grateful to Allah if it is [indeed] Him that you worship.

172

innamā إِنَّمَا Only ḥarrama حَرَّمَ He has forbidden ʿalaykumu عَلَيْكُمُ to you l-maytata الْمَيْتَةَ the dead animals wal-dama وَالدَّمَ and [the] blood walaḥma وَلَحْمَ and flesh l-khinzīri الْخِنْزِيرِ (of) swine wamā وَمَا and what uhilla أُهِلَّ has been dedicated bihi بِهِ [with it] lighayri لِغَيْرِ to other than l-lahi اللَّهِ Allah famani فَمَنِ So whoever uḍ'ṭurra اضْطُرَّ (is) forced by necessity ghayra غَيْرَ without bāghin بَاغٍ (being) disobedient walā وَلَا and not ʿādin عَادٍ transgressor falā فَلَا then no ith'ma إِثْمَ sin ʿalayhi عَلَيْهِ on him inna إِنَّ Indeed l-laha اللَّهَ Allah ghafūrun غَفُورٌ (is) Oft-Forgiving raḥīmun رَحِيمٌ Most Merciful

173

173.

He has only forbidden to you dead animals, blood, the flesh of swine, and that which has been dedicated to other than Allah. But whoever is forced [by necessity], neither desiring [it] nor transgressing [its limit], there is no sin upon him. Indeed, Allah is Forgiving and Merciful.

173

inna إِنَّ Indeed alladhīna الَّذِينَ those who yaktumūna يَكْتُمُونَ conceal mā مَا what anzala أَنْزَلَ (has) revealed l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah (has) mina مِنَ of l-kitābi الْكِتَابِ the Book wayashtarūna وَيَشْتَرُونَ and they purchase bihi بِهِ there with thamanan ثَمَنًا a gain qalīlan قَلِيلًا little ulāika أُولَئِكَ Those mā مَا not yakulūna يَأْكُلُونَ they eat fī فِي in buṭūnihim بُطُونِهِمْ their bellies illā إِلَّا except l-nāra النَّارَ the Fire walā وَلَا And not yukallimuhumu يُكَلِّمُهُمُ will speak to them l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah yawma يَوْمَ (on the) Day l-qiyāmati الْقِيَامَةِ (of) [the] Judgment walā وَلَا and not yuzakkīhim يُزَكِّيهِمْ will He purify them walahum وَلَهُمْ and for them ʿadhābun عَذَابٌ (is) a punishment alīmun أَلِيمٌ painful

174

174.

Indeed, they who conceal what Allah has sent down of the Book and exchange it for a small price - those consume not into their bellies except the Fire. And Allah will not speak to them on the Day of Resurrection, nor will He purify them. And they will have a painful punishment.

174

ulāika أُولَئِكَ Those alladhīna الَّذِينَ (are) they who ish'tarawū اشْتَرَوُا purchase[d] l-ḍalālata الضَّلَالَةَ [the] astraying bil-hudā بِالْهُدَى for [the] Guidance wal-ʿadhāba وَالْعَذَابَ and [the] punishment bil-maghfirati بِالْمَغْفِرَةِ for [the] forgiveness famā فَمَا So what (is) aṣbarahum أَصْبَرَهُمْ their endurance ʿalā عَلَى on l-nāri النَّارِ the Fire!

175

175.

Those are the ones who have exchanged guidance for error and forgiveness for punishment. How patient they are in pursuit of the Fire!

175

dhālika ذَلِكَ That bi-anna بِأَنَّ (is) because l-laha اللَّهَ Allah nazzala نَزَّلَ revealed l-kitāba الْكِتَابَ the Book bil-ḥaqi بِالْحَقِّ with [the] Truth wa-inna وَإِنَّ And indeed alladhīna الَّذِينَ those ikh'talafū اخْتَلَفُوا who differed fī فِي in l-kitābi الْكِتَابِ the Book lafī لَفِي (are) surely in shiqāqin شِقَاقٍ schism baʿīdin بَعِيدٍ far

176

176.

That is [deserved by them] because Allah has sent down the Book in truth. And indeed, those who differ over the Book are in extreme dissension.

176

laysa لَيْسَ It is not l-bira الْبِرَّ [the] righteousness an أَنْ that tuwallū تُوَلُّوا you turn wujūhakum وُجُوهَكُمْ your faces qibala قِبَلَ towards l-mashriqi الْمَشْرِقِ the east wal-maghribi وَالْمَغْرِبِ and the west walākinna وَلَكِنَّ [and] but l-bira الْبِرَّ the righteous[ness] man مَنْ (is he) who āmana ءَامَنَ believes bil-lahi بِاللَّهِ in Allah wal-yawmi وَالْيَوْمِ and the Day l-ākhiri الْءَاخِرِ [the] Last wal-malāikati وَالْمَلَائِكَةِ and the Angels wal-kitābi وَالْكِتَابِ and the Book wal-nabiyīna وَالنَّبِيِّينَ and the Prophets waātā وَءَاتَى and gives l-māla الْمَالَ the wealth ʿalā عَلَى in ḥubbihi حُبِّهِ spite of his love (for it) dhawī ذَوِي (to) those l-qur'bā الْقُرْبَى (of) the near relatives wal-yatāmā وَالْيَتَامَى and the orphans wal-masākīna وَالْمَسَاكِينَ and the needy wa-ib'na وَابْنَ and (of) l-sabīli السَّبِيلِ the wayfarer wal-sāilīna وَالسَّائِلِينَ and those who ask wafī وَفِي and in l-riqābi الرِّقَابِ freeing the necks (slaves) wa-aqāma وَأَقَامَ and (who) establish l-ṣalata الصَّلَوةَ the prayer waātā وَءَاتَى and give l-zakata الزَّكَوةَ the zakah wal-mūfūna وَالْمُوفُونَ and those who fulfill biʿahdihim بِعَهْدِهِمْ their covenant idhā إِذَا when ʿāhadū عَاهَدُوا they make it wal-ṣābirīna وَالصَّابِرِينَ and those who are patient fī فِي in l-basāi الْبَأْسَاءِ [the] suffering wal-ḍarāi وَالضَّرَّاءِ and [the] hardship waḥīna وَحِينَ at (the) time l-basi الْبَأْسِ (of) [the] stress ulāika أُولَئِكَ Those alladhīna الَّذِينَ (are) the ones who ṣadaqū صَدَقُوا are true wa-ulāika وَأُولَئِكَ and those humu هُمُ [they] l-mutaqūna الْمُتَّقُونَ (are) the righteous

177

177.

Righteousness is not that you turn your faces toward the east or the west, but [true] righteousness is [in] one who believes in Allah, the Last Day, the angels, the Book, and the prophets and gives wealth, in spite of love for it, to relatives, orphans, the needy, the traveler, those who ask [for help], and for freeing slaves; [and who] establishes prayer and gives zakah; [those who] fulfill their promise when they promise; and [those who] are patient in poverty and hardship and during battle. Those are the ones who have been true, and it is those who are the righteous.

177

yāayyuhā يَاأَيُّهَا O you alladhīna الَّذِينَ who āmanū ءَامَنُوا believe[d] kutiba كُتِبَ Prescribed ʿalaykumu عَلَيْكُمُ for you l-qiṣāṣu الْقِصَاصُ (is) the legal retribution fī فِي in l-qatlā الْقَتْلَى (the matter of) the murdered l-ḥuru الْحُرُّ the freeman bil-ḥuri بِالْحُرِّ for the freeman wal-ʿabdu وَالْعَبْدُ and the slave bil-ʿabdi بِالْعَبْدِ for the slave wal-unthā وَالْأُنْثَى and the female bil-unthā بِالْأُنْثَى for the female faman فَمَنْ But whoever ʿufiya عُفِيَ is pardoned lahu لَهُ [for it] min مِنْ from akhīhi أَخِيهِ his brother shayon شَيْءٌ anything fa-ittibāʿun فَاتِّبَاعٌ then follows up bil-maʿrūfi بِالْمَعْرُوفِ with suitable wa-adāon وَأَدَاءٌ [and] payment ilayhi إِلَيْهِ to him bi-iḥ'sānin بِإِحْسَانٍ with kindness dhālika ذَلِكَ That (is) takhfīfun تَخْفِيفٌ a concession min مِنْ from rabbikum رَبِّكُمْ your Lord waraḥmatun وَرَحْمَةٌ and mercy famani فَمَنِ Then whoever iʿ'tadā اعْتَدَى transgresses baʿda بَعْدَ after dhālika ذَلِكَ that falahu فَلَهُ then for him ʿadhābun عَذَابٌ (is) a punishment alīmun أَلِيمٌ painful

178

178.

O you who have believed, prescribed for you is legal retribution for those murdered - the free for the free, the slave for the slave, and the female for the female. But whoever overlooks from his brother anything, then there should be a suitable follow-up and payment to him with good conduct. This is an alleviation from your Lord and a mercy. But whoever transgresses after that will have a painful punishment.

178

walakum وَلَكُمْ And for you fī فِي in l-qiṣāṣi الْقِصَاصِ the legal retribution ḥayatun حَيَوةٌ (is) life yāulī يَاأُولِي O men l-albābi الْأَلْبَابِ (of) understanding laʿallakum لَعَلَّكُمْ So that you may tattaqūna تَتَّقُونَ (become) righteous

179

179.

And there is for you in legal retribution [saving of] life, O you [people] of understanding, that you may become righteous.

179

kutiba كُتِبَ Prescribed ʿalaykum عَلَيْكُمْ for you idhā إِذَا when ḥaḍara حَضَرَ approaches aḥadakumu أَحَدَكُمُ any of you l-mawtu الْمَوْتُ [the] death in إِنْ if taraka تَرَكَ he leaves khayran خَيْرًا good l-waṣiyatu الْوَصِيَّةُ (making) the will lil'wālidayni لِلْوَالِدَيْنِ for the parents wal-aqrabīna وَالْأَقْرَبِينَ and the near relatives bil-maʿrūfi بِالْمَعْرُوفِ with due fairness ḥaqqan حَقًّا a duty ʿalā عَلَى on l-mutaqīna الْمُتَّقِينَ the righteous ones

180

180.

Prescribed for you when death approaches [any] one of you if he leaves wealth [is that he should make] a bequest for the parents and near relatives according to what is acceptable - a duty upon the righteous.

180

faman فَمَنْ Then whoever baddalahu بَدَّلَهُ changes it baʿdamā بَعْدَمَا after what samiʿahu سَمِعَهُ he (has) heard [it] fa-innamā فَإِنَّمَا so only ith'muhu إِثْمُهُ its sin ʿalā عَلَى (would be) on alladhīna الَّذِينَ those who yubaddilūnahu يُبَدِّلُونَهُ alter it inna إِنَّ Indeed l-laha اللَّهَ Allah samīʿun سَمِيعٌ (is) All-Hearing ʿalīmun عَلِيمٌ All-Knowing

181

181.

Then whoever alters the bequest after he has heard it - the sin is only upon those who have altered it. Indeed, Allah is Hearing and Knowing.

181

faman فَمَنْ But whoever khāfa خَافَ fears min مِنْ from mūṣin مُوصٍ (the) testator janafan جَنَفًا (any) error aw أَوْ or ith'man إِثْمًا sin fa-aṣlaḥa فَأَصْلَحَ then reconciles baynahum بَيْنَهُمْ between them falā فَلَا then (there is) no ith'ma إِثْمَ sin ʿalayhi عَلَيْهِ on him inna إِنَّ Indeed l-laha اللَّهَ Allah ghafūrun غَفُورٌ (is) Oft-Forgiving raḥīmun رَحِيمٌ All-Merciful

182

182.

But if one fears from the bequeather [some] error or sin and corrects that which is between them, there is no sin upon him. Indeed, Allah is Forgiving and Merciful.

182

yāayyuhā يَاأَيُّهَا O you alladhīna الَّذِينَ who āmanū ءَامَنُوا believe[d] kutiba كُتِبَ Is prescribed ʿalaykumu عَلَيْكُمُ for you l-ṣiyāmu الصِّيَامُ [the] fasting kamā كَمَا as kutiba كُتِبَ was prescribed ʿalā عَلَى to alladhīna الَّذِينَ those min مِنْ from qablikum قَبْلِكُمْ before you laʿallakum لَعَلَّكُمْ so that you may tattaqūna تَتَّقُونَ (become) righteous

183

183.

O you who have believed, decreed upon you is fasting as it was decreed upon those before you that you may become righteous -

183

ayyāman أَيَّامًا (Fasting for) days maʿdūdātin مَعْدُودَاتٍ numbered faman فَمَنْ So whoever kāna كَانَ is minkum مِنْكُمْ among you marīḍan مَرِيضًا sick aw أَوْ or ʿalā عَلَى on safarin سَفَرٍ a journey faʿiddatun فَعِدَّةٌ then a prescribed number min مِنْ of ayyāmin أَيَّامٍ days ukhara أُخَرَ other waʿalā وَعَلَى And on alladhīna الَّذِينَ those who yuṭīqūnahu يُطِيقُونَهُ can afford it fid'yatun فِدْيَةٌ a ransom ṭaʿāmu طَعَامُ (of) feeding mis'kīnin مِسْكِينٍ a poor faman فَمَنْ And whoever taṭawwaʿa تَطَوَّعَ volunteers khayran خَيْرًا good fahuwa فَهُوَ then it khayrun خَيْرٌ (is) better lahu لَهُ for him wa-an وَأَنْ And to taṣūmū تَصُومُوا fast khayrun خَيْرٌ (is) better lakum لَكُمْ for you in إِنْ if kuntum كُنْتُمْ you taʿlamūna تَعْلَمُونَ know

184

184.

[Fasting for] a limited number of days. So whoever among you is ill or on a journey [during them] - then an equal number of days [are to be made up]. And upon those who are able [to fast, but with hardship] - a ransom [as substitute] of feeding a poor person [each day]. And whoever volunteers excess - it is better for him. But to fast is best for you, if you only knew.

184

shahru شَهْرُ Month ramaḍāna رَمَضَانَ (of) Ramadhaan alladhī الَّذِي (is) that unzila أُنْزِلَ was revealed fīhi فِيهِ therein l-qur'ānu الْقُرْءَانُ the Quran hudan هُدًى a Guidance lilnnāsi لِلنَّاسِ for mankind wabayyinātin وَبَيِّنَاتٍ and clear proofs mina مِنَ of l-hudā الْهُدَى [the] Guidance wal-fur'qāni وَالْفُرْقَانِ and the Criterion faman فَمَنْ So whoever shahida شَهِدَ witnesses minkumu مِنْكُمُ among you l-shahra الشَّهْرَ the month falyaṣum'hu فَلْيَصُمْهُ then he should fast in it waman وَمَنْ and whoever kāna كَانَ is marīḍan مَرِيضًا sick aw أَوْ or ʿalā عَلَى on safarin سَفَرٍ a journey faʿiddatun فَعِدَّةٌ then prescribed number (should be made up) min مِنْ from ayyāmin أَيَّامٍ days ukhara أُخَرَ other yurīdu يُرِيدُ Intends l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah bikumu بِكُمُ for you l-yus'ra الْيُسْرَ [the] ease walā وَلَا and not yurīdu يُرِيدُ intends bikumu بِكُمُ for you l-ʿus'ra الْعُسْرَ [the] hardship walituk'milū وَلِتُكْمِلُوا so that you complete l-ʿidata الْعِدَّةَ the prescribed period walitukabbirū وَلِتُكَبِّرُوا and that you magnify l-laha اللَّهَ Allah ʿalā عَلَى for mā مَا [what] hadākum هَدَاكُمْ He guided you walaʿallakum وَلَعَلَّكُمْ so that you may tashkurūna تَشْكُرُونَ (be) grateful

185

185.

The month of Ramadhan [is that] in which was revealed the Qur'an, a guidance for the people and clear proofs of guidance and criterion. So whoever sights [the new moon of] the month, let him fast it; and whoever is ill or on a journey - then an equal number of other days. Allah intends for you ease and does not intend for you hardship and [wants] for you to complete the period and to glorify Allah for that [to] which He has guided you; and perhaps you will be grateful.

185

wa-idhā وَإِذَا And when sa-alaka سَأَلَكَ ask you ʿibādī عِبَادِي My servants ʿannī عَنِّي about Me fa-innī فَإِنِّي then indeed I am qarībun قَرِيبٌ near ujību أُجِيبُ I respond daʿwata دَعْوَةَ (to the) invocation l-dāʿi الدَّاعِ (of) the supplicant idhā إِذَا when daʿāni دَعَانِ he calls Me falyastajībū فَلْيَسْتَجِيبُوا So let them respond lī لِي to Me walyu'minū وَلْيُؤْمِنُوا and let them believe bī بِي in Me laʿallahum لَعَلَّهُمْ so that they may yarshudūna يَرْشُدُونَ (be) led aright

186

186.

And when My servants ask you, [O Muhammad], concerning Me - indeed I am near. I respond to the invocation of the supplicant when he calls upon Me. So let them respond to Me [by obedience] and believe in Me that they may be [rightly] guided.

186

uḥilla أُحِلَّ Permitted lakum لَكُمْ for you laylata لَيْلَةَ (in the) nights l-ṣiyāmi الصِّيَامِ (of) fasting l-rafathu الرَّفَثُ (is) the approach ilā إِلَى to nisāikum نِسَائِكُمْ your wives hunna هُنَّ They libāsun لِبَاسٌ (are) garments lakum لَكُمْ for you wa-antum وَأَنْتُمْ and you libāsun لِبَاسٌ (are) garments lahunna لَهُنَّ for them ʿalima عَلِمَ Knows l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah annakum أَنَّكُمْ that you kuntum كُنْتُمْ used to takhtānūna تَخْتَانُونَ deceive anfusakum أَنْفُسَكُمْ yourselves fatāba فَتَابَ so He turned ʿalaykum عَلَيْكُمْ towards you waʿafā وَعَفَا and He forgave ʿankum عَنْكُمْ [on] you fal-āna فَالْءَانَ So now bāshirūhunna بَاشِرُوهُنَّ have relations with them wa-ib'taghū وَابْتَغُوا and seek mā مَا what kataba كَتَبَ has ordained l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah lakum لَكُمْ for you wakulū وَكُلُوا And eat wa-ish'rabū وَاشْرَبُوا and drink ḥattā حَتَّى until yatabayyana يَتَبَيَّنَ becomes distinct lakumu لَكُمُ to you l-khayṭu الْخَيْطُ the thread l-abyaḍu الْأَبْيَضُ [the] white mina مِنَ from l-khayṭi الْخَيْطِ the thread l-aswadi الْأَسْوَدِ [the] black mina مِنَ of l-fajri الْفَجْرِ [the] dawn thumma ثُمَّ Then atimmū أَتِمُّوا complete l-ṣiyāma الصِّيَامَ the fast ilā إِلَى till al-layli اللَّيْلِ the night walā وَلَا And (do) not tubāshirūhunna تُبَاشِرُوهُنَّ have relations with them wa-antum وَأَنْتُمْ while you ʿākifūna عَاكِفُونَ (are) secluded fī فِي in l-masājidi الْمَسَاجِدِ the masajid til'ka تِلْكَ These ḥudūdu حُدُودُ (are the) limits l-lahi اللَّهِ (set by) Allah falā فَلَا so (do) not taqrabūhā تَقْرَبُوهَا approach them kadhālika كَذَلِكَ Thus yubayyinu يُبَيِّنُ makes clear l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah āyātihi ءَايَاتِهِ His verses lilnnāsi لِلنَّاسِ for [the] people laʿallahum لَعَلَّهُمْ so that they may yattaqūna يَتَّقُونَ (become) righteous

187

187.

It has been made permissible for you the night preceding fasting to go to your wives [for sexual relations]. They are clothing for you and you are clothing for them. Allah knows that you used to deceive yourselves, so He accepted your repentance and forgave you. So now, have relations with them and seek that which Allah has decreed for you. And eat and drink until the white thread of dawn becomes distinct to you from the black thread [of night]. Then complete the fast until the sunset. And do not have relations with them as long as you are staying for worship in the mosques. These are the limits [set by] Allah, so do not approach them. Thus does Allah make clear His ordinances to the people that they may become righteous.

187

walā وَلَا And (do) not takulū تَأْكُلُوا eat amwālakum أَمْوَالَكُمْ your properties baynakum بَيْنَكُمْ among yourselves bil-bāṭili بِالْبَاطِلِ wrongfully watud'lū وَتُدْلُوا and present bihā بِهَا [with] it ilā إِلَى to l-ḥukāmi الْحُكَّامِ the authorities litakulū لِتَأْكُلُوا so that you may eat farīqan فَرِيقًا a portion min مِنْ from amwāli أَمْوَالِ (the) wealth l-nāsi النَّاسِ (of) the people bil-ith'mi بِالْإِثْمِ sinfully wa-antum وَأَنْتُمْ while you taʿlamūna تَعْلَمُونَ know

188

188.

And do not consume one another's wealth unjustly or send it [in bribery] to the rulers in order that [they might aid] you [to] consume a portion of the wealth of the people in sin, while you know [it is unlawful].

188

yasalūnaka يَسْءَلُونَكَ They ask you ʿani عَنِ about l-ahilati الْأَهِلَّةِ the new moons qul قُلْ Say hiya هِيَ They mawāqītu مَوَاقِيتُ (are) indicators of periods lilnnāsi لِلنَّاسِ for the people wal-ḥaji وَالْحَجِّ and (for) the Hajj walaysa وَلَيْسَ And it is not l-biru الْبِرُّ [the] righteousness bi-an بِأَنْ that tatū تَأْتُوا you come l-buyūta الْبُيُوتَ (to) the houses min مِنْ from ẓuhūrihā ظُهُورِهَا their backs walākinna وَلَكِنَّ [and] but l-bira الْبِرَّ [the] righteous mani مَنِ (is one) who ittaqā اتَّقَى fears (Allah) watū وَأْتُوا And come l-buyūta الْبُيُوتَ (to) the houses min مِنْ from abwābihā أَبْوَابِهَا their doors wa-ittaqū وَاتَّقُوا And fear l-laha اللَّهَ Allah laʿallakum لَعَلَّكُمْ so that you may tuf'liḥūna تُفْلِحُونَ (be) successful

189

189.

They ask you, [O Muhammad], about the new moons. Say, "They are measurements of time for the people and for Hajj." And it is not righteousness to enter houses from the back, but righteousness is [in] one who fears Allah. And enter houses from their doors. And fear Allah that you may succeed.

189

waqātilū وَقَاتِلُوا And fight fī فِي in sabīli سَبِيلِ (the) way l-lahi اللَّهِ (of) Allah alladhīna الَّذِينَ those who yuqātilūnakum يُقَاتِلُونَكُمْ fight you walā وَلَا and (do) not taʿtadū تَعْتَدُوا transgress inna إِنَّ Indeed l-laha اللَّهَ Allah lā لَا (does) not yuḥibbu يُحِبُّ like l-muʿ'tadīna الْمُعْتَدِينَ the transgressors

190

190.

Fight in the way of Allah those who fight you but do not transgress. Indeed. Allah does not like transgressors.

190

wa-uq'tulūhum وَاقْتُلُوهُمْ And kill them ḥaythu حَيْثُ wherever thaqif'tumūhum ثَقِفْتُمُوهُمْ you find them wa-akhrijūhum وَأَخْرِجُوهُمْ and drive them out min مِنْ from ḥaythu حَيْثُ wherever akhrajūkum أَخْرَجُوكُمْ they drove you out wal-fit'natu وَالْفِتْنَةُ and [the] oppression ashaddu أَشَدُّ (is) worse mina مِنَ than l-qatli الْقَتْلِ [the] killing walā وَلَا And (do) not tuqātilūhum تُقَاتِلُوهُمْ fight them ʿinda عِنْدَ near l-masjidi الْمَسْجِدِ Al-Masjid l-ḥarāmi الْحَرَامِ Al-Haraam ḥattā حَتَّى until yuqātilūkum يُقَاتِلُوكُمْ they fight you fīhi فِيهِ in it fa-in فَإِنْ Then if qātalūkum قَاتَلُوكُمْ they fight you fa-uq'tulūhum فَاقْتُلُوهُمْ then kill them kadhālika كَذَلِكَ Such jazāu جَزَاءُ (is the) reward l-kāfirīna الْكَافِرِينَ (of) the disbelievers

191

191.

And kill them wherever you overtake them and expel them from wherever they have expelled you, and fitnah is worse than killing. And do not fight them at al-Masjid al- Haram until they fight you there. But if they fight you, then kill them. Such is the recompense of the disbelievers.

191

fa-ini فَإِنِ Then if intahaw انْتَهَوْا they cease fa-inna فَإِنَّ then indeed l-laha اللَّهَ Allah ghafūrun غَفُورٌ (is) Oft-Forgiving raḥīmun رَحِيمٌ Most Merciful

192

192.

And if they cease, then indeed, Allah is Forgiving and Merciful.

192

waqātilūhum وَقَاتِلُوهُمْ And fight (against) them ḥattā حَتَّى until lā لَا not takūna تَكُونَ (there) is fit'natun فِتْنَةٌ oppression wayakūna وَيَكُونَ and becomes l-dīnu الدِّينُ the religion lillahi لِلَّهِ for Allah fa-ini فَإِنِ Then if intahaw انْتَهَوْا they cease falā فَلَا then (let there be) no ʿud'wāna عُدْوَانَ hostility illā إِلَّا except ʿalā عَلَى against l-ẓālimīna الظَّالِمِينَ the oppressors

193

193.

Fight them until there is no [more] fitnah and [until] worship is [acknowledged to be] for Allah. But if they cease, then there is to be no aggression except against the oppressors.

193

al-shahru الشَّهْرُ The month l-ḥarāmu الْحَرَامُ [the] sacred bil-shahri بِالشَّهْرِ (is) for the month l-ḥarāmi الْحَرَامِ [the] sacred wal-ḥurumātu وَالْحُرُمَاتُ and for all the violations qiṣāṣun قِصَاصٌ (is) legal retribution famani فَمَنِ Then whoever iʿ'tadā اعْتَدَى transgressed ʿalaykum عَلَيْكُمْ upon you fa-iʿ'tadū فَاعْتَدُوا then you transgress ʿalayhi عَلَيْهِ on him bimith'li بِمِثْلِ in (the) same manner mā مَا (as) iʿ'tadā اعْتَدَى he transgressed ʿalaykum عَلَيْكُمْ upon you wa-ittaqū وَاتَّقُوا And fear l-laha اللَّهَ Allah wa-iʿ'lamū وَاعْلَمُوا and know anna أَنَّ that l-laha اللَّهَ Allah maʿa مَعَ (is) with l-mutaqīna الْمُتَّقِينَ those who fear (Him)

194

194.

[Fighting in] the sacred month is for [aggression committed in] the sacred month, and for [all] violations is legal retribution. So whoever has assaulted you, then assault him in the same way that he has assaulted you. And fear Allah and know that Allah is with those who fear Him.

194

wa-anfiqū وَأَنْفِقُوا And spend fī فِي in sabīli سَبِيلِ (the) way l-lahi اللَّهِ (of) Allah walā وَلَا and (do) not tul'qū تُلْقُوا throw (yourselves) bi-aydīkum بِأَيْدِيكُمْ [with your hands] ilā إِلَى into l-tahlukati التَّهْلُكَةِ [the] destruction wa-aḥsinū وَأَحْسِنُوا And do good inna إِنَّ indeed l-laha اللَّهَ Allah yuḥibbu يُحِبُّ loves l-muḥ'sinīna الْمُحْسِنِينَ the good-doers

195

195.

And spend in the way of Allah and do not throw [yourselves] with your [own] hands into destruction [by refraining]. And do good; indeed, Allah loves the doers of good.

195

wa-atimmū وَأَتِمُّوا And complete l-ḥaja الْحَجَّ the Hajj wal-ʿum'rata وَالْعُمْرَةَ and the Umrah lillahi لِلَّهِ for Allah fa-in فَإِنْ And if uḥ'ṣir'tum أُحْصِرْتُمْ you are held back famā فَمَا then (offer) whatever is'taysara اسْتَيْسَرَ (can be) obtained with ease mina مِنَ of l-hadyi الْهَدْيِ the sacrificial animal walā وَلَا And (do) not taḥliqū تَحْلِقُوا shave ruūsakum رُءُوسَكُمْ your heads ḥattā حَتَّى until yablugha يَبْلُغَ reaches l-hadyu الْهَدْيُ the sacrificial animal maḥillahu مَحِلَّهُ (to) its destination faman فَمَنْ Then whoever kāna كَانَ is minkum مِنْكُمْ among you marīḍan مَرِيضًا ill aw أَوْ or bihi بِهِ he (has) adhan أَذًى an ailment min مِنْ of rasihi رَأْسِهِ his head fafid'yatun فَفِدْيَةٌ then a ransom min مِنْ of ṣiyāmin صِيَامٍ fasting aw أَوْ or ṣadaqatin صَدَقَةٍ charity aw أَوْ or nusukin نُسُكٍ sacrifice fa-idhā فَإِذَا Then when amintum أَمِنْتُمْ you are secure faman فَمَنْ then whoever tamattaʿa تَمَتَّعَ took advantage bil-ʿum'rati بِالْعُمْرَةِ of the Umrah ilā إِلَى followed l-ḥaji الْحَجِّ (by) the Hajj famā فَمَا then (offer) whatever is'taysara اسْتَيْسَرَ (can be) obtained with ease mina مِنَ of l-hadyi الْهَدْيِ the sacrificial animal faman فَمَنْ But whoever lam لَمْ (can) not yajid يَجِدْ find faṣiyāmu فَصِيَامُ then a fast thalāthati ثَلَاثَةِ (of) three ayyāmin أَيَّامٍ days fī فِي during l-ḥaji الْحَجِّ the Hajj wasabʿatin وَسَبْعَةٍ and seven (days) idhā إِذَا when rajaʿtum رَجَعْتُمْ you return til'ka تِلْكَ This ʿasharatun عَشَرَةٌ (is) ten (days) kāmilatun كَامِلَةٌ in all dhālika ذَلِكَ That liman لِمَنْ (is) for (the one) whose lam لَمْ not yakun يَكُنْ is ahluhu أَهْلُهُ his family ḥāḍirī حَاضِرِي present l-masjidi الْمَسْجِدِ (near) Al-Masjid l-ḥarāmi الْحَرَامِ Al-Haraam wa-ittaqū وَاتَّقُوا And fear l-laha اللَّهَ Allah wa-iʿ'lamū وَاعْلَمُوا and know anna أَنَّ that l-laha اللَّهَ Allah shadīdu شَدِيدُ (is) severe l-ʿiqābi الْعِقَابِ (in) retribution

196

196.

And complete the Hajj and 'umrah for Allah. But if you are prevented, then [offer] what can be obtained with ease of sacrificial animals. And do not shave your heads until the sacrificial animal has reached its place of slaughter. And whoever among you is ill or has an ailment of the head [making shaving necessary must offer] a ransom of fasting [three days] or charity or sacrifice. And when you are secure, then whoever performs 'umrah [during the Hajj months] followed by Hajj [offers] what can be obtained with ease of sacrificial animals. And whoever cannot find [or afford such an animal] - then a fast of three days during Hajj and of seven when you have returned [home]. Those are ten complete [days]. This is for those whose family is not in the area of al-Masjid al-Haram. And fear Allah and know that Allah is severe in penalty.

196

al-ḥaju الْحَجُّ (For) the Hajj ashhurun أَشْهُرٌ (are) months maʿlūmātun مَعْلُومَاتٌ well known faman فَمَنْ then whoever faraḍa فَرَضَ undertakes fīhinna فِيهِنَّ therein l-ḥaja الْحَجَّ the Hajj falā فَلَا then no rafatha رَفَثَ sexual relations walā وَلَا and no fusūqa فُسُوقَ wickedness walā وَلَا and no jidāla جِدَالَ quarrelling fī فِي during l-ḥaji الْحَجِّ the Hajj wamā وَمَا And whatever tafʿalū تَفْعَلُوا you do min مِنْ of khayrin خَيْرٍ good yaʿlamhu يَعْلَمْهُ knows it l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah watazawwadū وَتَزَوَّدُوا And take provision fa-inna فَإِنَّ (but) indeed khayra خَيْرَ (the) best l-zādi الزَّادِ provision l-taqwā التَّقْوَى (is) righteousness wa-ittaqūni وَاتَّقُونِ And fear Me yāulī يَاأُولِي O men l-albābi الْأَلْبَابِ (of) understanding

197

197.

Hajj is [during] well-known months, so whoever has made Hajj obligatory upon himself therein [by entering the state of ihram], there is [to be for him] no sexual relations and no disobedience and no disputing during Hajj. And whatever good you do - Allah knows it. And take provisions, but indeed, the best provision is fear of Allah. And fear Me, O you of understanding.

197

laysa لَيْسَ Not is ʿalaykum عَلَيْكُمْ on you junāḥun جُنَاحٌ any sin an أَنْ that tabtaghū تَبْتَغُوا you seek faḍlan فَضْلًا bounty min مِنْ from rabbikum رَبِّكُمْ your Lord fa-idhā فَإِذَا And when afaḍtum أَفَضْتُمْ you depart min مِنْ from ʿarafātin عَرَفَاتٍ (Mount) Arafat fa-udh'kurū فَاذْكُرُوا then remember l-laha اللَّهَ Allah ʿinda عِنْدَ near l-mashʿari الْمَشْعَرِ the Monument l-ḥarāmi الْحَرَامِ [the] Sacred wa-udh'kurūhu وَاذْكُرُوهُ And remember Him kamā كَمَا as hadākum هَدَاكُمْ He (has) guided you wa-in وَإِنْ [and] though kuntum كُنْتُمْ you were min مِنْ [from] qablihi قَبْلِهِ before [it] lamina لَمِنَ surely among l-ḍālīna الضَّالِّينَ those who went astray

198

198.

There is no blame upon you for seeking bounty from your Lord [during Hajj]. But when you depart from 'Arafat, remember Allah at al- Mash'ar al-Haram. And remember Him, as He has guided you, for indeed, you were before that among those astray.

198

thumma ثُمَّ Then afīḍū أَفِيضُوا depart min مِنْ from ḥaythu حَيْثُ wherever afāḍa أَفَاضَ depart l-nāsu النَّاسُ the people wa-is'taghfirū وَاسْتَغْفِرُوا and ask forgiveness l-laha اللَّهَ (of) Allah inna إِنَّ Indeed l-laha اللَّهَ Allah ghafūrun غَفُورٌ (is) Oft-Forgiving raḥīmun رَحِيمٌ All-Merciful

199

199.

Then depart from the place from where [all] the people depart and ask forgiveness of Allah. Indeed, Allah is Forgiving and Merciful.

199

fa-idhā فَإِذَا Then when qaḍaytum قَضَيْتُمْ you complete[d] manāsikakum مَنَاسِكَكُمْ your acts of worship fa-udh'kurū فَاذْكُرُوا then remember l-laha اللَّهَ Allah kadhik'rikum كَذِكْرِكُمْ as you remember ābāakum ءَابَاءَكُمْ your forefathers aw أَوْ or ashadda أَشَدَّ (with) greater dhik'ran ذِكْرًا remembrance famina فَمِنَ And from l-nāsi النَّاسِ the people man مَنْ who yaqūlu يَقُولُ say rabbanā رَبَّنَا Our Lord! ātinā ءَاتِنَا Grant us fī فِي in l-dun'yā الدُّنْيَا the world wamā وَمَا And not lahu لَهُ for him fī فِي in l-ākhirati الْءَاخِرَةِ the Hereafter min مِنْ [of] khalāqin خَلَاقٍ any share

200

200.

And when you have completed your rites, remember Allah like your [previous] remembrance of your fathers or with [much] greater remembrance. And among the people is he who says, "Our Lord, give us in this world," and he will have in the Hereafter no share.

200

wamin'hum وَمِنْهُمْ And from those man مَنْ who yaqūlu يَقُولُ say rabbanā رَبَّنَا Our Lord! ātinā ءَاتِنَا Grant us fī فِي in l-dun'yā الدُّنْيَا the world ḥasanatan حَسَنَةً good wafī وَفِي and in l-ākhirati الْءَاخِرَةِ the Hereafter ḥasanatan حَسَنَةً good waqinā وَقِنَا and save us ʿadhāba عَذَابَ (from the) punishment l-nāri النَّارِ (of) the Fire

201

201.

But among them is he who says, "Our Lord, give us in this world [that which is] good and in the Hereafter [that which is] good and protect us from the punishment of the Fire."

201

ulāika أُولَئِكَ Those lahum لَهُمْ for them naṣībun نَصِيبٌ (is) a share mimmā مِمَّا of what kasabū كَسَبُوا they earned wal-lahu وَاللَّهُ and Allah sarīʿu سَرِيعُ (is) swift l-ḥisābi الْحِسَابِ (in taking) account

202

202.

Those will have a share of what they have earned, and Allah is swift in account.

202

wa-udh'kurū وَاذْكُرُوا And remember l-laha اللَّهَ Allah fī فِي during ayyāmin أَيَّامٍ days maʿdūdātin مَعْدُودَاتٍ numbered faman فَمَنْ Then (he) who taʿajjala تَعَجَّلَ hurries fī فِي in yawmayni يَوْمَيْنِ two days falā فَلَا then no ith'ma إِثْمَ sin ʿalayhi عَلَيْهِ upon him waman وَمَنْ and whoever ta-akhara تَأَخَّرَ delays falā فَلَا then no ith'ma إِثْمَ sin ʿalayhi عَلَيْهِ upon him limani لِمَنِ for (the one) who ittaqā اتَّقَى fears wa-ittaqū وَاتَّقُوا And fear l-laha اللَّهَ Allah wa-iʿ'lamū وَاعْلَمُوا and know annakum أَنَّكُمْ that you ilayhi إِلَيْهِ unto Him tuḥ'sharūna تُحْشَرُونَ will be gathered

203

203.

And remember Allah during [specific] numbered days. Then whoever hastens [his departure] in two days - there is no sin upon him; and whoever delays [until the third] - there is no sin upon him - for him who fears Allah. And fear Allah and know that unto Him you will be gathered.

203

wamina وَمِنَ And of l-nāsi النَّاسِ the people man مَنْ (is the one) who yuʿ'jibuka يُعْجِبُكَ pleases you qawluhu قَوْلُهُ (with) his speech fī فِي in l-ḥayati الْحَيَوةِ the life l-dun'yā الدُّنْيَا (of) the world wayush'hidu وَيُشْهِدُ and he calls to witness l-laha اللَّهَ Allah ʿalā عَلَى on mā مَا what fī فِي (is) in qalbihi قَلْبِهِ his heart wahuwa وَهُوَ and he aladdu أَلَدُّ (is) the most quarrelsome l-khiṣāmi الْخِصَامِ (of) opponents

204

204.

And of the people is he whose speech pleases you in worldly life, and he calls Allah to witness as to what is in his heart, yet he is the fiercest of opponents.

204

wa-idhā وَإِذَا And when tawallā تَوَلَّى he turns away saʿā سَعَى he strives fī فِي in l-arḍi الْأَرْضِ the earth liyuf'sida لِيُفْسِدَ to spread corruption fīhā فِيهَا [in it] wayuh'lika وَيُهْلِكَ and destroys l-ḥartha الْحَرْثَ the crops wal-nasla وَالنَّسْلَ and progeny wal-lahu وَاللَّهُ And Allah lā لَا (does) not yuḥibbu يُحِبُّ love l-fasāda الْفَسَادَ [the] corruption

205

205.

And when he goes away, he strives throughout the land to cause corruption therein and destroy crops and animals. And Allah does not like corruption.

205

wa-idhā وَإِذَا And when qīla قِيلَ it is said lahu لَهُ to him ittaqi اتَّقِ Fear l-laha اللَّهَ Allah akhadhathu أَخَذَتْهُ takes him l-ʿizatu الْعِزَّةُ (his) pride bil-ith'mi بِالْإِثْمِ to [the] sins faḥasbuhu فَحَسْبُهُ Then enough for him jahannamu جَهَنَّمُ (is) Hell walabi'sa وَلَبِئْسَ [and] surely an evil l-mihādu الْمِهَادُ [the] resting-place

206

206.

And when it is said to him, "Fear Allah," pride in the sin takes hold of him. Sufficient for him is Hellfire, and how wretched is the resting place.

206

wamina وَمِنَ And of l-nāsi النَّاسِ the people man مَنْ (is the one) who yashrī يَشْرِي sells nafsahu نَفْسَهُ his own self ib'tighāa ابْتِغَاءَ seeking marḍāti مَرْضَاتِ pleasure l-lahi اللَّهِ (of) Allah wal-lahu وَاللَّهُ And Allah raūfun رَءُوفٌ (is) full of Kindness bil-ʿibādi بِالْعِبَادِ to His servants

207

207.

And of the people is he who sells himself, seeking means to the approval of Allah. And Allah is kind to [His] servants.

207

yāayyuhā يَاأَيُّهَا O you alladhīna الَّذِينَ who āmanū ءَامَنُوا believe[d]! ud'khulū ادْخُلُوا Enter fī فِي in l-sil'mi السِّلْمِ Islam kāffatan كَافَّةً completely walā وَلَا and (do) not tattabiʿū تَتَّبِعُوا follow khuṭuwāti خُطُوَاتِ footsteps l-shayṭāni الشَّيْطَانِ (of) the Shaitaan innahu إِنَّهُ Indeed he lakum لَكُمْ (is) for you ʿaduwwun عَدُوٌّ an enemy mubīnun مُبِينٌ open

208

208.

O you who have believed, enter into Islam completely [and perfectly] and do not follow the footsteps of Satan. Indeed, he is to you a clear enemy.

208

fa-in فَإِنْ Then if zalaltum زَلَلْتُمْ you slip min مِنْ from baʿdi بَعْدِ after mā مَا [what] jāatkumu جَاءَتْكُمُ came to you l-bayinātu الْبَيِّنَاتُ (from) the clear proofs fa-iʿ'lamū فَاعْلَمُوا then know anna أَنَّ that l-laha اللَّهَ Allah ʿazīzun عَزِيزٌ (is) All-Mighty ḥakīmun حَكِيمٌ All-Wise

209

209.

But if you deviate after clear proofs have come to you, then know that Allah is Exalted in Might and Wise.

209

hal هَلْ Are yanẓurūna يَنْظُرُونَ they waiting illā إِلَّا [except] an أَنْ that yatiyahumu يَأْتِيَهُمُ comes to them l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah fī فِي in ẓulalin ظُلَلٍ (the) shadows mina مِنَ of l-ghamāmi الْغَمَامِ [the] clouds wal-malāikatu وَالْمَلَائِكَةُ and the Angels waquḍiya وَقُضِيَ and is decreed l-amru الْأَمْرُ the matter wa-ilā وَإِلَى And to l-lahi اللَّهِ Allah tur'jaʿu تُرْجَعُ return l-umūru الْأُمُورُ (all) the matters

210

210.

Do they await but that Allah should come to them in covers of clouds and the angels [as well] and the matter is [then] decided? And to Allah [all] matters are returned.

210

sal سَلْ Ask banī بَنِي (the) Children is'rāīla إِسْرَاءِيلَ (of) Israel kam كَمْ how many ātaynāhum ءَاتَيْنَاهُمْ We gave them min مِنْ of āyatin ءَايَةٍ (the) Sign(s) bayyinatin بَيِّنَةٍ clear waman وَمَنْ And whoever yubaddil يُبَدِّلْ changes niʿ'mata نِعْمَةَ Favor l-lahi اللَّهِ (of) Allah min مِنْ from baʿdi بَعْدِ after mā مَا [what] jāathu جَاءَتْهُ it (has) come to him fa-inna فَإِنَّ then indeed l-laha اللَّهَ Allah shadīdu شَدِيدُ (is) severe l-ʿiqābi الْعِقَابِ in [the] chastising

211

211.

Ask the Children of Israel how many a sign of evidence We have given them. And whoever exchanges the favor of Allah [for disbelief] after it has come to him - then indeed, Allah is severe in penalty.

211

zuyyina زُيِّنَ Beautified lilladhīna لِلَّذِينَ for those who kafarū كَفَرُوا disbelieve[d] l-ḥayatu الْحَيَوةُ (is) the life l-dun'yā الدُّنْيَا (of) the world wayaskharūna وَيَسْخَرُونَ and they ridicule mina مِنَ [of] alladhīna الَّذِينَ those who āmanū ءَامَنُوا believe[d] wa-alladhīna وَالَّذِينَ And those who ittaqaw اتَّقَوْا fear (Allah) fawqahum فَوْقَهُمْ (they will be) above them yawma يَوْمَ (on the) Day l-qiyāmati الْقِيَامَةِ (of) Resurrection wal-lahu وَاللَّهُ And Allah yarzuqu يَرْزُقُ provides man مَنْ whom yashāu يَشَاءُ He wills bighayri بِغَيْرِ without ḥisābin حِسَابٍ measure

212

212.

Beautified for those who disbelieve is the life of this world, and they ridicule those who believe. But those who fear Allah are above them on the Day of Resurrection. And Allah gives provision to whom He wills without account.

212

kāna كَانَ Was l-nāsu النَّاسُ mankind ummatan أُمَّةً a community wāḥidatan وَاحِدَةً single fabaʿatha فَبَعَثَ then raised up l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah l-nabiyīna النَّبِيِّينَ [the] Prophets mubashirīna مُبَشِّرِينَ (as) bearers of glad tidings wamundhirīna وَمُنْذِرِينَ and (as) warners wa-anzala وَأَنْزَلَ and sent down maʿahumu مَعَهُمُ with them l-kitāba الْكِتَابَ the Book bil-ḥaqi بِالْحَقِّ in [the] truth liyaḥkuma لِيَحْكُمَ to judge bayna بَيْنَ between l-nāsi النَّاسِ [the] people fīmā فِيمَا in what ikh'talafū اخْتَلَفُوا they differed fīhi فِيهِ [in it] wamā وَمَا And (did) not ikh'talafa اخْتَلَفَ differ[ed] fīhi فِيهِ in it illā إِلَّا except alladhīna الَّذِينَ those who ūtūhu أُوتُوهُ were given it min مِنْ from baʿdi بَعْدِ after mā مَا [what] jāathumu جَاءَتْهُمُ came to them l-bayinātu الْبَيِّنَاتُ the clear proofs baghyan بَغْيًا (out of) jealousy baynahum بَيْنَهُمْ among themselves fahadā فَهَدَى And guided l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah alladhīna الَّذِينَ those who āmanū ءَامَنُوا believe[d] limā لِمَا regarding what ikh'talafū اخْتَلَفُوا they differed fīhi فِيهِ [in it] mina مِنَ of l-ḥaqi الْحَقِّ the Truth bi-idh'nihi بِإِذْنِهِ with His permission wal-lahu وَاللَّهُ And Allah yahdī يَهْدِي guides man مَنْ whom yashāu يَشَاءُ He wills ilā إِلَى to ṣirāṭin صِرَاطٍ a path mus'taqīmin مُسْتَقِيمٍ straight

213

213.

Mankind was [of] one religion [before their deviation]; then Allah sent the prophets as bringers of good tidings and warners and sent down with them the Scripture in truth to judge between the people concerning that in which they differed. And none differed over the Scripture except those who were given it - after the clear proofs came to them - out of jealous animosity among themselves. And Allah guided those who believed to the truth concerning that over which they had differed, by His permission. And Allah guides whom He wills to a straight path.

213

am أَمْ Or ḥasib'tum حَسِبْتُمْ (do) you think an أَنْ that tadkhulū تَدْخُلُوا you will enter l-janata الْجَنَّةَ Paradise walammā وَلَمَّا while not yatikum يَأْتِكُمْ (has) come to you mathalu مَثَلُ like (came to) alladhīna الَّذِينَ those who khalaw خَلَوْا passed away min مِنْ from qablikum قَبْلِكُمْ before you massathumu مَسَّتْهُمُ Touched them l-basāu الْبَأْسَاءُ [the] adversity wal-ḍarāu وَالضَّرَّاءُ and [the] hardship wazul'zilū وَزُلْزِلُوا and they were shaken ḥattā حَتَّى until yaqūla يَقُولَ said l-rasūlu الرَّسُولُ the Messenger wa-alladhīna وَالَّذِينَ and those who āmanū ءَامَنُوا believed maʿahu مَعَهُ with him matā مَتَى When naṣru نَصْرُ [will] (the) help l-lahi اللَّهِ (of) Allah (come) alā أَلَا Unquestionably inna إِنَّ [Indeed] naṣra نَصْرَ help l-lahi اللَّهِ (of) Allah qarībun قَرِيبٌ (is) near

214

214.

Or do you think that you will enter Paradise while such [trial] has not yet come to you as came to those who passed on before you? They were touched by poverty and hardship and were shaken until [even their] messenger and those who believed with him said, "When is the help of Allah?" Unquestionably, the help of Allah is near.

214

yasalūnaka يَسْءَلُونَكَ They ask you mādhā مَاذَا what yunfiqūna يُنْفِقُونَ they (should) spend qul قُلْ Say mā مَا Whatever anfaqtum أَنْفَقْتُمْ you spend min مِنْ of khayrin خَيْرٍ good falil'wālidayni فَلِلْوَالِدَيْنِ (is) for parents wal-aqrabīna وَالْأَقْرَبِينَ and the relatives wal-yatāmā وَالْيَتَامَى and the orphans wal-masākīni وَالْمَسَاكِينِ and the needy wa-ib'ni وَابْنِ and (of) l-sabīli السَّبِيلِ the wayfarer wamā وَمَا And whatever tafʿalū تَفْعَلُوا you do min مِنْ of khayrin خَيْرٍ good fa-inna فَإِنَّ So indeed l-laha اللَّهَ Allah bihi بِهِ of it ʿalīmun عَلِيمٌ (is) All-Aware

215

215.

They ask you, [O Muhammad], what they should spend. Say, "Whatever you spend of good is [to be] for parents and relatives and orphans and the needy and the traveler. And whatever you do of good - indeed, Allah is Knowing of it."

215
