kutiba كُتِبَ Is prescribed ʿalaykumu عَلَيْكُمُ upon you l-qitālu الْقِتَالُ [the] fighting wahuwa وَهُوَ while it kur'hun كُرْهٌ (is) hateful lakum لَكُمْ to you waʿasā وَعَسَى But perhaps an أَنْ [that] takrahū تَكْرَهُوا you dislike shayan شَيْئًا a thing wahuwa وَهُوَ and it khayrun خَيْرٌ (is) good lakum لَكُمْ for you waʿasā وَعَسَى and perhaps an أَنْ [that] tuḥibbū تُحِبُّوا you love shayan شَيْئًا a thing wahuwa وَهُوَ and it sharrun شَرٌّ (is) bad lakum لَكُمْ for you wal-lahu وَاللَّهُ And Allah yaʿlamu يَعْلَمُ knows wa-antum وَأَنْتُمْ while you lā لَا (do) not taʿlamūna تَعْلَمُونَ know

216

216.

Fighting has been enjoined upon you while it is hateful to you. But perhaps you hate a thing and it is good for you; and perhaps you love a thing and it is bad for you. And Allah Knows, while you know not.

216

yasalūnaka يَسْءَلُونَكَ They ask you ʿani عَنِ about l-shahri الشَّهْرِ the month l-ḥarāmi الْحَرَامِ [the] sacred qitālin قِتَالٍ (concerning) fighting fīhi فِيهِ in it qul قُلْ Say qitālun قِتَالٌ Fighting fīhi فِيهِ therein kabīrun كَبِيرٌ (is) a great (sin) waṣaddun وَصَدٌّ but hindering (people) ʿan عَنْ from sabīli سَبِيلِ (the) way l-lahi اللَّهِ (of) Allah wakuf'run وَكُفْرٌ and disbelief bihi بِهِ in Him wal-masjidi وَالْمَسْجِدِ and (preventing access to) Al-Masjid l-ḥarāmi الْحَرَامِ Al-Haraam wa-ikh'rāju وَإِخْرَاجُ and driving out ahlihi أَهْلِهِ its people min'hu مِنْهُ from it akbaru أَكْبَرُ (is) greater (sin) ʿinda عِنْدَ near l-lahi اللَّهِ Allah wal-fit'natu وَالْفِتْنَةُ And [the] oppression akbaru أَكْبَرُ (is) greater mina مِنَ than l-qatli الْقَتْلِ [the] killing walā وَلَا And not yazālūna يَزَالُونَ they will cease yuqātilūnakum يُقَاتِلُونَكُمْ (to) fight with you ḥattā حَتَّى until yaruddūkum يَرُدُّوكُمْ they turn you away ʿan عَنْ from dīnikum دِينِكُمْ your religion ini إِنِ if is'taṭāʿū اسْتَطَاعُوا they are able waman وَمَنْ And whoever yartadid يَرْتَدِدْ turns away minkum مِنْكُمْ among you ʿan عَنْ from dīnihi دِينِهِ his religion fayamut فَيَمُتْ then dies wahuwa وَهُوَ while he kāfirun كَافِرٌ (is) a disbeliever fa-ulāika فَأُولَئِكَ for those ḥabiṭat حَبِطَتْ became worthless aʿmāluhum أَعْمَالُهُمْ their deeds fī فِي in l-dun'yā الدُّنْيَا the world wal-ākhirati وَالْءَاخِرَةِ and the Hereafter wa-ulāika وَأُولَئِكَ And those aṣḥābu أَصْحَابُ (are) companions l-nāri النَّارِ (of) the Fire hum هُمْ they fīhā فِيهَا in it khālidūna خَالِدُونَ (will) abide forever

217

217.

They ask you about the sacred month - about fighting therein. Say, "Fighting therein is great [sin], but averting [people] from the way of Allah and disbelief in Him and [preventing access to] al-Masjid al-Haram and the expulsion of its people therefrom are greater [evil] in the sight of Allah. And fitnah is greater than killing." And they will continue to fight you until they turn you back from your religion if they are able. And whoever of you reverts from his religion [to disbelief] and dies while he is a disbeliever - for those, their deeds have become worthless in this world and the Hereafter, and those are the companions of the Fire, they will abide therein eternally.

217

inna إِنَّ Indeed alladhīna الَّذِينَ those who āmanū ءَامَنُوا believed wa-alladhīna وَالَّذِينَ and those who hājarū هَاجَرُوا emigrated wajāhadū وَجَاهَدُوا and strove fī فِي in sabīli سَبِيلِ (the) way l-lahi اللَّهِ (of) Allah ulāika أُولَئِكَ those yarjūna يَرْجُونَ they hope raḥmata رَحْمَتَ (for) Mercy l-lahi اللَّهِ (of) Allah wal-lahu وَاللَّهُ And Allah ghafūrun غَفُورٌ (is) Oft-Forgiving raḥīmun رَحِيمٌ All-Merciful

218

218.

Indeed, those who have believed and those who have emigrated and fought in the cause of Allah - those expect the mercy of Allah. And Allah is Forgiving and Merciful.

218

yasalūnaka يَسْءَلُونَكَ They ask you ʿani عَنِ about l-khamri الْخَمْرِ [the] intoxicants wal-maysiri وَالْمَيْسِرِ and [the] games of chance qul قُلْ Say fīhimā فِيهِمَا In both of them ith'mun إِثْمٌ (is) a sin kabīrun كَبِيرٌ great wamanāfiʿu وَمَنَافِعُ and (some) benefits lilnnāsi لِلنَّاسِ for [the] people wa-ith'muhumā وَإِثْمُهُمَا But sin of both of them akbaru أَكْبَرُ (is) greater min مِنْ than nafʿihimā نَفْعِهِمَا (the) benefit of (the) two wayasalūnaka وَيَسْءَلُونَكَ And they ask you mādhā مَاذَا what yunfiqūna يُنْفِقُونَ they (should) spend quli قُلِ Say l-ʿafwa الْعَفْوَ The surplus kadhālika كَذَلِكَ Thus yubayyinu يُبَيِّنُ makes clear l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah lakumu لَكُمُ to you l-āyāti الْءَايَاتِ [the] Verses laʿallakum لَعَلَّكُمْ so that you may tatafakkarūna تَتَفَكَّرُونَ ponder

219

219.

They ask you about wine and gambling. Say, "In them is great sin and [yet, some] benefit for people. But their sin is greater than their benefit." And they ask you what they should spend. Say, "The excess [beyond needs]." Thus Allah makes clear to you the verses [of revelation] that you might give thought.

219

fī فِي Concerning l-dun'yā الدُّنْيَا the world wal-ākhirati وَالْءَاخِرَةِ and the Hereafter wayasalūnaka وَيَسْءَلُونَكَ They ask you ʿani عَنِ about l-yatāmā الْيَتَامَى the orphans qul قُلْ Say iṣ'lāḥun إِصْلَاحٌ Setting right (their affairs) lahum لَهُمْ for them khayrun خَيْرٌ (is) best wa-in وَإِنْ And if tukhāliṭūhum تُخَالِطُوهُمْ you associate with them fa-ikh'wānukum فَإِخْوَانُكُمْ then they (are) your brothers wal-lahu وَاللَّهُ And Allah yaʿlamu يَعْلَمُ knows l-muf'sida الْمُفْسِدَ the corrupter mina مِنَ from l-muṣ'liḥi الْمُصْلِحِ the amender walaw وَلَوْ And if shāa شَاءَ (had) willed l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah la-aʿnatakum لَأَعْنَتَكُمْ surely He (could have) put you in difficulties inna إِنَّ Indeed l-laha اللَّهَ Allah ʿazīzun عَزِيزٌ (is) All-Mighty ḥakīmun حَكِيمٌ All-Wise

220

220.

To this world and the Hereafter. And they ask you about orphans. Say, "Improvement for them is best. And if you mix your affairs with theirs - they are your brothers. And Allah knows the corrupter from the amender. And if Allah had willed, He could have put you in difficulty. Indeed, Allah is Exalted in Might and Wise.

220

walā وَلَا And (do) not tankiḥū تَنْكِحُوا [you] marry l-mush'rikāti الْمُشْرِكَاتِ [the] polytheistic women ḥattā حَتَّى until yu'minna يُؤْمِنَّ they believe wala-amatun وَلَأَمَةٌ And a bondwoman mu'minatun مُؤْمِنَةٌ (who is) believing khayrun خَيْرٌ (is) better min مِنْ than mush'rikatin مُشْرِكَةٍ a polytheistic woman walaw وَلَوْ [and] even if aʿjabatkum أَعْجَبَتْكُمْ she pleases you walā وَلَا And (do) not tunkiḥū تُنْكِحُوا give in marriage (your women) l-mush'rikīna الْمُشْرِكِينَ (to) [the] polytheistic men ḥattā حَتَّى until yu'minū يُؤْمِنُوا they believe walaʿabdun وَلَعَبْدٌ and a bondman mu'minun مُؤْمِنٌ (who is) believing khayrun خَيْرٌ (is) better min مِنْ than mush'rikin مُشْرِكٍ a polytheistic man walaw وَلَوْ [and] even if aʿjabakum أَعْجَبَكُمْ he pleases you ulāika أُولَئِكَ [Those] yadʿūna يَدْعُونَ they invite ilā إِلَى to l-nāri النَّارِ the Fire wal-lahu وَاللَّهُ and Allah yadʿū يَدْعُوا invites ilā إِلَى to l-janati الْجَنَّةِ Paradise wal-maghfirati وَالْمَغْفِرَةِ and [the] forgiveness bi-idh'nihi بِإِذْنِهِ by His permission wayubayyinu وَيُبَيِّنُ And He makes clear āyātihi ءَايَاتِهِ His Verses lilnnāsi لِلنَّاسِ for the people laʿallahum لَعَلَّهُمْ so that they may yatadhakkarūna يَتَذَكَّرُونَ take heed

221

221.

And do not marry polytheistic women until they believe. And a believing slave woman is better than a polytheist, even though she might please you. And do not marry polytheistic men [to your women] until they believe. And a believing slave is better than a polytheist, even though he might please you. Those invite [you] to the Fire, but Allah invites to Paradise and to forgiveness, by His permission. And He makes clear His verses to the people that perhaps they may remember.

221

wayasalūnaka وَيَسْءَلُونَكَ And they ask you ʿani عَنِ about l-maḥīḍi الْمَحِيضِ [the] menstruation qul قُلْ Say huwa هُوَ It adhan أَذًى (is) a hurt fa-iʿ'tazilū فَاعْتَزِلُوا so keep away (from) l-nisāa النِّسَاءَ [the] women fī فِي during l-maḥīḍi الْمَحِيضِ (their) [the] menstruation walā وَلَا And (do) not taqrabūhunna تَقْرَبُوهُنَّ approach them ḥattā حَتَّى until yaṭhur'na يَطْهُرْنَ they are cleansed fa-idhā فَإِذَا Then when taṭahharna تَطَهَّرْنَ they are purified fatūhunna فَأْتُوهُنَّ then come to them min مِنْ from ḥaythu حَيْثُ where amarakumu أَمَرَكُمُ has ordered you l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah inna إِنَّ Indeed l-laha اللَّهَ Allah yuḥibbu يُحِبُّ loves l-tawābīna التَّوَّابِينَ those who turn in repentance wayuḥibbu وَيُحِبُّ and loves l-mutaṭahirīna الْمُتَطَهِّرِينَ those who purify themselves

222

222.

And they ask you about menstruation. Say, "It is harm, so keep away from wives during menstruation. And do not approach them until they are pure. And when they have purified themselves, then come to them from where Allah has ordained for you. Indeed, Allah loves those who are constantly repentant and loves those who purify themselves."

222

nisāukum نِسَاؤُكُمْ Your wives ḥarthun حَرْثٌ (are) a tilth lakum لَكُمْ for you fatū فَأْتُوا so come ḥarthakum حَرْثَكُمْ (to) your tilth annā أَنَّى when shi'tum شِئْتُمْ you wish waqaddimū وَقَدِّمُوا and send forth (good deeds) li-anfusikum لِأَنْفُسِكُمْ for yourselves wa-ittaqū وَاتَّقُوا And be conscious l-laha اللَّهَ (of) Allah wa-iʿ'lamū وَاعْلَمُوا and know annakum أَنَّكُمْ that you mulāqūhu مُلَاقُوهُ (will) meet Him wabashiri وَبَشِّرِ And give glad tidings l-mu'minīna الْمُؤْمِنِينَ (to) the believers

223

223.

Your wives are a place of sowing of seed for you, so come to your place of cultivation however you wish and put forth [righteousness] for yourselves. And fear Allah and know that you will meet Him. And give good tidings to the believers.

223

walā وَلَا And (do) not tajʿalū تَجْعَلُوا make l-laha اللَّهَ Allahs (name) ʿur'ḍatan عُرْضَةً an excuse li-aymānikum لِأَيْمَانِكُمْ in your oaths an أَنْ that tabarrū تَبَرُّوا you do good watattaqū وَتَتَّقُوا and be righteous watuṣ'liḥū وَتُصْلِحُوا and make peace bayna بَيْنَ between l-nāsi النَّاسِ [the] people wal-lahu وَاللَّهُ And Allah samīʿun سَمِيعٌ (is) All-Hearing ʿalīmun عَلِيمٌ All-Knowing

224

224.

And do not make [your oath by] Allah an excuse against being righteous and fearing Allah and making peace among people. And Allah is Hearing and Knowing.

224

lā لَا Not yuākhidhukumu يُؤَاخِذُكُمُ will take you to task l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah bil-laghwi بِاللَّغْوِ for (what is) unintentional fī فِي in aymānikum أَيْمَانِكُمْ your oaths walākin وَلَكِنْ [and] but yuākhidhukum يُؤَاخِذُكُمْ He takes you to task bimā بِمَا for what kasabat كَسَبَتْ (have) earned qulūbukum قُلُوبُكُمْ your hearts wal-lahu وَاللَّهُ And Allah ghafūrun غَفُورٌ (is) Oft-Forgiving ḥalīmun حَلِيمٌ Most Forbearing

225

225.

Allah does not impose blame upon you for what is unintentional in your oaths, but He imposes blame upon you for what your hearts have earned. And Allah is Forgiving and Forbearing.

225

lilladhīna لِلَّذِينَ For those who yu'lūna يُؤْلُونَ swear (off) min مِنْ from nisāihim نِسَائِهِمْ their wives tarabbuṣu تَرَبُّصُ (is a) waiting (of) arbaʿati أَرْبَعَةِ four ashhurin أَشْهُرٍ months fa-in فَإِنْ then if fāū فَاءُو they return fa-inna فَإِنَّ then indeed l-laha اللَّهَ Allah ghafūrun غَفُورٌ (is) Oft- Forgiving raḥīmun رَحِيمٌ Most Merciful

226

226.

For those who swear not to have sexual relations with their wives is a waiting time of four months, but if they return [to normal relations] - then indeed, Allah is Forgiving and Merciful.

226

wa-in وَإِنْ And if ʿazamū عَزَمُوا they resolve l-ṭalāqa الطَّلَاقَ (on) [the] divorce fa-inna فَإِنَّ then indeed l-laha اللَّهَ Allah samīʿun سَمِيعٌ (is) All-Hearing ʿalīmun عَلِيمٌ All-Knowing

227

227.

And if they decide on divorce - then indeed, Allah is Hearing and Knowing.

227

wal-muṭalaqātu وَالْمُطَلَّقَاتُ And the women who are divorced yatarabbaṣna يَتَرَبَّصْنَ shall wait bi-anfusihinna بِأَنْفُسِهِنَّ concerning themselves thalāthata ثَلَاثَةَ (for) three qurūin قُرُوءٍ monthly periods walā وَلَا And (it is) not yaḥillu يَحِلُّ lawful lahunna لَهُنَّ for them an أَنْ that yaktum'na يَكْتُمْنَ they conceal mā مَا what khalaqa خَلَقَ (has been) created l-lahu اللَّهُ (by) Allah fī فِي in arḥāmihinna أَرْحَامِهِنَّ their wombs in إِنْ if kunna كُنَّ they yu'minna يُؤْمِنَّ believe bil-lahi بِاللَّهِ in Allah wal-yawmi وَالْيَوْمِ and the Day l-ākhiri الْءَاخِرِ [the] Last wabuʿūlatuhunna وَبُعُولَتُهُنَّ And their husbands aḥaqqu أَحَقُّ (have) better right biraddihinna بِرَدِّهِنَّ to take them back fī فِي in dhālika ذَلِكَ that (period) in إِنْ if arādū أَرَادُوا they wish iṣ'lāḥan إِصْلَاحًا (for) reconciliation walahunna وَلَهُنَّ And for them (wives) mith'lu مِثْلُ (is the) like alladhī الَّذِي (of) that which ʿalayhinna عَلَيْهِنَّ (is) on them bil-maʿrūfi بِالْمَعْرُوفِ in a reasonable manner walilrrijāli وَلِلرِّجَالِ and for the men ʿalayhinna عَلَيْهِنَّ over them (wives) darajatun دَرَجَةٌ (is) a degree wal-lahu وَاللَّهُ And Allah ʿazīzun عَزِيزٌ (is) All-Mighty ḥakīmun حَكِيمٌ All-Wise

228

228.

Divorced women remain in waiting for three periods, and it is not lawful for them to conceal what Allah has created in their wombs if they believe in Allah and the Last Day. And their husbands have more right to take them back in this [period] if they want reconciliation. And due to the wives is similar to what is expected of them, according to what is reasonable. But the men have a degree over them [in responsibility and authority]. And Allah is Exalted in Might and Wise.

228

al-ṭalāqu الطَّلَاقُ The divorce marratāni مَرَّتَانِ (is) twice fa-im'sākun فَإِمْسَاكٌ Then to retain bimaʿrūfin بِمَعْرُوفٍ in a reasonable manner aw أَوْ or tasrīḥun تَسْرِيحٌ to release (her) bi-iḥ'sānin بِإِحْسَانٍ with kindness walā وَلَا And (it is) not yaḥillu يَحِلُّ lawful lakum لَكُمْ for you an أَنْ that takhudhū تَأْخُذُوا you take (back) mimmā مِمَّا whatever ātaytumūhunna ءَاتَيْتُمُوهُنَّ you have given them (wives) shayan شَيْئًا anything illā إِلَّا except an أَنْ if yakhāfā يَخَافَا both fear allā أَلَّا that not yuqīmā يُقِيمَا they both (can) keep ḥudūda حُدُودَ (the) limits l-lahi اللَّهِ (of) Allah fa-in فَإِنْ But if khif'tum خِفْتُمْ you fear allā أَلَّا that not yuqīmā يُقِيمَا they both (can) keep ḥudūda حُدُودَ (the) limits l-lahi اللَّهِ (of) Allah falā فَلَا then (there is) no junāḥa جُنَاحَ sin ʿalayhimā عَلَيْهِمَا on both of them fīmā فِيمَا in what if'tadat افْتَدَتْ she ransoms bihi بِهِ concerning it til'ka تِلْكَ These ḥudūdu حُدُودُ (are the) limits l-lahi اللَّهِ (of) Allah falā فَلَا so (do) not taʿtadūhā تَعْتَدُوهَا transgress them waman وَمَنْ And whoever yataʿadda يَتَعَدَّ transgresses ḥudūda حُدُودَ (the) limits l-lahi اللَّهِ (of) Allah fa-ulāika فَأُولَئِكَ then those humu هُمُ they l-ẓālimūna الظَّالِمُونَ (are) the wrongdoers

229

229.

Divorce is twice. Then, either keep [her] in an acceptable manner or release [her] with good treatment. And it is not lawful for you to take anything of what you have given them unless both fear that they will not be able to keep [within] the limits of Allah. But if you fear that they will not keep [within] the limits of Allah, then there is no blame upon either of them concerning that by which she ransoms herself. These are the limits of Allah, so do not transgress them. And whoever transgresses the limits of Allah - it is those who are the wrongdoers.

229

fa-in فَإِنْ Then if ṭallaqahā طَلَّقَهَا he divorces her (finally) falā فَلَا then (she is) not taḥillu تَحِلُّ lawful lahu لَهُ for him min مِنْ from baʿdu بَعْدُ after (that) ḥattā حَتَّى until tankiḥa تَنْكِحَ she marries zawjan زَوْجًا a spouse ghayrahu غَيْرَهُ other than him fa-in فَإِنْ Then if ṭallaqahā طَلَّقَهَا he divorces her falā فَلَا then no junāḥa جُنَاحَ sin ʿalayhimā عَلَيْهِمَا on them an أَنْ if yatarājaʿā يَتَرَاجَعَا they return to each other in إِنْ if ẓannā ظَنَّا they believe an أَنْ that yuqīmā يُقِيمَا they (will be able to) keep ḥudūda حُدُودَ (the) limits l-lahi اللَّهِ (of) Allah watil'ka وَتِلْكَ And these ḥudūdu حُدُودُ (are the) limits l-lahi اللَّهِ (of) Allah yubayyinuhā يُبَيِّنُهَا He makes them clear liqawmin لِقَوْمٍ to a people yaʿlamūna يَعْلَمُونَ who know

230

230.

And if he has divorced her [for the third time], then she is not lawful to him afterward until [after] she marries a husband other than him. And if the latter husband divorces her [or dies], there is no blame upon the woman and her former husband for returning to each other if they think that they can keep [within] the limits of Allah. These are the limits of Allah, which He makes clear to a people who know.

230

wa-idhā وَإِذَا And when ṭallaqtumu طَلَّقْتُمُ you divorce l-nisāa النِّسَاءَ the women fabalaghna فَبَلَغْنَ and they reach ajalahunna أَجَلَهُنَّ their (waiting) term fa-amsikūhunna فَأَمْسِكُوهُنَّ then retain them bimaʿrūfin بِمَعْرُوفٍ in a fair manner aw أَوْ or sarriḥūhunna سَرِّحُوهُنَّ release them bimaʿrūfin بِمَعْرُوفٍ in a fair manner walā وَلَا And (do) not tum'sikūhunna تُمْسِكُوهُنَّ retain them ḍirāran ضِرَارًا (to) hurt litaʿtadū لِتَعْتَدُوا so that you transgress waman وَمَنْ And whoever yafʿal يَفْعَلْ does dhālika ذَلِكَ that faqad فَقَدْ then indeed ẓalama ظَلَمَ he wronged nafsahu نَفْسَهُ himself walā وَلَا And (do) not tattakhidhū تَتَّخِذُوا take āyāti ءَايَاتِ (the) Verses l-lahi اللَّهِ (of) Allah huzuwan هُزُوًا (in) jest wa-udh'kurū وَاذْكُرُوا and remember niʿ'mata نِعْمَتَ (the) Favors l-lahi اللَّهِ (of) Allah ʿalaykum عَلَيْكُمْ upon you wamā وَمَا and what anzala أَنْزَلَ (is) revealed ʿalaykum عَلَيْكُمْ to you mina مِنَ of l-kitābi الْكِتَابِ the Book wal-ḥik'mati وَالْحِكْمَةِ and the wisdom yaʿiẓukum يَعِظُكُمْ He instructs you bihi بِهِ with it wa-ittaqū وَاتَّقُوا And fear l-laha اللَّهَ Allah wa-iʿ'lamū وَاعْلَمُوا and know anna أَنَّ that l-laha اللَّهَ Allah (is) bikulli بِكُلِّ of every shayin شَيْءٍ thing ʿalīmun عَلِيمٌ All-Knower

231

231.

And when you divorce women and they have [nearly] fulfilled their term, either retain them according to acceptable terms or release them according to acceptable terms, and do not keep them, intending harm, to transgress [against them]. And whoever does that has certainly wronged himself. And do not take the verses of Allah in jest. And remember the favor of Allah upon you and what has been revealed to you of the Book and wisdom by which He instructs you. And fear Allah and know that Allah is Knowing of all things.

231

wa-idhā وَإِذَا And when ṭallaqtumu طَلَّقْتُمُ you divorce l-nisāa النِّسَاءَ [the] women fabalaghna فَبَلَغْنَ and they reached ajalahunna أَجَلَهُنَّ their (waiting) term falā فَلَا then (do) not taʿḍulūhunna تَعْضُلُوهُنَّ hinder them an أَنْ [that] yankiḥ'na يَنْكِحْنَ (from) marrying azwājahunna أَزْوَاجَهُنَّ their husbands idhā إِذَا when tarāḍaw تَرَاضَوْا they agree baynahum بَيْنَهُمْ between themselves bil-maʿrūfi بِالْمَعْرُوفِ in a fair manner dhālika ذَلِكَ That yūʿaẓu يُوعَظُ is admonished bihi بِهِ with it man مَنْ whoever kāna كَانَ [is] minkum مِنْكُمْ among you yu'minu يُؤْمِنُ believes bil-lahi بِاللَّهِ in Allah wal-yawmi وَالْيَوْمِ and the Day l-ākhiri الْءَاخِرِ [the] Last dhālikum ذَلِكُمْ that azkā أَزْكَى (is) more virtuous lakum لَكُمْ for you wa-aṭharu وَأَطْهَرُ and more purer wal-lahu وَاللَّهُ And Allah yaʿlamu يَعْلَمُ knows wa-antum وَأَنْتُمْ and you lā لَا (do) not taʿlamūna تَعْلَمُونَ know

232

232.

And when you divorce women and they have fulfilled their term, do not prevent them from remarrying their [former] husbands if they agree among themselves on an acceptable basis. That is instructed to whoever of you believes in Allah and the Last Day. That is better for you and purer, and Allah knows and you know not.

232

wal-wālidātu وَالْوَالِدَاتُ And the mothers yur'ḍiʿ'na يُرْضِعْنَ shall suckle awlādahunna أَوْلَادَهُنَّ their children ḥawlayni حَوْلَيْنِ (for) two years kāmilayni كَامِلَيْنِ complete liman لِمَنْ for whoever arāda أَرَادَ wishes an أَنْ to yutimma يُتِمَّ complete l-raḍāʿata الرَّضَاعَةَ the suckling waʿalā وَعَلَى And upon l-mawlūdi الْمَوْلُودِ the father lahu لَهُ (on) him riz'quhunna رِزْقُهُنَّ (is) their provision wakis'watuhunna وَكِسْوَتُهُنَّ and their clothing bil-maʿrūfi بِالْمَعْرُوفِ in a fair manner lā لَا Not tukallafu تُكَلَّفُ is burdened nafsun نَفْسٌ any soul illā إِلَّا except wus'ʿahā وُسْعَهَا its capacity lā لَا Not tuḍārra تُضَارَّ made to suffer wālidatun وَالِدَةٌ (the) mother biwaladihā بِوَلَدِهَا because of her child walā وَلَا and not mawlūdun مَوْلُودٌ (the) father lahu لَهُ (be) biwaladihi بِوَلَدِهِ because of his child waʿalā وَعَلَى And on l-wārithi الْوَارِثِ the heirs mith'lu مِثْلُ (is a duty) like dhālika ذَلِكَ that fa-in فَإِنْ Then if arādā أَرَادَا they both desire fiṣālan فِصَالًا weaning ʿan عَنْ through tarāḍin تَرَاضٍ mutual consent min'humā مِنْهُمَا of both of them watashāwurin وَتَشَاوُرٍ and consultation falā فَلَا then no junāḥa جُنَاحَ blame ʿalayhimā عَلَيْهِمَا on both of them wa-in وَإِنْ And if aradttum أَرَدْتُمْ you want an أَنْ to tastarḍiʿū تَسْتَرْضِعُوا ask another women to suckle awlādakum أَوْلَادَكُمْ your child falā فَلَا then (there is) no junāḥa جُنَاحَ blame ʿalaykum عَلَيْكُمْ on you idhā إِذَا when sallamtum سَلَّمْتُمْ you pay mā مَا what ātaytum ءَاتَيْتُمْ (is) due (from) you bil-maʿrūfi بِالْمَعْرُوفِ in a fair manner wa-ittaqū وَاتَّقُوا And fear l-laha اللَّهَ Allah wa-iʿ'lamū وَاعْلَمُوا and know anna أَنَّ that l-laha اللَّهَ Allah bimā بِمَا of what taʿmalūna تَعْمَلُونَ you do baṣīrun بَصِيرٌ (is) All-Seer

233

233.

Mothers may breastfeed their children two complete years for whoever wishes to complete the nursing [period]. Upon the father is the mothers' provision and their clothing according to what is acceptable. No person is charged with more than his capacity. No mother should be harmed through her child, and no father through his child. And upon the [father's] heir is [a duty] like that [of the father]. And if they both desire weaning through mutual consent from both of them and consultation, there is no blame upon either of them. And if you wish to have your children nursed by a substitute, there is no blame upon you as long as you give payment according to what is acceptable. And fear Allah and know that Allah is Seeing of what you do.

233

wa-alladhīna وَالَّذِينَ And those who yutawaffawna يُتَوَفَّوْنَ pass away minkum مِنْكُمْ among you wayadharūna وَيَذَرُونَ and leave behind azwājan أَزْوَاجًا wives yatarabbaṣna يَتَرَبَّصْنَ (the widows) should wait bi-anfusihinna بِأَنْفُسِهِنَّ for themselves arbaʿata أَرْبَعَةَ (for) four ashhurin أَشْهُرٍ months waʿashran وَعَشْرًا and ten (days) fa-idhā فَإِذَا Then when balaghna بَلَغْنَ they reach ajalahunna أَجَلَهُنَّ their (specified) term falā فَلَا then (there is) no junāḥa جُنَاحَ blame ʿalaykum عَلَيْكُمْ upon you fīmā فِيمَا for what faʿalna فَعَلْنَ they do fī فِي concerning anfusihinna أَنْفُسِهِنَّ themselves bil-maʿrūfi بِالْمَعْرُوفِ in a fair manner wal-lahu وَاللَّهُ And Allah bimā بِمَا of what taʿmalūna تَعْمَلُونَ you do khabīrun خَبِيرٌ (is) All-Aware

234

234.

And those who are taken in death among you and leave wives behind - they, [the wives, shall] wait four months and ten [days]. And when they have fulfilled their term, then there is no blame upon you for what they do with themselves in an acceptable manner. And Allah is [fully] Acquainted with what you do.

234

walā وَلَا And (there is) no junāḥa جُنَاحَ blame ʿalaykum عَلَيْكُمْ upon you fīmā فِيمَا in what ʿarraḍtum عَرَّضْتُمْ you hint bihi بِهِ [with it] min مِنْ of khiṭ'bati خِطْبَةِ marriage proposal l-nisāi النِّسَاءِ [to] the women aw أَوْ or aknantum أَكْنَنْتُمْ you concealed it fī فِي in anfusikum أَنْفُسِكُمْ yourselves ʿalima عَلِمَ Knows l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah annakum أَنَّكُمْ that you satadhkurūnahunna سَتَذْكُرُونَهُنَّ will mention them walākin وَلَكِنْ [and] but lā لَا (do) not tuwāʿidūhunna تُوَاعِدُوهُنَّ promise them (widows) sirran سِرًّا secretly illā إِلَّا except an أَنْ that taqūlū تَقُولُوا you say qawlan قَوْلًا a saying maʿrūfan مَعْرُوفًا honorable walā وَلَا And (do) not taʿzimū تَعْزِمُوا resolve (on) ʿuq'data عُقْدَةَ the knot l-nikāḥi النِّكَاحِ (of) marriage ḥattā حَتَّى until yablugha يَبْلُغَ reaches l-kitābu الْكِتَابُ the prescribed term ajalahu أَجَلَهُ its end wa-iʿ'lamū وَاعْلَمُوا And know anna أَنَّ that l-laha اللَّهَ Allah yaʿlamu يَعْلَمُ knows mā مَا what fī فِي (is) within anfusikum أَنْفُسِكُمْ yourselves fa-iḥ'dharūhu فَاحْذَرُوهُ so beware of Him wa-iʿ'lamū وَاعْلَمُوا And know anna أَنَّ that l-laha اللَّهَ Allah ghafūrun غَفُورٌ (is) Oft-Forgiving ḥalīmun حَلِيمٌ Most Forbearing

235

235.

There is no blame upon you for that to which you [indirectly] allude concerning a proposal to women or for what you conceal within yourselves. Allah knows that you will have them in mind. But do not promise them secretly except for saying a proper saying. And do not determine to undertake a marriage contract until the decreed period reaches its end. And know that Allah knows what is within yourselves, so beware of Him. And know that Allah is Forgiving and Forbearing.

235

lā لَا (There is) no junāḥa جُنَاحَ blame ʿalaykum عَلَيْكُمْ upon you in إِنْ if ṭallaqtumu طَلَّقْتُمُ you divorce l-nisāa النِّسَاءَ [the] women mā مَا whom lam لَمْ not tamassūhunna تَمَسُّوهُنَّ you have touched aw أَوْ nor tafriḍū تَفْرِضُوا you specified lahunna لَهُنَّ for them farīḍatan فَرِيضَةً an obligation (dower) wamattiʿūhunna وَمَتِّعُوهُنَّ And make provision for them ʿalā عَلَى upon l-mūsiʿi الْمُوسِعِ the wealthy qadaruhu قَدَرُهُ according to his means waʿalā وَعَلَى and upon l-muq'tiri الْمُقْتِرِ the poor qadaruhu قَدَرُهُ according to his means matāʿan مَتَاعًا a provision bil-maʿrūfi بِالْمَعْرُوفِ in a fair manner ḥaqqan حَقًّا a duty ʿalā عَلَى upon l-muḥ'sinīna الْمُحْسِنِينَ the good-doers

236

236.

There is no blame upon you if you divorce women you have not touched nor specified for them an obligation. But give them [a gift of] compensation - the wealthy according to his capability and the poor according to his capability - a provision according to what is acceptable, a duty upon the doers of good.

236

wa-in وَإِنْ And if ṭallaqtumūhunna طَلَّقْتُمُوهُنَّ you divorce them min مِنْ from qabli قَبْلِ before an أَنْ [that] tamassūhunna تَمَسُّوهُنَّ you (have) touched them waqad وَقَدْ while already faraḍtum فَرَضْتُمْ you have specified lahunna لَهُنَّ for them farīḍatan فَرِيضَةً an obligation (dower) faniṣ'fu فَنِصْفُ then (give) half mā مَا (of) what faraḍtum فَرَضْتُمْ you have specified illā إِلَّا unless an أَنْ [that] yaʿfūna يَعْفُونَ they (women) forgo (it) aw أَوْ or yaʿfuwā يَعْفُوَا forgoes alladhī الَّذِي the one biyadihi بِيَدِهِ in whose hands ʿuq'datu عُقْدَةُ (is the) knot l-nikāḥi النِّكَاحِ (of) the marriage wa-an وَأَنْ And that taʿfū تَعْفُوا you forgo aqrabu أَقْرَبُ (is) nearer lilttaqwā لِلتَّقْوَى to [the] righteousness walā وَلَا And (do) not tansawū تَنْسَوُا forget l-faḍla الْفَضْلَ the graciousness baynakum بَيْنَكُمْ among you inna إِنَّ Indeed l-laha اللَّهَ Allah bimā بِمَا of what taʿmalūna تَعْمَلُونَ you do baṣīrun بَصِيرٌ (is) All-Seer

237

237.

And if you divorce them before you have touched them and you have already specified for them an obligation, then [give] half of what you specified - unless they forego the right or the one in whose hand is the marriage contract foregoes it. And to forego it is nearer to righteousness. And do not forget graciousness between you. Indeed Allah, of whatever you do, is Seeing.

237

ḥāfiẓū حَافِظُوا Guard strictly ʿalā عَلَى [on] l-ṣalawāti الصَّلَوَاتِ the prayers wal-ṣalati وَالصَّلَوةِ and the prayer l-wus'ṭā الْوُسْطَى [the] middle waqūmū وَقُومُوا and stand up lillahi لِلَّهِ for Allah qānitīna قَانِتِينَ devoutly obedient

238

238.

Maintain with care the [obligatory] prayers and [in particular] the middle prayer and stand before Allah, devoutly obedient.

238

fa-in فَإِنْ And if khif'tum خِفْتُمْ you fear farijālan فَرِجَالًا then (pray) on foot aw أَوْ or ruk'bānan رُكْبَانًا riding fa-idhā فَإِذَا Then when amintum أَمِنْتُمْ you are secure fa-udh'kurū فَاذْكُرُوا then remember l-laha اللَّهَ Allah kamā كَمَا as ʿallamakum عَلَّمَكُمْ He (has) taught you mā مَا what lam لَمْ not takūnū تَكُونُوا you were taʿlamūna تَعْلَمُونَ knowing

239

239.

And if you fear [an enemy, then pray] on foot or riding. But when you are secure, then remember Allah [in prayer], as He has taught you that which you did not [previously] know.

239

wa-alladhīna وَالَّذِينَ And those who yutawaffawna يُتَوَفَّوْنَ they die minkum مِنْكُمْ among you wayadharūna وَيَذَرُونَ and leave behind azwājan أَزْوَاجًا (their) wives waṣiyyatan وَصِيَّةً (should make) a will li-azwājihim لِأَزْوَاجِهِمْ for their wives matāʿan مَتَاعًا provision ilā إِلَى for l-ḥawli الْحَوْلِ the year ghayra غَيْرَ without ikh'rājin إِخْرَاجٍ driving (them) out fa-in فَإِنْ But if kharajna خَرَجْنَ they leave falā فَلَا then no junāḥa جُنَاحَ blame ʿalaykum عَلَيْكُمْ upon you fī فِي in mā مَا what faʿalna فَعَلْنَ they do fī فِي concerning anfusihinna أَنْفُسِهِنَّ themselves min مِنْ [of] maʿrūfin مَعْرُوفٍ honorably wal-lahu وَاللَّهُ And Allah ʿazīzun عَزِيزٌ (is) All-Mighty ḥakīmun حَكِيمٌ All-Wise

240

240.

And those who are taken in death among you and leave wives behind - for their wives is a bequest: maintenance for one year without turning [them] out. But if they leave [of their own accord], then there is no blame upon you for what they do with themselves in an acceptable way. And Allah is Exalted in Might and Wise.

240

walil'muṭallaqāti وَلِلْمُطَلَّقَاتِ And for the divorced women matāʿun مَتَاعٌ (is) a provision bil-maʿrūfi بِالْمَعْرُوفِ in a fair manner ḥaqqan حَقًّا a duty ʿalā عَلَى upon l-mutaqīna الْمُتَّقِينَ the righteous

241

241.

And for divorced women is a provision according to what is acceptable - a duty upon the righteous.

241

kadhālika كَذَلِكَ Thus yubayyinu يُبَيِّنُ makes clear l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah lakum لَكُمْ for you āyātihi ءَايَاتِهِ His Verses laʿallakum لَعَلَّكُمْ so that you may taʿqilūna تَعْقِلُونَ use your intellect

242

242.

Thus does Allah make clear to you His verses that you might use reason.

242

alam أَلَمْ Did not tara تَرَ you see ilā إِلَى [to] alladhīna الَّذِينَ those who kharajū خَرَجُوا went out min مِنْ from diyārihim دِيَارِهِمْ their homes wahum وَهُمْ and they ulūfun أُلُوفٌ (were in) thousands ḥadhara حَذَرَ (in) fear l-mawti الْمَوْتِ (of) [the] death faqāla فَقَالَ Then said lahumu لَهُمُ to them l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah mūtū مُوتُوا Die thumma ثُمَّ then aḥyāhum أَحْيَاهُمْ He restored them to life inna إِنَّ Indeed l-laha اللَّهَ Allah ladhū لَذُو (is) surely Possessor faḍlin فَضْلٍ (of) bounty ʿalā عَلَى for l-nāsi النَّاسِ [the] mankind walākinna وَلَكِنَّ [and] but akthara أَكْثَرَ most l-nāsi النَّاسِ (of) the people lā لَا (are) not yashkurūna يَشْكُرُونَ grateful

243

243.

Have you not considered those who left their homes in many thousands, fearing death? Allah said to them, "Die"; then He restored them to life. And Allah is full of bounty to the people, but most of the people do not show gratitude.

243

waqātilū وَقَاتِلُوا And fight fī فِي in sabīli سَبِيلِ (the) way l-lahi اللَّهِ (of) Allah wa-iʿ'lamū وَاعْلَمُوا and know anna أَنَّ that l-laha اللَّهَ Allah samīʿun سَمِيعٌ (is) All-Hearing ʿalīmun عَلِيمٌ All-Knowing

244

244.

And fight in the cause of Allah and know that Allah is Hearing and Knowing.

244

man مَنْ Who dhā ذَا (is) the one alladhī الَّذِي who yuq'riḍu يُقْرِضُ will lend l-laha اللَّهَ (to) Allah qarḍan قَرْضًا a loan ḥasanan حَسَنًا good fayuḍāʿifahu فَيُضَاعِفَهُ so (that) He multiplies it lahu لَهُ for him aḍʿāfan أَضْعَافًا manifolds kathīratan كَثِيرَةً many wal-lahu وَاللَّهُ And Allah yaqbiḍu يَقْبِضُ withholds wayabṣuṭu وَيَبْصُطُ and grants abundance wa-ilayhi وَإِلَيْهِ and to Him tur'jaʿūna تُرْجَعُونَ you will be returned

245

245.

Who is it that would loan Allah a goodly loan so He may multiply it for him many times over? And it is Allah who withholds and grants abundance, and to Him you will be returned.

245

alam أَلَمْ Did not tara تَرَ you see ilā إِلَى [towards] l-mala-i الْمَلَإِ the chiefs min مِنْ of banī بَنِي (the) Children is'rāīla إِسْرَاءِيلَ (of) Israel min مِنْ from baʿdi بَعْدِ after mūsā مُوسَى Musa idh إِذْ when qālū قَالُوا they said linabiyyin لِنَبِيٍّ to a Prophet lahumu لَهُمُ of theirs ib'ʿath ابْعَثْ Appoint lanā لَنَا for us malikan مَلِكًا a king nuqātil نُقَاتِلْ we may fight fī فِي in sabīli سَبِيلِ (the) way l-lahi اللَّهِ (of) Allah qāla قَالَ He said hal هَلْ Would ʿasaytum عَسَيْتُمْ you perhaps in إِنْ if kutiba كُتِبَ prescribed ʿalaykumu عَلَيْكُمُ upon you l-qitālu الْقِتَالُ [the] fighting allā أَلَّا that not tuqātilū تُقَاتِلُوا you fight qālū قَالُوا They said wamā وَمَا And what lanā لَنَا for us allā أَلَّا that not nuqātila نُقَاتِلَ we fight fī فِي in sabīli سَبِيلِ (the) way l-lahi اللَّهِ (of) Allah waqad وَقَدْ while surely ukh'rij'nā أُخْرِجْنَا we have been driven out min مِنْ from diyārinā دِيَارِنَا our homes wa-abnāinā وَأَبْنَائِنَا and our children falammā فَلَمَّا Yet, when kutiba كُتِبَ was prescribed ʿalayhimu عَلَيْهِمُ upon them l-qitālu الْقِتَالُ the fighting tawallaw تَوَلَّوْا they turned away illā إِلَّا except qalīlan قَلِيلًا a few min'hum مِنْهُمْ among them wal-lahu وَاللَّهُ And Allah ʿalīmun عَلِيمٌ (is) All-Knowing bil-ẓālimīna بِالظَّالِمِينَ of the wrongdoers

246

246.

Have you not considered the assembly of the Children of Israel after [the time of] Moses when they said to a prophet of theirs, "Send to us a king, and we will fight in the way of Allah "? He said, "Would you perhaps refrain from fighting if fighting was prescribed for you?" They said, "And why should we not fight in the cause of Allah when we have been driven out from our homes and from our children?" But when fighting was prescribed for them, they turned away, except for a few of them. And Allah is Knowing of the wrongdoers.

246

waqāla وَقَالَ And said lahum لَهُمْ to them nabiyyuhum نَبِيُّهُمْ their Prophet inna إِنَّ Indeed l-laha اللَّهَ Allah qad قَدْ (has) surely baʿatha بَعَثَ raised lakum لَكُمْ for you ṭālūta طَالُوتَ Talut malikan مَلِكًا (as) a king qālū قَالُوا They said annā أَنَّى How yakūnu يَكُونُ can be lahu لَهُ for him l-mul'ku الْمُلْكُ the kingship ʿalaynā عَلَيْنَا over us wanaḥnu وَنَحْنُ while we aḥaqqu أَحَقُّ (are) more entitled bil-mul'ki بِالْمُلْكِ to kingship min'hu مِنْهُ than him walam وَلَمْ and not yu'ta يُؤْتَ he has been given saʿatan سَعَةً abundance mina مِنَ of l-māli الْمَالِ [the] wealth qāla قَالَ He said inna إِنَّ Indeed l-laha اللَّهَ Allah iṣ'ṭafāhu اصْطَفَاهُ has chosen him ʿalaykum عَلَيْكُمْ over you wazādahu وَزَادَهُ and increased him basṭatan بَسْطَةً abundantly fī فِي in l-ʿil'mi الْعِلْمِ [the] knowledge wal-jis'mi وَالْجِسْمِ and [the] physique wal-lahu وَاللَّهُ And Allah yu'tī يُؤْتِي gives mul'kahu مُلْكَهُ His kingdom man مَنْ (to) whom yashāu يَشَاءُ He wills wal-lahu وَاللَّهُ And Allah wāsiʿun وَاسِعٌ (is) All-Encompassing ʿalīmun عَلِيمٌ All-Knowing

247

247.

And their prophet said to them, "Indeed, Allah has sent to you Saul as a king." They said, "How can he have kingship over us while we are more worthy of kingship than him and he has not been given any measure of wealth?" He said, "Indeed, Allah has chosen him over you and has increased him abundantly in knowledge and stature. And Allah gives His sovereignty to whom He wills. And Allah is all-Encompassing [in favor] and Knowing."

247

waqāla وَقَالَ And said lahum لَهُمْ to them nabiyyuhum نَبِيُّهُمْ their Prophet inna إِنَّ Indeed āyata ءَايَةَ a sign mul'kihi مُلْكِهِ (of) his kingship an أَنْ (is) that yatiyakumu يَأْتِيَكُمُ will come to you l-tābūtu التَّابُوتُ the ark fīhi فِيهِ in it sakīnatun سَكِينَةٌ (is) a tranquility min مِنْ from rabbikum رَبِّكُمْ your Lord wabaqiyyatun وَبَقِيَّةٌ and a remnant mimmā مِمَّا of what taraka تَرَكَ (was) left ālu ءَالُ (by the) family mūsā مُوسَى (of) Musa waālu وَءَالُ and family hārūna هَارُونَ (of) Harun taḥmiluhu تَحْمِلُهُ will carry it l-malāikatu الْمَلَائِكَةُ the Angels inna إِنَّ Indeed fī فِي in dhālika ذَلِكَ that laāyatan لَءَايَةً (is) surely a sign lakum لَكُمْ for you in إِنْ if kuntum كُنْتُمْ you are mu'minīna مُؤْمِنِينَ believers

248

248.

And their prophet said to them, "Indeed, a sign of his kingship is that the chest will come to you in which is assurance from your Lord and a remnant of what the family of Moses and the family of Aaron had left, carried by the angels. Indeed in that is a sign for you, if you are believers."

248

falammā فَلَمَّا Then when faṣala فَصَلَ set out ṭālūtu طَالُوتُ Talut bil-junūdi بِالْجُنُودِ with the forces qāla قَالَ he said inna إِنَّ Indeed l-laha اللَّهَ Allah mub'talīkum مُبْتَلِيكُمْ will test you binaharin بِنَهَرٍ with a river faman فَمَنْ So whoever shariba شَرِبَ drinks min'hu مِنْهُ from it falaysa فَلَيْسَ then he is not minnī مِنِّي from me waman وَمَنْ and whoever lam لَمْ (does) not yaṭʿamhu يَطْعَمْهُ taste it fa-innahu فَإِنَّهُ then indeed, he minnī مِنِّي (is) from me illā إِلَّا except mani مَنِ whoever igh'tarafa اغْتَرَفَ takes ghur'fatan غُرْفَةً (in the) hollow biyadihi بِيَدِهِ (of) his hand fasharibū فَشَرِبُوا Then they drank min'hu مِنْهُ from it illā إِلَّا except qalīlan قَلِيلًا a few min'hum مِنْهُمْ of them falammā فَلَمَّا Then when jāwazahu جَاوَزَهُ he crossed it huwa هُوَ he wa-alladhīna وَالَّذِينَ and those who āmanū ءَامَنُوا believed maʿahu مَعَهُ with him qālū قَالُوا they said lā لَا No ṭāqata طَاقَةَ strength lanā لَنَا for us l-yawma الْيَوْمَ today bijālūta بِجَالُوتَ against Jalut wajunūdihi وَجُنُودِهِ and his troops qāla قَالَ Said alladhīna الَّذِينَ those who yaẓunnūna يَظُنُّونَ were certain annahum أَنَّهُمْ that they mulāqū مُلَاقُوا (would) meet l-lahi اللَّهِ Allah kam كَمْ How many min مِنْ of fi-atin فِئَةٍ a company qalīlatin قَلِيلَةٍ small ghalabat غَلَبَتْ overcame fi-atan فِئَةً a company kathīratan كَثِيرَةً large bi-idh'ni بِإِذْنِ by (the) permission l-lahi اللَّهِ (of) Allah wal-lahu وَاللَّهُ And Allah maʿa مَعَ (is) with l-ṣābirīna الصَّابِرِينَ the patient ones

249

249.

And when Saul went forth with the soldiers, he said, "Indeed, Allah will be testing you with a river. So whoever drinks from it is not of me, and whoever does not taste it is indeed of me, excepting one who takes [from it] in the hollow of his hand." But they drank from it, except a [very] few of them. Then when he had crossed it along with those who believed with him, they said, "There is no power for us today against Goliath and his soldiers." But those who were certain that they would meet Allah said, "How many a small company has overcome a large company by permission of Allah. And Allah is with the patient."

249

walammā وَلَمَّا And when barazū بَرَزُوا they went forth lijālūta لِجَالُوتَ to (face) Jalut wajunūdihi وَجُنُودِهِ and his troops qālū قَالُوا they said rabbanā رَبَّنَا Our Lord afrigh أَفْرِغْ Pour ʿalaynā عَلَيْنَا on us ṣabran صَبْرًا patience wathabbit وَثَبِّتْ and make firm aqdāmanā أَقْدَامَنَا our feet wa-unṣur'nā وَانْصُرْنَا and help us ʿalā عَلَى against l-qawmi الْقَوْمِ the people l-kāfirīna الْكَافِرِينَ (who are) disbelieving

250

250.

And when they went forth to [face] Goliath and his soldiers, they said, "Our Lord, pour upon us patience and plant firmly our feet and give us victory over the disbelieving people."

250

fahazamūhum فَهَزَمُوهُمْ So they defeated them bi-idh'ni بِإِذْنِ by (the) permission l-lahi اللَّهِ (of) Allah waqatala وَقَتَلَ and killed dāwūdu دَاوُدُ Dawood jālūta جَالُوتَ Jalut waātāhu وَءَاتَاهُ and gave him l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah l-mul'ka الْمُلْكَ the kingdom wal-ḥik'mata وَالْحِكْمَةَ and the wisdom waʿallamahu وَعَلَّمَهُ and taught him mimmā مِمَّا that which yashāu يَشَاءُ He willed walawlā وَلَوْلَا And if not dafʿu دَفْعُ (for the) repelling l-lahi اللَّهِ (by) Allah l-nāsa النَّاسَ [the] people baʿḍahum بَعْضَهُمْ some of them bibaʿḍin بِبَعْضٍ with others lafasadati لَفَسَدَتِ certainly (would have) corrupted l-arḍu الْأَرْضُ the Earth walākinna وَلَكِنَّ [and] but l-laha اللَّهَ Allah dhū ذُو (is) Possessor faḍlin فَضْلٍ (of) bounty ʿalā عَلَى to l-ʿālamīna الْعَالَمِينَ the worlds

251

251.

So they defeated them by permission of Allah, and David killed Goliath, and Allah gave him the kingship and prophethood and taught him from that which He willed. And if it were not for Allah checking [some] people by means of others, the earth would have been corrupted, but Allah is full of bounty to the worlds.

251

til'ka تِلْكَ These āyātu ءَايَاتُ (are the) Verses l-lahi اللَّهِ (of) Allah natlūhā نَتْلُوهَا We recite them ʿalayka عَلَيْكَ to you bil-ḥaqi بِالْحَقِّ in [the] truth wa-innaka وَإِنَّكَ And indeed you lamina لَمِنَ (are) surely of l-mur'salīna الْمُرْسَلِينَ the Messengers

252

252.

These are the verses of Allah which We recite to you, [O Muhammad], in truth. And indeed, you are from among the messengers.

252

til'ka تِلْكَ These l-rusulu الرُّسُلُ (are) the Messengers faḍḍalnā فَضَّلْنَا We (have) preferred baʿḍahum بَعْضَهُمْ some of them ʿalā عَلَى over baʿḍin بَعْضٍ others min'hum مِنْهُمْ Among them man مَنْ (were those with) whom kallama كَلَّمَ spoke l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah warafaʿa وَرَفَعَ and He raised baʿḍahum بَعْضَهُمْ some of them darajātin دَرَجَاتٍ (in) degrees waātaynā وَءَاتَيْنَا And We gave ʿīsā عِيسَى Isa ib'na ابْنَ son maryama مَرْيَمَ (of) Maryam l-bayināti الْبَيِّنَاتِ the clear proofs wa-ayyadnāhu وَأَيَّدْنَاهُ and We supported him birūḥi بِرُوحِ with Spirit l-qudusi الْقُدُسِ [the] Holy walaw وَلَوْ And if shāa شَاءَ (had) willed l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah mā مَا not iq'tatala اقْتَتَلَ (would have) fought each other alladhīna الَّذِينَ those who min مِنْ (came) from baʿdihim بَعْدِهِمْ after them min مِنْ from baʿdi بَعْدِ after mā مَا [what] jāathumu جَاءَتْهُمُ came to them l-bayinātu الْبَيِّنَاتُ the clear proofs walākini وَلَكِنِ [And] but ikh'talafū اخْتَلَفُوا they differed famin'hum فَمِنْهُمْ [so] of them man مَنْ (are some) who āmana ءَامَنَ believed wamin'hum وَمِنْهُمْ and of them man مَنْ (are some) who kafara كَفَرَ denied walaw وَلَوْ And if shāa شَاءَ (had) willed l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah mā مَا not iq'tatalū اقْتَتَلُوا they (would have) fought each other walākinna وَلَكِنَّ [and] but l-laha اللَّهَ Allah yafʿalu يَفْعَلُ does mā مَا what yurīdu يُرِيدُ He intends

253

253.

Those messengers - some of them We caused to exceed others. Among them were those to whom Allah spoke, and He raised some of them in degree. And We gave Jesus, the Son of Mary, clear proofs, and We supported him with the Pure Spirit. If Allah had willed, those [generations] succeeding them would not have fought each other after the clear proofs had come to them. But they differed, and some of them believed and some of them disbelieved. And if Allah had willed, they would not have fought each other, but Allah does what He intends.

253

yāayyuhā يَاأَيُّهَا O you alladhīna الَّذِينَ who āmanū ءَامَنُوا believe[d] anfiqū أَنْفِقُوا Spend mimmā مِمَّا of what razaqnākum رَزَقْنَاكُمْ We (have) provided you min مِنْ from qabli قَبْلِ before an أَنْ that yatiya يَأْتِيَ comes yawmun يَوْمٌ a Day lā لَا no bayʿun بَيْعٌ bargaining fīhi فِيهِ in it walā وَلَا and no khullatun خُلَّةٌ friendship walā وَلَا and no shafāʿatun شَفَاعَةٌ intercession wal-kāfirūna وَالْكَافِرُونَ And the deniers humu هُمُ they l-ẓālimūna الظَّالِمُونَ (are) the wrongdoers

254

254.

O you who have believed, spend from that which We have provided for you before there comes a Day in which there is no exchange and no friendship and no intercession. And the disbelievers - they are the wrongdoers.

254

al-lahu اللَّهُ Allah lā لَا (there is) no ilāha إِلَهَ God illā إِلَّا except huwa هُوَ Him l-ḥayu الْحَيُّ the Ever-Living l-qayūmu الْقَيُّومُ the Sustainer of all that exists lā لَا Not takhudhuhu تَأْخُذُهُ overtakes Him sinatun سِنَةٌ slumber walā وَلَا [and] not nawmun نَوْمٌ sleep lahu لَهُ To Him (belongs) mā مَا what(ever) fī فِي (is) in l-samāwāti السَّمَاوَاتِ the heavens wamā وَمَا and what(ever) fī فِي (is) in l-arḍi الْأَرْضِ the earth man مَنْ Who dhā ذَا (is) the one alladhī الَّذِي who yashfaʿu يَشْفَعُ (can) intercede ʿindahu عِنْدَهُ with Him illā إِلَّا except bi-idh'nihi بِإِذْنِهِ by His permission yaʿlamu يَعْلَمُ He knows mā مَا what bayna بَيْنَ (is) aydīhim أَيْدِيهِمْ before them wamā وَمَا and what khalfahum خَلْفَهُمْ (is) behind them walā وَلَا And not yuḥīṭūna يُحِيطُونَ they encompass bishayin بِشَيْءٍ anything min مِنْ of ʿil'mihi عِلْمِهِ His Knowledge illā إِلَّا except bimā بِمَا [of] what shāa شَاءَ He willed wasiʿa وَسِعَ Extends kur'siyyuhu كُرْسِيُّهُ His Throne l-samāwāti السَّمَاوَاتِ (to) the heavens wal-arḍa وَالْأَرْضَ and the earth walā وَلَا And not yaūduhu يَئُودُهُ tires Him ḥif'ẓuhumā حِفْظُهُمَا (the) guarding of both of them wahuwa وَهُوَ And He l-ʿaliyu الْعَلِيُّ (is) the Most High l-ʿaẓīmu الْعَظِيمُ the Most Great

255

255.

Allah - there is no deity except Him, the Ever-Living, the Sustainer of [all] existence. Neither drowsiness overtakes Him nor sleep. To Him belongs whatever is in the heavens and whatever is on the earth. Who is it that can intercede with Him except by His permission? He knows what is [presently] before them and what will be after them, and they encompass not a thing of His knowledge except for what He wills. His Kursi extends over the heavens and the earth, and their preservation tires Him not. And He is the Most High, the Most Great.

255

lā لَا (There is) no ik'rāha إِكْرَاهَ compulsion fī فِي in l-dīni الدِّينِ the religion qad قَدْ Surely tabayyana تَبَيَّنَ has become distinct l-rush'du الرُّشْدُ the right (path) mina مِنَ from l-ghayi الْغَيِّ the wrong faman فَمَنْ Then whoever yakfur يَكْفُرْ disbelieves bil-ṭāghūti بِالطَّاغُوتِ in false deities wayu'min وَيُؤْمِنْ and believes bil-lahi بِاللَّهِ in Allah faqadi فَقَدِ then surely is'tamsaka اسْتَمْسَكَ he grasped bil-ʿur'wati بِالْعُرْوَةِ the handhold l-wuth'qā الْوُثْقَى [the] firm lā لَا (which) not infiṣāma انْفِصَامَ (will) break lahā لَهَا [for it] wal-lahu وَاللَّهُ And Allah samīʿun سَمِيعٌ (is) All-Hearing ʿalīmun عَلِيمٌ All-Knowing

256

256.

There shall be no compulsion in [acceptance of] the religion. The right course has become clear from the wrong. So whoever disbelieves in Taghut and believes in Allah has grasped the most trustworthy handhold with no break in it. And Allah is Hearing and Knowing.

256

al-lahu اللَّهُ Allah waliyyu وَلِيُّ (is the) Protecting Guardian alladhīna الَّذِينَ (of) those who āmanū ءَامَنُوا believe[d] yukh'rijuhum يُخْرِجُهُمْ He brings them out mina مِنَ from l-ẓulumāti الظُّلُمَاتِ [the] darkness ilā إِلَى towards l-nūri النُّورِ [the] light wa-alladhīna وَالَّذِينَ And those who kafarū كَفَرُوا disbelieve(d) awliyāuhumu أَوْلِيَاؤُهُمُ their guardians l-ṭāghūtu الطَّاغُوتُ (are) the evil ones yukh'rijūnahum يُخْرِجُونَهُمْ they bring them out mina مِنَ from l-nūri النُّورِ the light ilā إِلَى towards l-ẓulumāti الظُّلُمَاتِ the darkness ulāika أُولَئِكَ Those aṣḥābu أَصْحَابُ (are the) companions l-nāri النَّارِ (of) the Fire hum هُمْ they fīhā فِيهَا in it khālidūna خَالِدُونَ will abide forever

257

257.

Allah is the ally of those who believe. He brings them out from darknesses into the light. And those who disbelieve - their allies are Taghut. They take them out of the light into darknesses. Those are the companions of the Fire; they will abide eternally therein.

257

alam أَلَمْ Did not tara تَرَ you see ilā إِلَى [towards] alladhī الَّذِي the one who ḥājja حَاجَّ argued ib'rāhīma إِبْرَاهِيمَ (with) Ibrahim fī فِي concerning rabbihi رَبِّهِ his Lord an أَنْ because ātāhu ءَاتَاهُ gave him l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah l-mul'ka الْمُلْكَ the kingdom idh إِذْ When qāla قَالَ Said ib'rāhīmu إِبْرَاهِيمُ Ibrahim rabbiya رَبِّيَ My Lord alladhī الَّذِي (is) the One Who yuḥ'yī يُحْيِي grants life wayumītu وَيُمِيتُ and causes death qāla قَالَ He said anā أَنَا I uḥ'yī أُحْيِي give life wa-umītu وَأُمِيتُ and cause death qāla قَالَ Said ib'rāhīmu إِبْرَاهِيمُ Ibrahim fa-inna فَإِنَّ [Then] indeed l-laha اللَّهَ Allah yatī يَأْتِي brings up bil-shamsi بِالشَّمْسِ the sun mina مِنَ from l-mashriqi الْمَشْرِقِ the east fati فَأْتِ so you bring bihā بِهَا it mina مِنَ from l-maghribi الْمَغْرِبِ the west fabuhita فَبُهِتَ So became dumbfounded alladhī الَّذِي the one who kafara كَفَرَ disbelieved wal-lahu وَاللَّهُ and Allah lā لَا (does) not yahdī يَهْدِي guide l-qawma الْقَوْمَ the people l-ẓālimīna الظَّالِمِينَ (who are) [the] wrongdoers

258

258.

Have you not considered the one who argued with Abraham about his Lord [merely] because Allah had given him kingship? When Abraham said, "My Lord is the one who gives life and causes death," he said, "I give life and cause death." Abraham said, "Indeed, Allah brings up the sun from the east, so bring it up from the west." So the disbeliever was overwhelmed [by astonishment], and Allah does not guide the wrongdoing people.

258

aw أَوْ Or ka-alladhī كَالَّذِي like the one who marra مَرَّ passed ʿalā عَلَى by qaryatin قَرْيَةٍ a township wahiya وَهِيَ and it khāwiyatun خَاوِيَةٌ (had) overturned ʿalā عَلَى on ʿurūshihā عُرُوشِهَا its roofs qāla قَالَ He said annā أَنَّى How yuḥ'yī يُحْيِي (will) bring to life hādhihi هَذِهِ this (town) l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah baʿda بَعْدَ after mawtihā مَوْتِهَا its death fa-amātahu فَأَمَاتَهُ Then he was made to die l-lahu اللَّهُ (by) Allah mi-ata مِائَةَ (for) a hundred ʿāmin عَامٍ year(s) thumma ثُمَّ then baʿathahu بَعَثَهُ He raised him qāla قَالَ He said kam كَمْ How long labith'ta لَبِثْتَ (have) you remained qāla قَالَ He said labith'tu لَبِثْتُ I remained yawman يَوْمًا (for) a day aw أَوْ or baʿḍa بَعْضَ a part yawmin يَوْمٍ (of) a day qāla قَالَ He said bal بَلْ Nay labith'ta لَبِثْتَ you (have) remained mi-ata مِائَةَ one hundred ʿāmin عَامٍ year(s) fa-unẓur فَانْظُرْ Then look ilā إِلَى at ṭaʿāmika طَعَامِكَ your food washarābika وَشَرَابِكَ and your drink lam لَمْ (they did) not yatasannah يَتَسَنَّهْ change with time wa-unẓur وَانْظُرْ and look ilā إِلَى at ḥimārika حِمَارِكَ your donkey walinajʿalaka وَلِنَجْعَلَكَ and We will make you āyatan ءَايَةً a sign lilnnāsi لِلنَّاسِ for the people wa-unẓur وَانْظُرْ And look ilā إِلَى at l-ʿiẓāmi الْعِظَامِ the bones kayfa كَيْفَ how nunshizuhā نُنْشِزُهَا We raise them thumma ثُمَّ then naksūhā نَكْسُوهَا We cover them laḥman لَحْمًا (with) flesh falammā فَلَمَّا Then when tabayyana تَبَيَّنَ became clear lahu لَهُ to him qāla قَالَ he said aʿlamu أَعْلَمُ I know anna أَنَّ that l-laha اللَّهَ Allah ʿalā عَلَى (is) on kulli كُلِّ every shayin شَيْءٍ thing qadīrun قَدِيرٌ All-Powerful

259

259.

Or [consider such an example] as the one who passed by a township which had fallen into ruin. He said, "How will Allah bring this to life after its death?" So Allah caused him to die for a hundred years; then He revived him. He said, "How long have you remained?" The man said, "I have remained a day or part of a day." He said, "Rather, you have remained one hundred years. Look at your food and your drink; it has not changed with time. And look at your donkey; and We will make you a sign for the people. And look at the bones [of this donkey] - how We raise them and then We cover them with flesh." And when it became clear to him, he said, "I know that Allah is over all things competent."

259

wa-idh وَإِذْ And when qāla قَالَ said ib'rāhīmu إِبْرَاهِيمُ Ibrahim rabbi رَبِّ My Lord arinī أَرِنِي show me kayfa كَيْفَ how tuḥ'yī تُحْيِي You give life l-mawtā الْمَوْتَى (to) the dead qāla قَالَ He said awalam أَوَلَمْ Have not tu'min تُؤْمِنْ you believed qāla قَالَ He said balā بَلَى Yes walākin وَلَكِنْ [and] but liyaṭma-inna لِيَطْمَئِنَّ to satisfy qalbī قَلْبِي my heart qāla قَالَ He said fakhudh فَخُذْ Then take arbaʿatan أَرْبَعَةً four mina مِنَ of l-ṭayri الطَّيْرِ the birds faṣur'hunna فَصُرْهُنَّ and incline them ilayka إِلَيْكَ towards you thumma ثُمَّ then ij'ʿal اجْعَلْ put ʿalā عَلَى on kulli كُلِّ each jabalin جَبَلٍ hill min'hunna مِنْهُنَّ of them juz'an جُزْءًا a portion thumma ثُمَّ then ud'ʿuhunna ادْعُهُنَّ call them yatīnaka يَأْتِينَكَ they will come to you saʿyan سَعْيًا (in) haste wa-iʿ'lam وَاعْلَمْ And know anna أَنَّ that l-laha اللَّهَ Allah ʿazīzun عَزِيزٌ (is) All-Mighty ḥakīmun حَكِيمٌ All-Wise

260

260.

And [mention] when Abraham said, "My Lord, show me how You give life to the dead." [Allah] said, "Have you not believed?" He said, "Yes, but [I ask] only that my heart may be satisfied." [Allah] said, "Take four birds and commit them to yourself. Then [after slaughtering them] put on each hill a portion of them; then call them - they will come [flying] to you in haste. And know that Allah is Exalted in Might and Wise."

260

mathalu مَثَلُ Example alladhīna الَّذِينَ (of) those who yunfiqūna يُنْفِقُونَ spend amwālahum أَمْوَالَهُمْ their wealth fī فِي in sabīli سَبِيلِ (the) way l-lahi اللَّهِ (of) Allah kamathali كَمَثَلِ (is) like ḥabbatin حَبَّةٍ a grain anbatat أَنْبَتَتْ which grows sabʿa سَبْعَ seven sanābila سَنَابِلَ ears fī فِي in kulli كُلِّ each sunbulatin سُنْبُلَةٍ ear mi-atu مِائَةُ hundred ḥabbatin حَبَّةٍ grain(s) wal-lahu وَاللَّهُ And Allah yuḍāʿifu يُضَاعِفُ gives manifold liman لِمَنْ to whom yashāu يَشَاءُ He wills wal-lahu وَاللَّهُ And Allah wāsiʿun وَاسِعٌ (is) All-Encompassing ʿalīmun عَلِيمٌ All-Knowing

261

261.

The example of those who spend their wealth in the way of Allah is like a seed [of grain] which grows seven spikes; in each spike is a hundred grains. And Allah multiplies [His reward] for whom He wills. And Allah is all-Encompassing and Knowing.

261

alladhīna الَّذِينَ Those who yunfiqūna يُنْفِقُونَ spend amwālahum أَمْوَالَهُمْ their wealth fī فِي in sabīli سَبِيلِ (the) way l-lahi اللَّهِ (of) Allah thumma ثُمَّ then lā لَا not yut'biʿūna يُتْبِعُونَ they follow mā مَا what anfaqū أَنْفَقُوا they spend mannan مَنًّا (with) reminders of generosity walā وَلَا and not adhan أَذًى hurt lahum لَهُمْ for them ajruhum أَجْرُهُمْ their reward ʿinda عِنْدَ (is) with rabbihim رَبِّهِمْ their Lord walā وَلَا and (there will be) no khawfun خَوْفٌ fear ʿalayhim عَلَيْهِمْ on them walā وَلَا and not hum هُمْ they yaḥzanūna يَحْزَنُونَ will grieve

262

262.

Those who spend their wealth in the way of Allah and then do not follow up what they have spent with reminders [of it] or [other] injury will have their reward with their Lord, and there will be no fear concerning them, nor will they grieve.

262

qawlun قَوْلٌ A word maʿrūfun مَعْرُوفٌ kind wamaghfiratun وَمَغْفِرَةٌ and (seeking) forgiveness khayrun خَيْرٌ (are) better min مِنْ than ṣadaqatin صَدَقَةٍ a charity yatbaʿuhā يَتْبَعُهَا followed [it] adhan أَذًى (by) hurt wal-lahu وَاللَّهُ And Allah ghaniyyun غَنِيٌّ (is) All-Sufficient ḥalīmun حَلِيمٌ All-Forbearing

263

263.

Kind speech and forgiveness are better than charity followed by injury. And Allah is Free of need and Forbearing.

263

yāayyuhā يَاأَيُّهَا O you alladhīna الَّذِينَ who āmanū ءَامَنُوا believe[d]! lā لَا (Do) not tub'ṭilū تُبْطِلُوا render in vain ṣadaqātikum صَدَقَاتِكُمْ your charities bil-mani بِالْمَنِّ with reminders (of it) wal-adhā وَالْأَذَى or [the] hurt ka-alladhī كَالَّذِي like the one who yunfiqu يُنْفِقُ spends mālahu مَالَهُ his wealth riāa رِئَاءَ (to) be seen l-nāsi النَّاسِ (by) the people walā وَلَا and (does) not yu'minu يُؤْمِنُ believe bil-lahi بِاللَّهِ in Allah wal-yawmi وَالْيَوْمِ and the Day l-ākhiri الْءَاخِرِ [the] Last famathaluhu فَمَثَلُهُ Then his example kamathali كَمَثَلِ (is) like ṣafwānin صَفْوَانٍ (that of a) smooth rock ʿalayhi عَلَيْهِ upon it turābun تُرَابٌ (is) dust fa-aṣābahu فَأَصَابَهُ then fell on it wābilun وَابِلٌ heavy rain fatarakahu فَتَرَكَهُ then left it ṣaldan صَلْدًا bare lā لَا Not yaqdirūna يَقْدِرُونَ they have control ʿalā عَلَى on shayin شَيْءٍ anything mimmā مِمَّا of what kasabū كَسَبُوا they (have) earned wal-lahu وَاللَّهُ And Allah lā لَا (does) not yahdī يَهْدِي guide l-qawma الْقَوْمَ the people l-kāfirīna الْكَافِرِينَ [the] disbelieving

264

264.

O you who have believed, do not invalidate your charities with reminders or injury as does one who spends his wealth [only] to be seen by the people and does not believe in Allah and the Last Day. His example is like that of a [large] smooth stone upon which is dust and is hit by a downpour that leaves it bare. They are unable [to keep] anything of what they have earned. And Allah does not guide the disbelieving people.

264

wamathalu وَمَثَلُ And (the) example alladhīna الَّذِينَ (of) those who yunfiqūna يُنْفِقُونَ spend amwālahumu أَمْوَالَهُمُ their wealth ib'tighāa ابْتِغَاءَ seeking marḍāti مَرْضَاتِ (the) pleasure l-lahi اللَّهِ (of) Allah watathbītan وَتَثْبِيتًا and certainty min مِنْ from anfusihim أَنْفُسِهِمْ their (inner) souls kamathali كَمَثَلِ (is) like jannatin جَنَّةٍ a garden birabwatin بِرَبْوَةٍ on a height aṣābahā أَصَابَهَا fell on it wābilun وَابِلٌ heavy rain faātat فَءَاتَتْ so it yielded ukulahā أُكُلَهَا its harvest ḍiʿ'fayni ضِعْفَيْنِ double fa-in فَإِنْ Then if lam لَمْ (does) not yuṣib'hā يُصِبْهَا fall (on) it wābilun وَابِلٌ heavy rain faṭallun فَطَلٌّ then a drizzle wal-lahu وَاللَّهُ And Allah bimā بِمَا of what taʿmalūna تَعْمَلُونَ you do baṣīrun بَصِيرٌ (is) All-Seer

265

265.

And the example of those who spend their wealth seeking means to the approval of Allah and assuring [reward for] themselves is like a garden on high ground which is hit by a downpour - so it yields its fruits in double. And [even] if it is not hit by a downpour, then a drizzle [is sufficient]. And Allah, of what you do, is Seeing.

265

ayawaddu أَيَوَدُّ Would like aḥadukum أَحَدُكُمْ any of you an أَنْ that takūna تَكُونَ it be lahu لَهُ for him jannatun جَنَّةٌ a garden min مِنْ of nakhīlin نَخِيلٍ date-palms wa-aʿnābin وَأَعْنَابٍ and grapevines tajrī تَجْرِي flowing min مِنْ [from] taḥtihā تَحْتِهَا underneath it l-anhāru الْأَنْهَارُ the rivers lahu لَهُ for him fīhā فِيهَا in it min مِنْ of kulli كُلِّ all (kinds) l-thamarāti الثَّمَرَاتِ (of) [the] fruits wa-aṣābahu وَأَصَابَهُ and strikes him l-kibaru الْكِبَرُ [the] old age walahu وَلَهُ and [for] his dhurriyyatun ذُرِّيَّةٌ children ḍuʿafāu ضُعَفَاءُ (are) weak fa-aṣābahā فَأَصَابَهَا then falls on it iʿ'ṣārun إِعْصَارٌ whirlwind fīhi فِيهِ in it nārun نَارٌ (is) fire fa-iḥ'taraqat فَاحْتَرَقَتْ then it is burnt kadhālika كَذَلِكَ Thus yubayyinu يُبَيِّنُ makes clear l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah lakumu لَكُمُ for you l-āyāti الْءَايَاتِ (His) Signs laʿallakum لَعَلَّكُمْ so that you may tatafakkarūna تَتَفَكَّرُونَ ponder

266

266.

Would one of you like to have a garden of palm trees and grapevines underneath which rivers flow in which he has from every fruit? But he is afflicted with old age and has weak offspring, and it is hit by a whirlwind containing fire and is burned. Thus does Allah make clear to you [His] verses that you might give thought.

266

yāayyuhā يَاأَيُّهَا O you alladhīna الَّذِينَ who āmanū ءَامَنُوا believe[d]! anfiqū أَنْفِقُوا Spend min مِنْ from ṭayyibāti طَيِّبَاتِ (the) good things mā مَا that kasabtum كَسَبْتُمْ you have earned wamimmā وَمِمَّا and whatever akhrajnā أَخْرَجْنَا We brought forth lakum لَكُمْ for you mina مِنَ from l-arḍi الْأَرْضِ the earth walā وَلَا And (do) not tayammamū تَيَمَّمُوا aim at l-khabītha الْخَبِيثَ the bad min'hu مِنْهُ of it tunfiqūna تُنْفِقُونَ you spend walastum وَلَسْتُمْ while you (would) not biākhidhīhi بِءَاخِذِيهِ take it illā إِلَّا except an أَنْ [that] tugh'miḍū تُغْمِضُوا (with) close(d) eyes fīhi فِيهِ [in it] wa-iʿ'lamū وَاعْلَمُوا and know anna أَنَّ that l-laha اللَّهَ Allah ghaniyyun غَنِيٌّ (is) Self-Sufficient ḥamīdun حَمِيدٌ Praiseworthy

267

267.

O you who have believed, spend from the good things which you have earned and from that which We have produced for you from the earth. And do not aim toward the defective therefrom, spending [from that] while you would not take it [yourself] except with closed eyes. And know that Allah is Free of need and Praiseworthy.

267

al-shayṭānu الشَّيْطَانُ The Shaitaan yaʿidukumu يَعِدُكُمُ promises you l-faqra الْفَقْرَ [the] poverty wayamurukum وَيَأْمُرُكُمْ and orders you bil-faḥshāi بِالْفَحْشَاءِ to immorality wal-lahu وَاللَّهُ while Allah yaʿidukum يَعِدُكُمْ promises you maghfiratan مَغْفِرَةً forgiveness min'hu مِنْهُ from Him wafaḍlan وَفَضْلًا and bounty wal-lahu وَاللَّهُ And Allah wāsiʿun وَاسِعٌ (is) All-Encompassing ʿalīmun عَلِيمٌ All-Knowing

268

268.

Satan threatens you with poverty and orders you to immorality, while Allah promises you forgiveness from Him and bounty. And Allah is all-Encompassing and Knowing.

268

yu'tī يُؤْتِي He grants l-ḥik'mata الْحِكْمَةَ [the] wisdom man مَنْ (to) whom yashāu يَشَاءُ He wills waman وَمَنْ and whoever yu'ta يُؤْتَ is granted l-ḥik'mata الْحِكْمَةَ [the] wisdom faqad فَقَدْ then certainly ūtiya أُوتِيَ he is granted khayran خَيْرًا good kathīran كَثِيرًا abundant wamā وَمَا And none yadhakkaru يَذَّكَّرُ remembers illā إِلَّا except ulū أُولُوا those l-albābi الْأَلْبَابِ (of) understanding

269

269.

He gives wisdom to whom He wills, and whoever has been given wisdom has certainly been given much good. And none will remember except those of understanding.

269

wamā وَمَا And whatever anfaqtum أَنْفَقْتُمْ you spend min مِنْ (out) of nafaqatin نَفَقَةٍ (your) expenditures aw أَوْ or nadhartum نَذَرْتُمْ you vow min مِنْ of nadhrin نَذْرٍ vow(s) fa-inna فَإِنَّ then indeed l-laha اللَّهَ Allah yaʿlamuhu يَعْلَمُهُ knows it wamā وَمَا and not lilẓẓālimīna لِلظَّالِمِينَ for the wrongdoers min مِنْ any anṣārin أَنْصَارٍ helpers

270

270.

And whatever you spend of expenditures or make of vows - indeed, Allah knows of it. And for the wrongdoers there are no helpers.

270

in إِنْ If tub'dū تُبْدُوا you disclose l-ṣadaqāti الصَّدَقَاتِ the charities faniʿimmā فَنِعِمَّا then well hiya هِيَ it (is) wa-in وَإِنْ But if tukh'fūhā تُخْفُوهَا you keep it secret watu'tūhā وَتُؤْتُوهَا and give it l-fuqarāa الْفُقَرَاءَ (to) the poor fahuwa فَهُوَ then it khayrun خَيْرٌ (is) better lakum لَكُمْ for you wayukaffiru وَيُكَفِّرُ And He will remove ʿankum عَنْكُمْ from you min مِنْ [of] sayyiātikum سَيِّئَاتِكُمْ your evil deeds wal-lahu وَاللَّهُ And Allah bimā بِمَا with what taʿmalūna تَعْمَلُونَ you do khabīrun خَبِيرٌ (is) All-Aware

271

271.

If you disclose your charitable expenditures, they are good; but if you conceal them and give them to the poor, it is better for you, and He will remove from you some of your misdeeds [thereby]. And Allah, with what you do, is [fully] Acquainted.

271

laysa لَيْسَ Not ʿalayka عَلَيْكَ on you hudāhum هُدَاهُمْ (is) their guidance walākinna وَلَكِنَّ [and] but l-laha اللَّهَ Allah yahdī يَهْدِي guides man مَنْ whom yashāu يَشَاءُ He wills wamā وَمَا And whatever tunfiqū تُنْفِقُوا you spend min مِنْ of khayrin خَيْرٍ good fali-anfusikum فَلِأَنْفُسِكُمْ then it is for yourself wamā وَمَا and not tunfiqūna تُنْفِقُونَ you spend illā إِلَّا except ib'tighāa ابْتِغَاءَ seeking wajhi وَجْهِ (the) face l-lahi اللَّهِ (of) Allah wamā وَمَا And whatever tunfiqū تُنْفِقُوا you spend min مِنْ of khayrin خَيْرٍ good yuwaffa يُوَفَّ will be repaid in full ilaykum إِلَيْكُمْ to you wa-antum وَأَنْتُمْ and you lā لَا (will) not tuẓ'lamūna تُظْلَمُونَ be wronged

272

272.

Not upon you, [O Muhammad], is [responsibility for] their guidance, but Allah guides whom He wills. And whatever good you [believers] spend is for yourselves, and you do not spend except seeking the countenance of Allah. And whatever you spend of good - it will be fully repaid to you, and you will not be wronged.

272

lil'fuqarāi لِلْفُقَرَاءِ For the poor alladhīna الَّذِينَ those who uḥ'ṣirū أُحْصِرُوا are wrapped up fī فِي in sabīli سَبِيلِ (the) way l-lahi اللَّهِ (of) Allah lā لَا not yastaṭīʿūna يَسْتَطِيعُونَ they are able ḍarban ضَرْبًا (to) move about fī فِي in l-arḍi الْأَرْضِ the earth yaḥsabuhumu يَحْسَبُهُمُ Think (about) them l-jāhilu الْجَاهِلُ the ignorant one aghniyāa أَغْنِيَاءَ (that they are) self-sufficient mina مِنَ (because) of l-taʿafufi التَّعَفُّفِ (their) restraint taʿrifuhum تَعْرِفُهُمْ you recognize them bisīmāhum بِسِيمَاهُمْ by their mark lā لَا Not yasalūna يَسْءَلُونَ (do) they ask l-nāsa النَّاسَ the people il'ḥāfan إِلْحَافًا with importunity wamā وَمَا And whatever tunfiqū تُنْفِقُوا you spend min مِنْ of khayrin خَيْرٍ good fa-inna فَإِنَّ then indeed l-laha اللَّهَ Allah bihi بِهِ of it ʿalīmun عَلِيمٌ (is) All-Knower

273

273.

[Charity is] for the poor who have been restricted for the cause of Allah, unable to move about in the land. An ignorant [person] would think them self-sufficient because of their restraint, but you will know them by their [characteristic] sign. They do not ask people persistently [or at all]. And whatever you spend of good - indeed, Allah is Knowing of it.

273

alladhīna الَّذِينَ Those who yunfiqūna يُنْفِقُونَ spend amwālahum أَمْوَالَهُمْ their wealth bi-al-layli بِاللَّيْلِ by night wal-nahāri وَالنَّهَارِ and day sirran سِرًّا secretly waʿalāniyatan وَعَلَانِيَةً and openly falahum فَلَهُمْ then for them ajruhum أَجْرُهُمْ (is) their reward ʿinda عِنْدَ with rabbihim رَبِّهِمْ their Lord walā وَلَا and no khawfun خَوْفٌ fear ʿalayhim عَلَيْهِمْ on them walā وَلَا and not hum هُمْ they yaḥzanūna يَحْزَنُونَ will grieve

274

274.

Those who spend their wealth [in Allah 's way] by night and by day, secretly and publicly - they will have their reward with their Lord. And no fear will there be concerning them, nor will they grieve.

274

alladhīna الَّذِينَ Those who yakulūna يَأْكُلُونَ consume l-riba الرِّبَوا [the] usury lā لَا not yaqūmūna يَقُومُونَ they can stand illā إِلَّا except kamā كَمَا like yaqūmu يَقُومُ stands alladhī الَّذِي the one who yatakhabbaṭuhu يَتَخَبَّطُهُ confounds him l-shayṭānu الشَّيْطَانُ the Shaitaan mina مِنَ with l-masi الْمَسِّ (his) touch dhālika ذَلِكَ That bi-annahum بِأَنَّهُمْ (is) because they qālū قَالُوا say innamā إِنَّمَا Only l-bayʿu الْبَيْعُ the trade mith'lu مِثْلُ (is) like l-riba الرِّبَوا [the] usury wa-aḥalla وَأَحَلَّ While has permitted l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah l-bayʿa الْبَيْعَ [the] trade waḥarrama وَحَرَّمَ but (has) forbidden l-riba الرِّبَوا [the] usury faman فَمَنْ Then whoever jāahu جَاءَهُ comes to him mawʿiẓatun مَوْعِظَةٌ (the) admonition min مِنْ from rabbihi رَبِّهِ His Lord fa-intahā فَانْتَهَى and he refrained falahu فَلَهُ then for him mā مَا what salafa سَلَفَ (has) passed wa-amruhu وَأَمْرُهُ and his case ilā إِلَى (is) with l-lahi اللَّهِ Allah waman وَمَنْ and whoever ʿāda عَادَ repeated fa-ulāika فَأُولَئِكَ then those aṣḥābu أَصْحَابُ (are the) companions l-nāri النَّارِ (of) the Fire hum هُمْ they fīhā فِيهَا in it khālidūna خَالِدُونَ will abide forever

275

275.

Those who consume interest cannot stand [on the Day of Resurrection] except as one stands who is being beaten by Satan into insanity. That is because they say, "Trade is [just] like interest." But Allah has permitted trade and has forbidden interest. So whoever has received an admonition from his Lord and desists may have what is past, and his affair rests with Allah. But whoever returns to [dealing in interest or usury] - those are the companions of the Fire; they will abide eternally therein.

275

yamḥaqu يَمْحَقُ Destroys l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah l-riba الرِّبَوا the usury wayur'bī وَيُرْبِي and (gives) increase l-ṣadaqāti الصَّدَقَاتِ (for) the charities wal-lahu وَاللَّهُ And Allah lā لَا (does) not yuḥibbu يُحِبُّ love kulla كُلَّ every kaffārin كَفَّارٍ ungrateful athīmin أَثِيمٍ sinner

276

276.

Allah destroys interest and gives increase for charities. And Allah does not like every sinning disbeliever.

276

inna إِنَّ Indeed alladhīna الَّذِينَ those who āmanū ءَامَنُوا believe[d] waʿamilū وَعَمِلُوا and did l-ṣāliḥāti الصَّالِحَاتِ good deeds wa-aqāmū وَأَقَامُوا and established l-ṣalata الصَّلَوةَ the prayer waātawū وَءَاتَوُا and gave l-zakata الزَّكَوةَ the zakah lahum لَهُمْ for them ajruhum أَجْرُهُمْ their reward ʿinda عِنْدَ (is) with rabbihim رَبِّهِمْ their Lord walā وَلَا and no khawfun خَوْفٌ fear ʿalayhim عَلَيْهِمْ on them walā وَلَا and not hum هُمْ they yaḥzanūna يَحْزَنُونَ will grieve

277

277.

Indeed, those who believe and do righteous deeds and establish prayer and give zakah will have their reward with their Lord, and there will be no fear concerning them, nor will they grieve.

277

yāayyuhā يَاأَيُّهَا O you alladhīna الَّذِينَ who āmanū ءَامَنُوا believe[d]! ittaqū اتَّقُوا Fear l-laha اللَّهَ Allah wadharū وَذَرُوا and give up mā مَا what baqiya بَقِيَ remained mina مِنَ of l-riba الرِّبَوا [the] usury in إِنْ if kuntum كُنْتُمْ you are mu'minīna مُؤْمِنِينَ believers

278

278.

O you who have believed, fear Allah and give up what remains [due to you] of interest, if you should be believers.

278

fa-in فَإِنْ And if lam لَمْ not tafʿalū تَفْعَلُوا you do fadhanū فَأْذَنُوا then be informed biḥarbin بِحَرْبٍ of a war mina مِنَ from l-lahi اللَّهِ Allah warasūlihi وَرَسُولِهِ and His Messenger wa-in وَإِنْ And if tub'tum تُبْتُمْ you repent falakum فَلَكُمْ then for you ruūsu رُءُوسُ (is) amwālikum أَمْوَالِكُمْ your capital lā لَا (do) not taẓlimūna تَظْلِمُونَ wrong walā وَلَا and not tuẓ'lamūna تُظْلَمُونَ you will be wronged

279

279.

And if you do not, then be informed of a war [against you] from Allah and His Messenger. But if you repent, you may have your principal - [thus] you do no wrong, nor are you wronged.

279

wa-in وَإِنْ And if kāna كَانَ is dhū ذُو the (debtor) ʿus'ratin عُسْرَةٍ in difficulty fanaẓiratun فَنَظِرَةٌ then postponement ilā إِلَى until maysaratin مَيْسَرَةٍ ease wa-an وَأَنْ And if taṣaddaqū تَصَدَّقُوا you remit as charity khayrun خَيْرٌ (it is) better lakum لَكُمْ for you in إِنْ If kuntum كُنْتُمْ you taʿlamūna تَعْلَمُونَ know

280

280.

And if someone is in hardship, then [let there be] postponement until [a time of] ease. But if you give [from your right as] charity, then it is better for you, if you only knew.

280

wa-ittaqū وَاتَّقُوا And fear yawman يَوْمًا a Day tur'jaʿūna تُرْجَعُونَ you will be brought back fīhi فِيهِ [in it] ilā إِلَى to l-lahi اللَّهِ Allah thumma ثُمَّ Then tuwaffā تُوَفَّى (will be) repaid in full kullu كُلُّ every nafsin نَفْسٍ soul mā مَا what kasabat كَسَبَتْ it earned wahum وَهُمْ and they lā لَا not yuẓ'lamūna يُظْلَمُونَ will be wronged

281

281.

And fear a Day when you will be returned to Allah. Then every soul will be compensated for what it earned, and they will not be treated unjustly.

281

yāayyuhā يَاأَيُّهَا O you alladhīna الَّذِينَ who āmanū ءَامَنُوا believe[d] idhā إِذَا When tadāyantum تَدَايَنْتُمْ you contract with one another bidaynin بِدَيْنٍ any debt ilā إِلَى for ajalin أَجَلٍ a term musamman مُسَمًّى fixed fa-uk'tubūhu فَاكْتُبُوهُ then write it walyaktub وَلْيَكْتُبْ And let write baynakum بَيْنَكُمْ between you kātibun كَاتِبٌ a scribe bil-ʿadli بِالْعَدْلِ in justice walā وَلَا And not yaba يَأْبَ (should) refuse kātibun كَاتِبٌ a scribe an أَنْ that yaktuba يَكْتُبَ he writes kamā كَمَا as ʿallamahu عَلَّمَهُ (has) taught him l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah falyaktub فَلْيَكْتُبْ So let him write walyum'lili وَلْيُمْلِلِ and let dictate alladhī الَّذِي the one ʿalayhi عَلَيْهِ on whom l-ḥaqu الْحَقُّ (is) the right walyattaqi وَلْيَتَّقِ and let him fear l-laha اللَّهَ Allah rabbahu رَبَّهُ his Lord walā وَلَا and (let him) not yabkhas يَبْخَسْ diminish min'hu مِنْهُ from it shayan شَيْئًا anything fa-in فَإِنْ Then if kāna كَانَ is alladhī الَّذِي the one ʿalayhi عَلَيْهِ on him l-ḥaqu الْحَقُّ (is) the right safīhan سَفِيهًا (of) limited understanding aw أَوْ or ḍaʿīfan ضَعِيفًا weak aw أَوْ or lā لَا not yastaṭīʿu يَسْتَطِيعُ capable an أَنْ that yumilla يُمِلَّ (can) dictate huwa هُوَ he falyum'lil فَلْيُمْلِلْ then let dictate waliyyuhu وَلِيُّهُ his guardian bil-ʿadli بِالْعَدْلِ with justice wa-is'tashhidū وَاسْتَشْهِدُوا And call for evidence shahīdayni شَهِيدَيْنِ two witnesses min مِنْ among rijālikum رِجَالِكُمْ your men fa-in فَإِنْ And if lam لَمْ not yakūnā يَكُونَا there are rajulayni رَجُلَيْنِ two men farajulun فَرَجُلٌ then one man wa-im'ra-atāni وَامْرَأَتَانِ and two women mimman مِمَّنْ of whom tarḍawna تَرْضَوْنَ you agree mina مِنَ of l-shuhadāi الشُّهَدَاءِ [the] witnesses an أَنْ (so) that (if) taḍilla تَضِلَّ [she] errs iḥ'dāhumā إِحْدَاهُمَا one of the two fatudhakkira فَتُذَكِّرَ then will remind iḥ'dāhumā إِحْدَاهُمَا one of the two l-ukh'rā الْأُخْرَى the other walā وَلَا And not yaba يَأْبَ (should) refuse l-shuhadāu الشُّهَدَاءُ the witnesses idhā إِذَا when mā مَا that duʿū دُعُوا they are called walā وَلَا And not tasamū تَسْءَمُوا (be) weary an أَنْ that taktubūhu تَكْتُبُوهُ you write it ṣaghīran صَغِيرًا small aw أَوْ or kabīran كَبِيرًا large ilā إِلَى for ajalihi أَجَلِهِ its term dhālikum ذَلِكُمْ That aqsaṭu أَقْسَطُ (is) more just ʿinda عِنْدَ near l-lahi اللَّهِ Allah wa-aqwamu وَأَقْوَمُ and more upright lilshahādati لِلشَّهَادَةِ for evidence wa-adnā وَأَدْنَى and nearer allā أَلَّا that not tartābū تَرْتَابُوا you (have) doubt illā إِلَّا except an أَنْ that takūna تَكُونَ be tijāratan تِجَارَةً a transaction ḥāḍiratan حَاضِرَةً present tudīrūnahā تُدِيرُونَهَا you carry out baynakum بَيْنَكُمْ among you falaysa فَلَيْسَ then not ʿalaykum عَلَيْكُمْ on you junāḥun جُنَاحٌ any sin allā أَلَّا that not taktubūhā تَكْتُبُوهَا you write it wa-ashhidū وَأَشْهِدُوا And take witness idhā إِذَا when tabāyaʿtum تَبَايَعْتُمْ you make commercial transaction walā وَلَا And not yuḍārra يُضَارَّ (should) be harmed kātibun كَاتِبٌ (the) scribe walā وَلَا and not shahīdun شَهِيدٌ (the) witness wa-in وَإِنْ and if tafʿalū تَفْعَلُوا you do fa-innahu فَإِنَّهُ then indeed it fusūqun فُسُوقٌ (is) sinful conduct bikum بِكُمْ for you wa-ittaqū وَاتَّقُوا and fear l-laha اللَّهَ Allah wayuʿallimukumu وَيُعَلِّمُكُمُ And teaches l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah wal-lahu وَاللَّهُ And Allah bikulli بِكُلِّ of every shayin شَيْءٍ thing ʿalīmun عَلِيمٌ (is) All-Knower

282

282.

O you who have believed, when you contract a debt for a specified term, write it down. And let a scribe write [it] between you in justice. Let no scribe refuse to write as Allah has taught him. So let him write and let the one who has the obligation dictate. And let him fear Allah, his Lord, and not leave anything out of it. But if the one who has the obligation is of limited understanding or weak or unable to dictate himself, then let his guardian dictate in justice. And bring to witness two witnesses from among your men. And if there are not two men [available], then a man and two women from those whom you accept as witnesses - so that if one of the women errs, then the other can remind her. And let not the witnesses refuse when they are called upon. And do not be [too] weary to write it, whether it is small or large, for its [specified] term. That is more just in the sight of Allah and stronger as evidence and more likely to prevent doubt between you, except when it is an immediate transaction which you conduct among yourselves. For [then] there is no blame upon you if you do not write it. And take witnesses when you conclude a contract. Let no scribe be harmed or any witness. For if you do so, indeed, it is [grave] disobedience in you. And fear Allah. And Allah teaches you. And Allah is Knowing of all things.

282

wa-in وَإِنْ And if kuntum كُنْتُمْ you are ʿalā عَلَى on safarin سَفَرٍ a journey walam وَلَمْ and not tajidū تَجِدُوا you find kātiban كَاتِبًا a scribe farihānun فَرِهَانٌ then pledge maqbūḍatun مَقْبُوضَةٌ in hand fa-in فَإِنْ Then if amina أَمِنَ entrusts baʿḍukum بَعْضُكُمْ one of you baʿḍan بَعْضًا (to) another falyu-addi فَلْيُؤَدِّ then let discharge alladhī الَّذِي the one who u'tumina اؤْتُمِنَ is entrusted amānatahu أَمَانَتَهُ his trust walyattaqi وَلْيَتَّقِ And let him fear l-laha اللَّهَ Allah rabbahu رَبَّهُ his Lord walā وَلَا And (do) not taktumū تَكْتُمُوا conceal l-shahādata الشَّهَادَةَ the evidence waman وَمَنْ And whoever yaktum'hā يَكْتُمْهَا conceals it fa-innahu فَإِنَّهُ then indeed he āthimun ءَاثِمٌ (is) sinful qalbuhu قَلْبُهُ his heart wal-lahu وَاللَّهُ And Allah bimā بِمَا of what taʿmalūna تَعْمَلُونَ you do ʿalīmun عَلِيمٌ (is) All-Knower

283

283.

And if you are on a journey and cannot find a scribe, then a security deposit [should be] taken. And if one of you entrusts another, then let him who is entrusted discharge his trust [faithfully] and let him fear Allah, his Lord. And do not conceal testimony, for whoever conceals it - his heart is indeed sinful, and Allah is Knowing of what you do.

283

lillahi لِلَّهِ To Allah (belongs) mā مَا whatever fī فِي (is) in l-samāwāti السَّمَاوَاتِ the heavens wamā وَمَا and whatever fī فِي (is) in l-arḍi الْأَرْضِ the earth wa-in وَإِنْ And if tub'dū تُبْدُوا you disclose mā مَا what fī فِي (is) in anfusikum أَنْفُسِكُمْ yourselves aw أَوْ or tukh'fūhu تُخْفُوهُ you conceal it yuḥāsib'kum يُحَاسِبْكُمْ will call you to account bihi بِهِ for it l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah fayaghfiru فَيَغْفِرُ Then He will forgive liman لِمَنْ [to] whom yashāu يَشَاءُ He wills wayuʿadhibu وَيُعَذِّبُ and He will punish man مَنْ whom yashāu يَشَاءُ He wills wal-lahu وَاللَّهُ And Allah ʿalā عَلَى on kulli كُلِّ every shayin شَيْءٍ thing qadīrun قَدِيرٌ (is) All-Powerful

284

284.

To Allah belongs whatever is in the heavens and whatever is in the earth. Whether you show what is within yourselves or conceal it, Allah will bring you to account for it. Then He will forgive whom He wills and punish whom He wills, and Allah is over all things competent.

284

āmana ءَامَنَ Believed l-rasūlu الرَّسُولُ the Messenger bimā بِمَا in what unzila أُنْزِلَ was revealed ilayhi إِلَيْهِ to him min مِنْ from rabbihi رَبِّهِ his Lord wal-mu'minūna وَالْمُؤْمِنُونَ and the believers kullun كُلٌّ All āmana ءَامَنَ believed bil-lahi بِاللَّهِ in Allah wamalāikatihi وَمَلَائِكَتِهِ and His Angels wakutubihi وَكُتُبِهِ and His Books warusulihi وَرُسُلِهِ and His Messengers lā لَا Not nufarriqu نُفَرِّقُ we make distinction bayna بَيْنَ between aḥadin أَحَدٍ any min مِنْ of rusulihi رُسُلِهِ His Messengers waqālū وَقَالُوا And they said samiʿ'nā سَمِعْنَا We heard wa-aṭaʿnā وَأَطَعْنَا and we obeyed ghuf'rānaka غُفْرَانَكَ (Grant) us Your forgiveness rabbanā رَبَّنَا our Lord wa-ilayka وَإِلَيْكَ and to You l-maṣīru الْمَصِيرُ (is) the return

285

285.

The Messenger has believed in what was revealed to him from his Lord, and [so have] the believers. All of them have believed in Allah and His angels and His books and His messengers, [saying], "We make no distinction between any of His messengers." And they say, "We hear and we obey. [We seek] Your forgiveness, our Lord, and to You is the [final] destination."

285

lā لَا (Does) not yukallifu يُكَلِّفُ burden l-lahu اللَّهُ Allah nafsan نَفْسًا any soul illā إِلَّا except wus'ʿahā وُسْعَهَا its capacity lahā لَهَا for it mā مَا what kasabat كَسَبَتْ it earned waʿalayhā وَعَلَيْهَا and against it mā مَا what ik'tasabat اكْتَسَبَتْ it earned rabbanā رَبَّنَا Our Lord lā لَا (Do) not tuākhidh'nā تُؤَاخِذْنَا take us to task in إِنْ if nasīnā نَسِينَا we forget aw أَوْ or akhṭanā أَخْطَأْنَا we err rabbanā رَبَّنَا Our Lord walā وَلَا And (do) not taḥmil تَحْمِلْ lay ʿalaynā عَلَيْنَا upon us iṣ'ran إِصْرًا a burden kamā كَمَا like that ḥamaltahu حَمَلْتَهُ (which) You laid [it] ʿalā عَلَى on alladhīna الَّذِينَ those who min مِنْ (were) from qablinā قَبْلِنَا before us rabbanā رَبَّنَا Our Lord walā وَلَا [And] (do) not tuḥammil'nā تُحَمِّلْنَا lay on us mā مَا what lā لَا not ṭāqata طَاقَةَ (the) strength lanā لَنَا we have bihi بِهِ [of it] (to bear) wa-uʿ'fu وَاعْفُ And pardon ʿannā عَنَّا [from] us wa-igh'fir وَاغْفِرْ and forgive lanā لَنَا [for] us wa-ir'ḥamnā وَارْحَمْنَا and have mercy on us anta أَنْتَ You (are) mawlānā مَوْلَانَا our Protector fa-unṣur'nā فَانْصُرْنَا so help us ʿalā عَلَى against l-qawmi الْقَوْمِ the people l-kāfirīna الْكَافِرِينَ [the] disbelievers

286

286.

Allah does not charge a soul except [with that within] its capacity. It will have [the consequence of] what [good] it has gained, and it will bear [the consequence of] what [evil] it has earned. "Our Lord, do not impose blame upon us if we have forgotten or erred. Our Lord, and lay not upon us a burden like that which You laid upon those before us. Our Lord, and burden us not with that which we have no ability to bear. And pardon us; and forgive us; and have mercy upon us. You are our protector, so give us victory over the disbelieving people."

286

Al-Faatiha
